# Comprehensive Reference Projects Analysis

## 1. What Each Reference Project Is

### `.agents/references/siyuan/`
The **SiYuan Note** kernel source code and API documentation. Contains `API.md` (1585 lines) documenting the full SiYuan backend HTTP API (notebooks, documents, blocks, attributes, SQL, files, export, notifications, network proxy, system), plus `kernel/main.go` as the Go backend entrypoint. This is your source of truth for backend API calls.

### `.agents/references/petal/`
The **SiYuan Frontend (Petal)** type definitions. Contains `siyuan.d.ts` (kernel types), `kernel.d.ts`, and an extensive `types/` directory with TypeScript declarations for:
- `index.d.ts` (704 lines) -- ISiyuan global state, App, Editor, Layout, Dock, Custom, Protyle, IWebSocketData, IMenu, IOperation, IAV (attribute view) types
- `protyle.d.ts` (915 lines) -- IProtyle interface (the editor model), Protyle class, Lute (Markdown engine), Toolbar, Hint, WYSIWYG, Undo, Upload, Preview, Scroll, Breadcrumb, Background, Gutter, Title classes
- `events.d.ts` -- IMenuBaseDetail (menu events with protyle context)
- `config.d.ts` -- App configuration types (IConf)
- `block/Panel.d.ts`, `layout/Tab.d.ts`, `layout/Wnd.d.ts`, `layout/Model.d.ts`

### `.agents/references/plugin-sample/`
The **official SiYuan pure TypeScript plugin sample** (webpack-based). Demonstrates:
- `Plugin` base class with lifecycle: `onload()`, `onLayoutReady()`, `onunload()`
- `addTopBar()`, `addCommand()`, `addDock()`, `addTab()`, `addStatusBar()`, `addFloatLayer()`
- `Menu` system with `addItem()`, `addSeparator()`, `fullscreen()`
- `Dialog` creation, `Setting` API, `Protyle` (editor) API
- `eventBus` events (click-blockicon, paste, ws-main, etc.)
- I18n with `this.i18n`
- `plugin.json` with `displayName`, `description`, `keywords`, `backends`, `frontends`

### `.agents/references/plugin-sample-vite-svelte/`
The **Vite + Svelte 5 version** of the SiYuan plugin sample (branch `svelte5`). Same plugin features as plugin-sample but:
- Uses Vite as bundler (`vite.config.ts`)
- Uses Svelte 5 components (`.svelte` files) for UI
- Has `SettingUtils` helper class for typed setting management (`src/libs/setting-utils.ts`)
- Has `svelteDialog()` helper for creating dialogs with Svelte components (`src/libs/dialog.ts`)
- Has `promise-pool.ts`, `const.ts`, `api.ts` in `src/libs/`
- Scripts: `make_install.js`, `make_dev_link.js`, `update_version.js`, `elevate.ps1`

### `.agents/references/vscode-background-cover/`
The **VS Code Background Cover** extension (v3.2.5), the primary reference for feature parity. A full-featured VS Code background image/pet/particle extension.

### `.agents/references/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/`
The **current SiYuan Background Cover plugin** (v0.5.1, branch `master` -- pure TypeScript, webpack-based). The plugin being developed/referenced.

## 2. VSCode Background Cover -- Complete Feature List & Architecture

### File Structure (14 source files)
```
src/
├── extension.ts           -- Entry point: activation, commands, views, theme listener
├── PickList.ts            -- Core logic: all user actions, image selection, DOM update
├── FileDom.ts             -- CSS/JS injection into VSCode workbench files (1604 lines)
├── backgroundCoverView.ts -- Tree View (settings panel in sidebar)
├── ImgItem.ts             -- QuickPick item data class
├── BlendHelper.ts         -- Auto blend mode based on theme (dark=lighten, light=multiply)
├── ParticleEffect.ts      -- Particle effect JS string generator
├── OnlineImageHelper.ts   -- Online image URL resolution (JSON API, HTML, VS20988xyz)
├── readerView.ts          -- Webview for online gallery browsing
├── global.ts              -- ExtensionContext singleton
├── color.ts               -- Color name-to-RGB map (30+ colors)
├── version.ts             -- Version constant
├── vsHelp.ts              -- Notification helpers
├── SudoPromptHelper.ts    -- Sudo/elevation for file permissions
└── uninstall.ts           -- Cleanup on uninstall
```

### Complete Feature List

| Category | Feature | Implementation |
|----------|---------|---------------|
| **Image Source** | Select single image file | `PickList.SelectPictures` -> OS file dialog |
| | Add directory for random selection | `PickList.AddDirectory` -> fs.readdirSync |
| | Input URL/path manually | `PickList.InputPath` -> supports local, HTTPS, JSON API, HTML, online gallery URLs |
| | Online gallery browsing | `readerView.ts` webview with iframe to vs.20988.xyz |
| | Refresh online folder | `OnlineImageHelper.getOnlineImages()` |
| **Appearance** | Opacity (0-0.8) | CSS `opacity` on `body::before` pseudo-element |
| | Blur (0-100px) | CSS `filter: blur()` |
| | Size mode (11 modes) | `cover`, `repeat`, `contain`, `center`, `not_center`, `not_right_bottom`, `not_right_top`, `not_left`, `not_right`, `not_top`, `not_bottom` |
| | Blend mode (3 modes) | `auto` (theme-based), `multiply`, `lighten` via CSS `mix-blend-mode` |
| **Auto Random** | Enable/disable auto switch | `PickList.startAutoRandomTask()` with setInterval |
| | Configurable interval (seconds) | `backgroundCover.autoInterval` config |
| | Prevents concurrent auto-updates | `PickList.isAutoRunning` flag |
| | Source: local folder, online folder, or single URL | `autoUpdateBackground()` |
| **Particle Effects** | Toggle on/off | `setContextValue('backgroundCoverParticleEffect', ...)` |
| | Opacity (0-1) | Globally configurable |
| | Color (RGB preset or custom) | 30+ preset colors + custom RGB input |
| | Count (1-200) | Globally configurable |
| **Pet Assistant** | Toggle on/off | `backgroundCoverPetEnabled` globalState |
| | 17 pet types | akita, totoro, fox, pika, deno2, clippy, rubber-duck, crab, zappy, cockatiel, snake, chicken, turtle, panda, snail, deno, morph |
| | Walking animation + idle | GIF-based sprites with CSS animations |
| | Collision detection | Jumps when hitting titlebar elements (window-title, etc.) |
| | Random messages | 60+ Chinese programming humor messages in speech bubbles |
| **Video Background** | Support `.mp4`, `.webm`, `.ogg`, `.mov` | `<video>` element injected into DOM |
| **Hot Reload** | No restart needed for most changes | MutationObserver + CSS fetch on status bar trigger |
| **Multi-platform** | Desktop + code-server (browser) | Workbench target detection |
| **Online Images** | JSON API parsing | Tries `?format=json`, `?list=json`, `.json` |
| | HTML `<a>` tag parsing | Regex patterns for image links |
| | VS20988xyz forum support | Post-body `<img>` extraction |
| | Image caching | Downloads to extension globalStorage |
| | Private address blocking | Blocks localhost, RFC1918 addresses |
| **Hotkey** | `Ctrl+Shift+F7` for random refresh | Registered keybinding |

### Architecture: How It Integrates with VSCode API

1. **CSS Injection via Core File Patching**: The plugin patches `workbench.desktop.main.js` (or `workbench.js` for code-server) by appending JS/CSS. The CSS uses a `body::before` pseudo-element for the background image. This is the only way to modify the VSCode workbench DOM.

2. **The Loader JS** (injected into workbench JS):
   - Fetches the CSS file dynamically: `fetch(cssUrl).then(r => r.text()).then(css => updateStyleTag(css))`
   - Monitors status bar via `MutationObserver` for a trigger message `"background-cover-reload-trigger"`
   - On `window.focus`, re-fetches CSS for hot reload
   - Creates/removes `<video>` element for video backgrounds
   - Creates/animates pet assistant element

3. **Sidebar Views**:
   - TreeDataProvider (`BackgroundCoverViewProvider`): renders settings tree with checkboxes, toggles, sliders
   - WebviewViewProvider (`ReaderViewProvider`): iframe-based online gallery

4. **Status Bar Items**: Two buttons -- background config (file-media icon) and particle effects (sparkle icon)

5. **Configuration** (`package.json` contributes): 9 config properties -- `opacity`, `blur`, `imagePath`, `randomImageFolder`, `autoStatus`, `autoInterval`, `sizeModel`, `blendModel`, `defaultOnlinePage`

---

## 3. Siyuan Background Cover Plugin -- Complete Feature List & Architecture

### File Structure (15 source files)
```
src/
├── index.ts               -- Plugin entry: BgCoverPlugin class, lifecycle, commands
├── types.ts               -- Type definitions: bgMode, bgObj, bgObjCfg, fileIdx, configs
├── constants.ts            -- Package info, paths, cache limits, supported suffixes
├── utils/
│   ├── configs.ts          -- ConfigManager: local/sync config with localStorage + plugin data
│   ├── api.ts              -- KernelApi: wrappers for SiYuan HTTP API (putFile, readDir, etc.)
│   ├── theme.ts            -- Theme helpers: getCurrentThemeInfo(), getInstalledThemes()
│   ├── logger.ts           -- Timestamped console.log (debug only in dev mode)
│   └── pythonic.ts         -- Python-like wrappers: OS (file ops), CloseCV (image size calc)
├── services/
│   └── bgRender.ts         -- Background rendering: canvas layer, opacity, blur, position
└── ui/
    ├── topbar.ts           -- Top bar button + dropdown menu
    ├── settings.ts         -- Settings dialog (5 tabs: config, assets, theme, advance, about)
    ├── fileManager.ts      -- File management: upload, cache check, delete, folder picker
    ├── notice.ts           -- Notification dialogs
    └── components/
        ├── dialogs.ts      -- Reusable dialog factories
        └── templates.ts    -- HTML templates (if exists)
```

### Complete Feature List

| Category | Feature | Implementation |
|----------|---------|---------------|
| **Image Management** | Manual image selection | `topbarUI.selectPictureByHand()` -> file picker dialog + `uploadOneImage()` |
| | Batch add multiple images | `addSeveralLocalImagesFile()` -> multiple file picker |
| | Add directory (bulk import) | `addDirectory()` -> folder picker, iterates files, checks MD5 duplicates |
| | Cache image list viewer/manager | `fileManagerUI.selectPictureDialog()` with list + preview + set-as-bg/delete |
| **Background Rendering** | Canvas-based background layer | `<canvas id="bglayer">` inserted before `<head>`, z-index -10000 |
| | Background image display | CSS `background-image: url()` on canvas element |
| | Opacity control (0-1) | Sets `document.body.style.opacity` |
| | Blur control (0-10px) | CSS `filter: blur()` on canvas |
| | Image position offset (X/Y) | CSS `background-position: x% y%` with sliders |
| | Smart offset direction | Auto-detects full axis (X or Y) based on image/container ratio |
| **Random Selection** | Random image from cache | `selectPictureRandom()`: excludes current, random from fileidx |
| | Auto-refresh timer | `setInterval` at configurable minutes, with stop/restart |
| **Plugin Toggle** | Enable/disable background | `pluginOnOff()` toggles `activate` flag, hides background layer |
| **Theme Integration** | Per-theme disable | `disabledTheme` config: dark/light × theme name, renders checkbox cards |
| | Theme change detection | MutationObserver on `<html>` attributes |
| | Theme refresh prompt | Dialog asking to reload when theme changes |
| **Data Persistence** | Dual config storage | `localCfg` (localStorage, per-device) vs `syncCfg` (plugin data, cloud-sync) |
| | Image file index | `fileidx` maps MD5 hash -> bgObj metadata (name, path, dimensions, mode) |
| | Cache validation on startup | `checkAssetsDir()` compares file system vs fileidx, reports extras/missing |
| | MD5 deduplication | 2MB chunk hash prevents duplicate uploads |
| **Settings Dialog** | 5-tab settings panel | Config, Assets, Theme, Advance, About |
| | Sliders for opacity/blur | `b3-slider` with live preview |
| | Auto-refresh toggle + time | Switch + number input for minutes |
| | Developer mode toggle | Debug logging switch |
| | Reset all settings | Clears cache + resets configs |
| **Hotkeys** | `Shift+Cmd+F6`: Manual select | `selectPictureByHand()` |
| | `Shift+Cmd+F7`: Random select | `selectPictureRandom(true)` |
| | `Shift+Cmd+F4`: Toggle on/off | `pluginOnOff()` |
| | `Shift+Cmd+7/8`: Opacity +/- | `opacityShortcut()` |
| | `Shift+Cmd+9/0`: Blur +/- | `blurShortcut()` |
| **Platform Support** | All frontends (desktop, mobile, browser) | `plugin.json` frontends config |
| | All backends (win/linux/mac/ios/android) | `plugin.json` backends config |
| | Mobile layout detection | `isMobileLayout` flag adjusts dialog widths |
| **Asset Folder Picker** | Browse `data/assets/` tree | `openAssetsFolderPickerDialog()` with recursive folder tree, checkboxes, image counts |
| **Default Image** | Fallback demo image | `demoImgURL` (bundled JPG) when no images cached |
| **i18n** | Chinese/English | Separate JSON files in `src/i18n/` |

### Architecture: How It Integrates with Siyuan API

1. **Plugin Base Class**: Extends `Plugin` from `"siyuan"`. Lifecycle:
   - `onload()`: Initialize topbar icon, register commands, add icons
   - `onLayoutReady()`: Load configs, create background layer, check assets, apply settings
   - `onunload()`: Remove background layer, cleanup

2. **Top Bar Integration**: `this.addTopBar()` places an icon button in Siyuan's top bar. Click opens a `Menu` with nested submenus.

3. **Command Registration**: `this.addCommand()` with `langKey`, `hotkey`, `callback` -- registered globally.

4. **Background Injection**: Direct DOM manipulation -- creates `<canvas id="bglayer">` and inserts it before `<head>` with `style.*` properties set programmatically. **No CSS file injection** needed (unlike VSCode which requires patching core files).

5. **File System API**: Uses `KernelApi` (wraps SiYuan HTTP endpoints):
   - `putFile(path, file)` -- upload images to `/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/`
   - `readDir(path)` -- list directory contents
   - `removeFile(path)` -- delete cached images
   - `putFolder(path)` -- create directories
   - `getLocalStorage()` / `setLocalStorage()` -- per-device settings
   - `plugin.loadData()` / `plugin.saveData()` -- cloud-syncable settings

6. **Theme Detection**: Reads from `(window as any).siyuan.config.appearance`:
   - `mode`: 0=light, 1=dark
   - `themeLight` / `themeDark`: current theme name
   - `lightThemes` / `darkThemes`: installed theme lists

7. **File Picker**: Uses DOM `<input type="file">` (not VSCode `window.showOpenDialog`):
   - `openFilePicker()` for image files
   - `openFolderPicker()` with `webkitdirectory` for whole folders

---

## 4. Key Differences: VSCode vs Siyuan Plugins

| Aspect | VSCode Background Cover | Siyuan Background Cover |
|--------|------------------------|------------------------|
| **Background injection** | Patches workbench JS/CSS files; uses `body::before` pseudo-element | Direct DOM: inserts `<canvas>` element; sets CSS properties programmatically |
| **Hot reload** | MutationObserver on status bar + window.focus re-fetch | Direct DOM style changes, no reload needed |
| **Permission model** | Requires sudo/elevation to patch app files; lockfile-based concurrency | Uses Siyuan's built-in file API; no elevation needed |
| **Video support** | Yes -- `<video>` element with `.mp4/.webm/.ogg/.mov` | Planned but not implemented (commented out code exists) |
| **Live2D support** | No | Planned (bgMode.live2d enum defined) |
| **Particle effects** | Yes -- injects particle JS library | Not implemented |
| **Pet assistant** | Yes -- 17 animated pets with collision detection, messages, walking/idle | Not implemented |
| **Size modes** | 11 modes (cover, repeat, contain, center, not_*) | Single mode (cover only), but has X/Y position sliders |
| **Blend modes** | auto/multiply/lighten (CSS mix-blend-mode) | Not implemented |
| **Online images** | Full URL resolver: JSON API, HTML parsing, VS20988xyz, caching | Not implemented (local images only) |
| **Image source** | Local files, directories, URLs, online galleries | Local files and directories only |
| **Image caching** | Downloads remote images to globalStorage | Copies local images to plugin's data/public directory with MD5 naming |
| **Duplicate detection** | File path-based | MD5 hash-based (2MB chunk) |
| **Cache max** | No limit | 198 images max |
| **Config storage** | VSCode workspace configuration + globalState | Dual: localStorage (per-device) + plugin data (cloud-synced) |
| **Theme integration** | Blend mode auto-switches with theme (lighten/multiply) | Per-theme enable/disable toggle |
| **Interface** | Tree view sidebar + QuickPick menu + Webview gallery | Custom settings dialog with 5 tabs + topbar dropdown menu |
| **Mobile support** | No | Yes (desktop, mobile, browser-desktop, browser-mobile) |
| **Android backend** | N/A | Supported |
| **Build tool** | TypeScript compiler (`tsc`) | Webpack |
| **i18n** | Inline Chinese/English in code | JSON files (`en_US.json`, `zh_CN.json`) |

---

## 5. Siyuan API Patterns Used (from references)

### Plugin Lifecycle (from plugin-sample)
```typescript
export default class extends Plugin {
    onload()        // Register commands, icons, protyleSlash, protyleOptions
    onLayoutReady() // addTopBar, addDock, addStatusBar, loadData
    onunload()      // Cleanup
    uninstall()     // removeData
}
```

### Key Plugin APIs (from plugin-sample & petal types)
- `this.addTopBar({icon, title, position, callback})` -- Top bar button
- `this.addCommand({langKey, hotkey, callback})` -- Keyboard shortcut
- `this.addDock({config, data, type, init, destroy})` -- Side dock panel
- `this.addTab({type, init, destroy})` -- Custom tab with Svelte component
- `this.addStatusBar({element})` -- Status bar element
- `this.addIcons(svgString)` -- Register SVG icon symbols
- `this.i18n` -- Internationalized strings
- `new Menu(id, onClose)` -- Dropdown menu with `addItem()`, `addSeparator()`
- `new Dialog({title, content, width, height})` -- Custom dialog
- `this.eventBus.on/off(event, handler)` -- Event system
- `this.loadData(key)` / `this.saveData(key, value)` -- Plugin data persistence
- `this.setting` -- `new Setting({confirmCallback})` with `addItem()`

### Backend HTTP API (from api.ts & siyuan/API.md)
- `fetchPost(url, formData, callback)` -- Siyuan's built-in fetch wrapper
- `/api/file/putFile` -- Upload files (multipart)
- `/api/file/readDir` -- List directory
- `/api/file/removeFile` -- Delete file
- `/api/file/getFile` -- Read file
- `/api/storage/getLocalStorage` / `setLocalStorage` -- Key-value store
- `/api/bazaar/getInstalledTheme` -- Get installed themes

### Global Siyuan State (from petal/types)
- `(window as any).siyuan.config.system.workspaceDir` -- Data directory path
- `(window as any).siyuan.config.system.os` -- OS type
- `(window as any).siyuan.config.appearance.mode` -- Theme mode (0=light, 1=dark)
- `(window as any).siyuan.config.appearance.themeLight/themeDark` -- Theme names
- `(window as any).siyuan.config.appearance.lightThemes/darkThemes` -- Theme lists

### Utility Functions (from plugin-sample)
- `getFrontend()` -- Returns "desktop"/"mobile"/"browser-desktop"/"browser-mobile"
- `getBackend()` -- Returns "windows"/"linux"/"darwin"/"android"/"ios"/"docker"
- `showMessage(msg, timeout, type)` -- Toast notification
- `confirm(title, msg, callback)` -- Confirmation dialog
- `adaptHotkey(hotkey)` -- Platform-adaptive hotkey display
- `getAllEditor()` -- Get all open Protyle editors

---

This completes the thorough exploration. The VSCode plugin has significantly richer features (particles, pets, online images, 11 size modes, blend modes, video support) compared to the current Siyuan plugin which focuses on local image management with basic opacity/blur/position controls. The Siyuan plugin benefits from simpler DOM manipulation (no file patching needed) but lacks many of the visual flair features from its VSCode counterpart. Nya~♡
</task_result>
```

## 综合项目总结：思源插件-背景封面

### 1. 项目结构与架构

```
siyuan-plugin-background-cover/
├── plugin.json                  # 思源插件清单
├── package.json                 # npm/依赖配置
├── tsconfig.json                # TypeScript 配置 (ES6, CommonJS)
├── webpack.config.js            # Webpack 打包 (开发和生产)
├── .eslintrc.js                 # ESLint 规则
├── .gitignore                   # Git 忽略（包括 i18n/, static/, dist/）
├── README.md / README_en_US.md  # 双语文档
├── scripts/
│   └── copy2dev.js              # 构建后脚本：将 dist/ 复制到思源开发工作区
├── static/                      # 静态资源（图片：ali.jpg, wechat.png, 默认背景等）（gitignored）
├── icon.png / preview.png       # 插件图标和预览
├── .agents/                     # AI 代理上下文和引用
│   ├── references/              # 子模块：思源代码库、petal、vscode-background-cover 等
│   ├── conversations/           # 代理对话记录
│   └── rules/                   # 代理行为规则
└── src/
    ├── index.ts                 # 插件入口点：扩展 Plugin 基类
    ├── constants.ts             # 应用程序常量、图标 SVG、资产路径
    ├── types.ts                 # TypeScript 类型、接口、默认配置
    │
    ├── utils/
    │   ├── configs.ts           # ConfigManager 单例（两层存储）
    │   ├── api.ts               # 思源内核 API 封装（KernelApi + BaseApi）
    │   ├── logger.ts            # info/debug/warn/error 带时间戳的日志
    │   ├── theme.ts             # 主题检测辅助函数
    │   └── pythonic.ts          # 类似 Python 的工具类（Numpy, CloseCV, OS）
    │
    ├── services/
    │   └── bgRender.ts          # 背景渲染引擎（canvas 层、透明度、模糊、自动刷新）
    │
    └── ui/
        ├── topbar.ts            # 顶部栏菜单（添加图片、随机选择、开关）
        ├── settings.ts          # 设置面板（选项卡：配置、资产、主题、高级、关于）
        ├── fileManager.ts       # 文件管理（上传、缓存验证、图片选择对话框）
        ├── notice.ts            # 通知对话框（Bug 报告、主题刷新、功能未实现）
        └── components/
            ├── dialogs.ts       # 通用对话框工厂（确认、通知）
            └── templates.ts     # 对话框的 HTML 模板字符串
```

**架构模式**：一个纯粹的 TypeScript 思源插件——没有 Vue/Svelte/React。所有 UI 都是通过 HTML 模板字符串和直接 DOM 操作命令式构建的。代码库组织为工具类、一个后台渲染服务和 UI 模块。

---

### 2. 当前实现的所有功能

| 功能 | 状态 | 实现位置 |
|---------|--------|-----------------|
| 背景图片（canvas 元素作为 `<html>` 的子元素）| ✅ | `src/services/bgRender.ts: createBgLayer()` |
| 透明度控制（滑块 `[0, 1]`，加权至 `[0.74, 0.99]`）| ✅ | `src/services/bgRender.ts: changeOpacity()` |
| 模糊控制（滑块 `[0, 10]px`） | ✅ | `src/services/bgRender.ts: changeBlur()` |
| 背景 X/Y 位置偏移（智能轴切换） | ✅ | `src/services/bgRender.ts: changeBgPosition()` |
| 插件开关切换 | ✅ | `src/ui/topbar.ts: pluginOnOff()` |
| 主题禁用（每个主题暗/亮黑名单） | ✅ | `src/ui/settings.ts: generatedisabledThemeElement()` |
| 图片缓存系统（通过哈希去重） | ✅ | `src/ui/fileManager.ts` |
| 上传单张图片 | ✅ | `src/ui/fileManager.ts: uploadOneImage()` |
| 上传整个文件夹的图片 | ✅ | `src/ui/topbar.ts: addDirectory()` |
| 多图片选择上传 | ✅ | `src/ui/topbar.ts: addSeveralLocalImagesFile()` |
| 随机背景选择 | ✅ | `src/ui/topbar.ts: selectPictureRandom()` |
| 启动时自动刷新（可配置间隔，单位分钟） | ✅ | `src/services/bgRender.ts: applySettings()` |
| 缓存管理器对话框（查看、设置为背景、删除） | ✅ | `src/ui/fileManager.ts: selectPictureDialog()` |
| 清除所有缓存 | ✅ | `src/ui/fileManager.ts: clearCacheFolder()` |
| 设置面板（5 个选项卡：配置、资产、主题、高级、关于） | ✅ | `src/ui/settings.ts: openSettingDialog()` |
| 热键（7 个命令：手动选择、随机选择、开关、透明度 +/-、模糊 +/-） | ✅ | `src/index.ts: onload()` |
| 跨设备同步（通过思源的 API 分离本地/同步配置） | ✅ | `src/utils/configs.ts`（两层存储） |
| 主题变更检测和刷新提示 | ✅ | `src/index.ts: themeOnChange()` |
| 移动布局支持 | ✅ | 所有对话框中的响应式宽度 |
| Android 后端限制通知 | ✅ | `src/ui/topbar.ts`（顶部栏子菜单） |
| 开发者/调试模式 | ✅ | 仅在该模式下通过标志和日志记录 |
| 旧版本迁移（v0.x → v0.5+） | ✅ | `src/ui/fileManager.ts: checkAssetsDir()` |
| 资产文件夹选取器对话框（未完成，在菜单中被注释掉） | 🚧 | `src/ui/fileManager.ts: openAssetsFolderPickerDialog()` |
| 视频背景 | ❌ | 仅存根（`bgRender.ts` 中有占位代码） |
| Live2D 背景 | ❌ | 类型已定义但未实现 |

---

### 3. 使用的依赖

**生产依赖**（2 个）：
| 包名 | 版本 | 用途 |
|---------|---------|-------|
| `ts-md5` | ^2.0.1 | 图片去重和文件哈希 |
| `install` | ^0.13.0 | （可能不常用——可能是遗留依赖） |

**开发依赖**（15 个）：
| 包名 | 版本 | 用途 |
|---------|---------|-------|
| `siyuan` | 0.7.4 | 思源类型定义和 API（已外置） |
| `webpack` + `webpack-cli` | ^5.99.5 / ^5.1.4 | 打包器 |
| `esbuild-loader` | ^3.2.0 | 快速的 TS/JS 转译 |
| `typescript` | 4.7.4 | TypeScript 编译器 |
| `sass` + `sass-loader` | ^1.86.3 / ^12.6.0 | SCSS 样式处理 |
| `css-loader` | ^6.11.0 | CSS 加载器 |
| `mini-css-extract-plugin` | 2.3.0 | 将 CSS 提取到单独的文件 |
| `copy-webpack-plugin` | ^11.0.0 | 构建时将静态资源复制到 dist/ |
| `zip-webpack-plugin` | ^4.0.3 | 在构建时创建 package.zip |
| `fs-extra` | ^11.3.2 | 开发脚本的文件系统工具 |
| `eslint` + `@typescript-eslint/*` | ^8.57.1 / 5.29.0 | Linting |
| `@types/node` | ^20.17.30 | Node.js 类型 |
| `@types/wicg-file-system-access` | ^2020.9.8 | 文件系统 API 类型 |

---

### 4. 构建系统配置

**Webpack**（`webpack.config.js`）：
- **入口**：`src/index.ts`
- **输出**：开发模式为 `./index.js`，生产模式为 `./dist/index.js`
- **目标**：CommonJS2（思源插件要求）
- **外置**：`siyuan`（在运行时由思源提供）
- **加载器**：`.ts` 文件使用 `esbuild-loader`，`.scss` 文件使用 `sass-loader` + `css-loader` + `MiniCssExtractPlugin`
- **压缩**：生产模式使用 `EsbuildPlugin`
- **监控模式**：开发时自动重建
- **构建后**：`scripts/copy2dev.js` 使用 env `SIYUANDEV` 将 `dist/` 复制到思源开发工作区
- **生产打包**：将资产、README 和 `plugin.json` 复制到 `dist/`，然后创建 `package.zip`

**TypeScript**（`tsconfig.json`）：
- 目标/模块：`es6` / `commonjs`
- 严格模式：`noImplicitAny: true`
- 包含：仅 `src/**/*.ts`

---

### 5. 插件如何在思源中注册

**清单**（`plugin.json`）：
```json
{
  "name": "siyuan-plugin-background-cover",
  "version": "0.5.1",
  "minAppVersion": "3.1.20",
  "backends": ["all"],
  "frontends": ["desktop", "mobile", "desktop-window", "browser-desktop", "browser-mobile"]
}
```

**入口点**（`src/index.ts`）：导出默认类 `BgCoverPlugin extends Plugin`。

**生命周期**：
1. **`onload()`**：设置 `window.bgCoverPlugin` 全局对象，添加图标，初始化顶部栏按钮，注册 7 个快捷键命令，加载国际化。
2. **`onLayoutReady()`**：初始化配置管理器，创建 `<canvas id="bglayer">` 背景层，验证资产目录（处理迁移），加载配置，应用背景设置，如果必要则移除主题刷新对话框。
3. **`onunload()`**：移除 `#bglayer` 元素，移除主体的 `opacity` 样式，日志记录。
4. **`openSetting()`**：委托给 `settingsUI.openSettingDialog()`。

**全局 API 表面**：`window.bgCoverPlugin = { i18n, isMobileLayout, isBrowser, isAndroid, isDev }`——由所有其他模块用来访问国际化字符串和环境状态，而无需传递 plugin 实例。

---

### 6. 所有 UI 组件及其用途

| 组件 | 文件 | 用途 |
|-----------|------|---------|
| **顶部栏菜单** | `src/ui/topbar.ts` | 通过 `addTopBar()` 在右侧添加插件图标按钮；点击展开菜单：选择图片（手动/随机），添加图片（多文件/文件夹），插件开关，Bug 报告，设置 |
| **设置面板** | `src/ui/settings.ts` | 在 `openSettingDialog()` 中构建一个 5 选项卡的对话框（~550 行模板 HTML）；处理所有交互和配置持久化 |
| **配置选项卡** | 设置面板内 | 当前图片名称 + X/Y 偏移滑块，开关开启/关闭，自动刷新开关 + 时间输入，透明度滑块，模糊滑块 |
| **资产选项卡** | 设置面板内 | 显示缓存目录路径 + 图片数量，打开缓存管理器的按钮 |
| **主题选项卡** | 设置面板内 | 为已安装的暗色主题和亮色主题动态生成每个主题的开/关切换；高亮当前活动主题 |
| **高级选项卡** | 设置面板内 | 重置按钮（删除缓存 + 重置配置），开发者模式切换（显示诊断信息） |
| **关于选项卡** | 设置面板内 | 版本号，支付宝/微信捐赠二维码 |
| **缓存管理器对话框** | `src/ui/fileManager.ts` | 列出所有缓存图片的滚动列表（显示名称，悬停预览缩略图），每项："设为背景"按钮，"删除"按钮，"删除全部"按钮 |
| **资产文件夹选取器** | `src/ui/fileManager.ts` | 用于从 `data/assets/` 选取文件夹的树形视图对话框（已实现但目前在菜单中被注释掉） |
| **通知对话框** | `src/ui/notice.ts` | 主题更改时的刷新提示对话框，Bug 报告确认，功能未实现提示 |
| **对话框工厂** | `src/ui/components/dialogs.ts` | 为整个插件使用的通用确认/通知对话框，具有一致的样式 |
| **对话框模板** | `src/ui/components/templates.ts` | 生成确认和通知对话框 HTML 的纯函数 |

---

### 7. 所有设置 / 数据管理

该插件实现了**两层存储架构**：

| 层级 | 存储位置 | 用途 | 内容 |
|-------|----------------|------|----------|
| **本地配置** | 思源的 `localStorage`（键：`"siyuan-plugin-background-cover"`） | 每设备设置（不同步） | `version`, `crtBgObj`, `bgObjCfg`（每图 X/Y 偏移）, `prevTheme`, `autoRefresh`, `autoRefreshTime`, `opacity`, `blur`, `activate`, `disabledTheme`（按主题黑名单）, `inDev` |
| **同步配置** | `plugin.loadData("configs.json")` → `/data/storage/petal/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/` → 实际存储于思源的发布/同步系统 | 跨设备设置（同步） | `fileidx`（哈希到 bgObj 的映射）, `noteAssetsFolder` |

**ConfigManager**（`src/utils/configs.ts`）：
- 单例模式（`export const confmngr`）
- API：`get(key)`, `set(key, value)`, `remove(key)`, `load()`, `save()`, `reset()`
- 跟踪 `changedKeys` 的脏检测，实现按需持久化
- 启动时从各自的存储层读取，将值合并到默认值之上

**图片存储**：上传的图片存储在 `/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/` 中，文件名为 `hash-{md5slice}.{ext}`。一个 `fileIdx` 映射（同步配置）通过 15 个字符的 MD5 哈希跟踪所有图片，并附带元数据（名称、路径、尺寸、父级资产）。Nya~♡
</task_result>
```

26: import { CUSTOM_CSS_FILE_PATH } from './FileDom';
27: import { BackgroundCoverViewProvider } from './backgroundCoverView';
28: 
29: 
30: export function activate(context: ExtensionContext) {
31: 	setContext(context);
32: 	// 创建底部按钮 - 背景图片配置
33: 	let backImgBtn = window.createStatusBarItem(StatusBarAlignment.Right, -999);
34: 	backImgBtn.text = '$(file-media)';
35: 	backImgBtn.command = 'extension.backgroundCover.showMenu';
36: 	backImgBtn.tooltip = 'Switch background image / 切换背景图';
37: 	backImgBtn.show();
38: 	context.subscriptions.push(backImgBtn);
39: 
40: 	// 创建底部按钮 - 粒子效果配置
41: 	let particleBtn = window.createStatusBarItem(StatusBarAlignment.Right, -999);
42: 	particleBtn.text = '$(sparkle)';
43: 	particleBtn.command = 'extension.backgroundCover.nest';
44: 	particleBtn.tooltip = 'Particle effect / 粒子效果';
45: 	particleBtn.show();
46: 	context.subscriptions.push(particleBtn);
47: 
48: 	// 异步检查 VSCode 版本变化，不阻塞启动
49: 	checkVSCodeVersionChanged(context).then(isChanged => {
50: 		if (!isChanged) {
51: 			const config = workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
52: 			if (config.imagePath && !fs.existsSync(CUSTOM_CSS_FILE_PATH)) {
53: 				window.showInformationMessage(
54: 					'BackgroundCover 3.0：新版本支持免重启切换背景，需要重新初始化核心文件。是否立即执行？ / BackgroundCover 3.0: Supports background switching without restart. Core file re-initialization required. Proceed?',
55: 					'Yes', 'No'
56: 				).then(result => {
57: 					if (result === 'Yes') {
58: 						PickList.needAutoUpdate(config);
59: 					}
60: 				});
61: 			} else {
62: 				// 防止同时运行
63: 				PickList.autoUpdateBackground();
64: 			}
65: 		}
66: 	});
67: 
68: 	// 启动自动更换任务
69: 	PickList.startAutoRandomTask();
70: 
71: 	// 监听配置变化
72: 	context.subscriptions.push(workspace.onDidChangeConfiguration(e => {
73: 		if (e.affectsConfiguration('backgroundCover.autoStatus') || e.affectsConfiguration('backgroundCover.autoInterval')) {
74: 			PickList.startAutoRandomTask();
75: 		}
76: 	}));
77: 
78: 	let randomCommand = commands.registerCommand('extension.backgroundCover.refresh', () => { PickList.randomUpdateBackground(); });
79: 	let startCommand = commands.registerCommand('extension.backgroundCover.start', () => { 
80: 		commands.executeCommand('setContext', 'backgroundCover.mode', 'menu');
81: 		commands.executeCommand('workbench.view.extension.backgroundCover-explorer');
82: 	});
83: 	let particleEffectCommand = commands.registerCommand('extension.backgroundCover.nest', () => { PickList.startNest() });
84: 	let showMenuCommand = commands.registerCommand('extension.backgroundCover.showMenu', () => {
85: 		commands.executeCommand('setContext', 'backgroundCover.mode', 'menu');
86: 		commands.executeCommand('workbench.view.extension.backgroundCover-explorer');
87: 	});
88: 	context.subscriptions.push(startCommand);
89: 	context.subscriptions.push(randomCommand);
90: 	context.subscriptions.push(particleEffectCommand);
91: 	context.subscriptions.push(showMenuCommand);
92: 
93: 	// webview
94: 	const readerViewProvider = new ReaderViewProvider();
95: 	window.registerWebviewViewProvider('backgroundCover.readerView', readerViewProvider, {
96: 	  webviewOptions: {
97: 		retainContextWhenHidden: true,
98: 	  },
99: 	});
100: 	commands.registerCommand('backgroundCover.refreshEntry',() => {
101: 		commands.executeCommand('setContext', 'backgroundCover.mode', 'gallery');
102: 		readerViewProvider.refresh()
103: 		}
104: 	);
105: 	commands.registerCommand('backgroundCover.home',() => {
106: 		commands.executeCommand('setContext', 'backgroundCover.mode', 'gallery');
107: 		readerViewProvider.home();
108: 	});
109: 	commands.registerCommand('backgroundCover.switchMode',() => {
110: 		commands.executeCommand('setContext', 'backgroundCover.mode', 'menu');
111: 	});
112: 	commands.registerCommand('backgroundCover.support',() => readerViewProvider.support());
113: 
114: 	// Register Tree Data Provider
115: 	const backgroundCoverViewProvider = new BackgroundCoverViewProvider();
116: 	window.registerTreeDataProvider('backgroundCover.menu', backgroundCoverViewProvider);
117: 
118: 	// Register Command for Tree Item Click
119: 	context.subscriptions.push(commands.registerCommand('backgroundCover.runAction', (type: number, path?: string) => {
120: 		const config = workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
121: 		const quickPick = window.createQuickPick<ImgItem>();
122: 		const pickList = new PickList(config, quickPick);
123: 		pickList.handleAction(type, path);
124: 	}));
125: 
126: 
127: 	context.subscriptions.push(commands.registerCommand('backgroundCover.setConfig', async (key: string, value: any) => {
128: 		const config = workspace.getConfiguration();
129: 		await config.update(key, value, true);
130: 		// Trigger update
131: 		const newConfig = workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
132: 		PickList.needAutoUpdate(newConfig);
133: 	}));
134: 
135: 	// Initialize context
136: 	commands.executeCommand('setContext', 'backgroundCover.mode', 'menu');
137: 
138: 	// 监听主题变化
139: 	window.onDidChangeActiveColorTheme((event) => {
140:         PickList.autoUpdateBlendModel();
141:     });

145: 	 // 首次打开-提示语
146: 	let openVersion:string|undefined           = context.globalState.get('ext_version');
147: 	let ex:Extension<any>|undefined = extensions.getExtension('manasxx.background-cover');
148: 	let version:string           = ex ? ex.packageJSON['version'] : '';
149:

151: 		context.globalState.update('ext_version',version);
152: 		vsHelp.showInfoSupport(`🎉 BackgroundCover 已更新至 ${version}
153: 🚀 更新内容：
154:     1.  修复远程随机图片自动切换时 "Lock file is already being held" 错误 (#193 by @Aierlanta)
155:     2.  优化自动轮播任务防止并发执行 (#193 by @Aierlanta)
156:     3.  修复 code-server 模式下静态资源缓存导致背景不更新的问题 (#194 by @WaaSakura)
157: 
158: 感谢 @Aierlanta 和 @WaaSakura 的贡献！
159: ❤️ 觉得好用吗？支持一下在线图库运营吧！`);
160: 	}
161: }
162: 
163: // 检查 VSCode 版本是否变化
164: async function checkVSCodeVersionChanged(context: ExtensionContext): Promise<boolean> {
165: 	// 获取配置
166: 	let config = workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
167: 	// 如果没有设置背景图，则不处理
168: 	if (!config.imagePath) {
169: 		return false;
170: 	}
171: 
172: 	// 从全局状态中获取上次记录的 VSCode 版本
173: 	let lastVSCodeVersion = context.globalState.get('vscode_version');
174: 	// 如果版本不同，说明 VSCode 更新了
175: 	if (lastVSCodeVersion && lastVSCodeVersion !== vscodeVersion) {
176: 		// 弹出提示框确认是否更新背景
177: 		const value = await window.showInformationMessage(
178: 			`检测到 VSCode 已更新，背景图可能已被重置，是否重新应用背景图？ / Reapply the background image?`,
179: 			'YES',
180: 			'NO'
181: 		);
182: 		
183: 		if (value === 'YES') {
184: 			// 更新DOM
185: 			PickList.needAutoUpdate(config);
186: 		}
187: 		
188: 		// 更新全局状态中的 VSCode 版本
189: 		context.globalState.update('vscode_version', vscodeVersion);
190: 		return true;
191: 	}
192: 
193: 	// 修复：首次运行或版本未记录时，也需要更新版本号，防止下次误判
194: 	if (!lastVSCodeVersion) {
195: 		context.globalState.update('vscode_version', vscodeVersion);
196: 	}
197: 
198: 	return false;
199: }
200: 
201: // this method is called when your extension is deactivated
202: export function deactivate() {
203: 	PickList.stopAutoRandomTask();
204: }
205: 

(End of file - total 205 lines)
</content>

84:         return messages.zh[key];
85:     }

89: // Define a data structure for tree items
90: export class ConfigItem extends vscode.TreeItem {
91:     constructor(
92:         public readonly label: string,
93:         public readonly collapsibleState: vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState,
94:         public readonly type: 'group' | 'setting' | 'action' | 'value',
95:         public readonly key?: string, // Config key e.g. 'backgroundCover.opacity'
96:         public readonly value?: any, // Value for 'value' type items
97:         public readonly commandType?: ActionType, // For mapping to PickList actions
98:         public readonly description?: string,
99:         public readonly icon?: string
100:     ) {
101:         super(label, collapsibleState);
102:         this.contextValue = type;
103:         if (description) {
104:             this.description = description;
105:         }
106:         if (icon) {
107:             this.iconPath = new vscode.ThemeIcon(icon);
108:         }

112: export class BackgroundCoverViewProvider implements vscode.TreeDataProvider<ConfigItem> {
113:     private _onDidChangeTreeData: vscode.EventEmitter<ConfigItem | undefined | void> = new vscode.EventEmitter<ConfigItem | undefined | void>();
114:     readonly onDidChangeTreeData: vscode.Event<ConfigItem | undefined | void> = this._onDidChangeTreeData.event;
115: 
116:     constructor() {
117:         vscode.workspace.onDidChangeConfiguration(e => {
118:             if (e.affectsConfiguration('backgroundCover')) {
119:                 this.refresh();
120:             }
121:         });
122: 
123:         onDidChangeGlobalState.event(() => {
124:             this.refresh();
125:         });
126:     }
127: 
128:     refresh(): void {
129:         this._onDidChangeTreeData.fire();
130:     }
131: 
132:     getTreeItem(element: ConfigItem): vscode.TreeItem {
133:         return element;
134:     }
135: 
136:     getChildren(element?: ConfigItem): Thenable<ConfigItem[]> {
137:         const config = vscode.workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
138:         
139:         if (!element) {
140:             return Promise.resolve(this.getRootItems(config));
141:         }
142: 
143:         if (element.type === 'group') {
144:             return Promise.resolve(this.getGroupChildren(element, config));
145:         }
146: 
147:         if (element.type === 'setting' && element.key === 'backgroundCover.sizeModel') {
148:              return Promise.resolve(this.getSizeModeOptions(config));
149:         }
150:         
151:         if (element.type === 'setting' && element.key === 'backgroundCover.blendModel') {
152:              return Promise.resolve(this.getBlendModeOptions(config));
153:         }
154: 
155:         return Promise.resolve([]);
156:     }
157: 
158:     private getRootItems(config: vscode.WorkspaceConfiguration): ConfigItem[] {
159:         const items: ConfigItem[] = [];
160: 
161:         // 1. Image Source
162:         items.push(new ConfigItem(t('imageSource'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.Expanded, 'group', undefined, undefined, undefined, undefined, 'file-media'));
163: 
164:         // 2. Appearance
165:         items.push(new ConfigItem(t('appearance'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.Expanded, 'group', undefined, undefined, undefined, undefined, 'paintcan'));
166: 
167:         // 3. Auto Random
168:         items.push(new ConfigItem(t('autoRandom'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.Collapsed, 'group', undefined, undefined, undefined, undefined, 'sync'));
169: 
170:         // 4. Particle Effects
171:         items.push(new ConfigItem(t('particleEffects'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.Collapsed, 'group', undefined, undefined, undefined, undefined, 'sparkle'));
172: 
173:         // 5. Pet Assistant
174:         items.push(new ConfigItem(t('petAssistant'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.Collapsed, 'group', undefined, undefined, undefined, undefined, 'github'));
175: 
176:         // 6. Actions
177:         items.push(new ConfigItem(t('actions'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.Expanded, 'group', undefined, undefined, undefined, undefined, 'tools'));
178: 
179:         return items;
180:     }
181: 
182:     private getGroupChildren(element: ConfigItem, config: vscode.WorkspaceConfiguration): ConfigItem[] {
183:         const items: ConfigItem[] = [];
184: 
185:         const context = getContext();
186:         const onlineFolder = context?.globalState.get<string>('backgroundCoverOnlineFolder');
187: 
188:         if (element.label === t('imageSource')) {
189:             const currentPath = config.get<string>('imagePath') || t('none');
190:             const displayPath = currentPath.length > 30 ? '...' + currentPath.substr(-30) : currentPath;
191:             
192:             items.push(new ConfigItem(t('currentImage'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None, 'value', undefined, undefined, undefined, displayPath, 'file'));
193:             
194:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('selectImage'), ActionType.SelectPictures, 'folder-opened'));
195:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('addDirectory'), ActionType.AddDirectory, 'file-directory'));
196:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('inputPath'), ActionType.InputPath, 'link'));
197: 
198:             if (onlineFolder) {
199:                 const displayOnlineFolder = onlineFolder.length > 30 ? '...' + onlineFolder.substr(-30) : onlineFolder;
200:                 items.push(this.createActionItem(t('refreshFolder'), ActionType.RefreshOnlineFolder, 'cloud-download', displayOnlineFolder));
201:             }
202:         }
203: 
204:         if (element.label === t('appearance')) {
205:             items.push(this.createSettingItem(t('opacity'), 'backgroundCover.opacity', config.get('opacity'), ActionType.BackgroundOpacity, 'eye'));
206:             items.push(this.createSettingItem(t('blur'), 'backgroundCover.blur', config.get('blur'), ActionType.BackgroundBlur, 'star-half'));
207:             
208:             items.push(new ConfigItem(t('sizeMode'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.Collapsed, 'setting', 'backgroundCover.sizeModel', config.get('sizeModel'), undefined, config.get('sizeModel'), 'layout'));
209:             items.push(new ConfigItem(t('blendMode'), vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.Collapsed, 'setting', 'backgroundCover.blendModel', config.get('blendModel'), undefined, config.get('blendModel'), 'symbol-color'));
210:         }
211: 
212:         if (element.label === t('autoRandom')) {
213:             const status = config.get<boolean>('autoStatus') || false;
214:             items.push(this.createToggleItem(t('enabled'), 'backgroundCover.autoStatus', status, 'play-circle'));
215:             items.push(this.createSettingItem(t('interval'), 'backgroundCover.autoInterval', config.get('autoInterval'), ActionType.AutoRandomSettings, 'watch'));
216:             
217:             const randomFolder = config.get<string>('randomImageFolder') || t('notSet');
218:             const displayFolder = randomFolder.length > 30 ? '...' + randomFolder.substr(-30) : randomFolder;
219:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('sourceFolder'), ActionType.AddDirectory, 'folder', displayFolder));
220:         }
221: 
222:         if (element.label === t('particleEffects')) {
223:             const context = getContext();
224:             const enabled = context.globalState.get<boolean>('backgroundCoverParticleEffect', false);
225:             const opacity = context.globalState.get<number>('backgroundCoverParticleOpacity', 0.6);
226:             const color = context.globalState.get<string>('backgroundCoverParticleColor', '#ffffff');
227:             const count = context.globalState.get<number>('backgroundCoverParticleCount', 50);
228: 
229:             // Toggle
230:             const toggleItem = new ConfigItem(
231:                 t('toggleParticles'), 
232:                 vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None, 
233:                 'setting', 
234:                 'backgroundCoverParticleEffect', 
235:                 enabled, 
236:                 ActionType.ToggleParticle, 
237:                 enabled ? 'ON' : 'OFF', 
238:                 enabled ? 'check' : 'circle-outline'
239:             );
240:             toggleItem.command = {
241:                 command: 'backgroundCover.runAction',
242:                 title: t('toggleParticles'),
243:                 arguments: [ActionType.ToggleParticle]
244:             };
245:             items.push(toggleItem);
246: 
247:             items.push(this.createSettingItem(t('particleOpacity'), 'backgroundCoverParticleOpacity', opacity, ActionType.ParticleOpacity, 'eye'));
248:             items.push(this.createSettingItem(t('particleColor'), 'backgroundCoverParticleColor', color, ActionType.ParticleColor, 'symbol-color'));
249:             items.push(this.createSettingItem(t('particleCount'), 'backgroundCoverParticleCount', count, ActionType.ParticleCount, 'multiple-windows'));
250:         }
251: 
252:         if (element.label === t('petAssistant')) {
253:             const context = getContext();
254:             const enabled = context.globalState.get<boolean>('backgroundCoverPetEnabled', true);
255:             const currentPet = context.globalState.get<string>('backgroundCoverPetType', 'akita');
256: 
257:             // Toggle
258:             const toggleItem = new ConfigItem(
259:                 t('togglePet'), 
260:                 vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None, 
261:                 'setting', 
262:                 'backgroundCoverPetEnabled', 
263:                 enabled, 
264:                 ActionType.TogglePet, 
265:                 enabled ? 'ON' : 'OFF', 
266:                 enabled ? 'check' : 'circle-outline'
267:             );
268:             toggleItem.command = {
269:                 command: 'backgroundCover.runAction',
270:                 title: t('togglePet'),
271:                 arguments: [ActionType.TogglePet]
272:             };
273:             items.push(toggleItem);
274: 
275:             // Select Pet
276:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('selectPet'), ActionType.SelectPet, 'github', currentPet));
277:         }
278: 
279:         if (element.label === t('actions')) {
280:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('clearBackground'), ActionType.CloseBackground, 'trash'));
281:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('refresh'), ActionType.UpdateBackground, 'refresh'));
282:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('openCacheFolder'), ActionType.OpenCacheFolder, 'folder-opened'));
283:             items.push(this.createActionItem(t('supportAuthor'), ActionType.OpenFilePath, 'heart', undefined, '//resources//support.jpg'));
284:         }
285: 
286:         return items;
287:     }

289:     private getSizeModeOptions(config: vscode.WorkspaceConfiguration): ConfigItem[] {
290:         const modes = [
291:             "cover", "repeat", "contain", "center", "not_center", 
292:             "not_right_bottom", "not_right_top", "not_left", 
293:             "not_right", "not_top", "not_bottom"
294:         ];
295:         const current = config.get<string>('sizeModel');
296:         
297:         return modes.map(mode => {
298:             const item = new ConfigItem(mode, vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None, 'value', 'backgroundCover.sizeModel', mode, undefined, undefined, current === mode ? 'check' : 'circle-outline');
299:             item.command = {
300:                 command: 'backgroundCover.setConfig',
301:                 title: t('setSizeMode'),
302:                 arguments: ['backgroundCover.sizeModel', mode]
303:             };
304:             return item;
305:         });
306:     }
307: 
308:     private getBlendModeOptions(config: vscode.WorkspaceConfiguration): ConfigItem[] {
309:         const modes = ["auto", "multiply", "lighten"];
310:         const current = config.get<string>('blendModel');
311:         
312:         return modes.map(mode => {
313:             const item = new ConfigItem(mode, vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None, 'value', 'backgroundCover.blendModel', mode, undefined, undefined, current === mode ? 'check' : 'circle-outline');
314:             item.command = {
315:                 command: 'backgroundCover.setConfig',
316:                 title: t('setBlendMode'),
317:                 arguments: ['backgroundCover.blendModel', mode]
318:             };
319:             return item;
320:         });
321:     }
322: 
323:     private createActionItem(label: string, actionType: ActionType, icon: string, description?: string, path?: string): ConfigItem {
324:         const item = new ConfigItem(label, vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None, 'action', undefined, undefined, actionType, description, icon);
325:         item.command = {
326:             command: 'backgroundCover.runAction',
327:             title: label,
328:             arguments: [actionType, path]
329:         };
330:         return item;
331:     }
332: 
333:     private createSettingItem(label: string, key: string, value: any, actionType: ActionType, icon: string): ConfigItem {
334:         const item = new ConfigItem(label, vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None, 'setting', key, value, actionType, String(value), icon);
335:         item.command = {
336:             command: 'backgroundCover.runAction',
337:             title: label,
338:             arguments: [actionType]
339:         };
340:         return item;
341:     }
342: 
343:     private createToggleItem(label: string, key: string, value: boolean, icon: string): ConfigItem {
344:         const item = new ConfigItem(label, vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None, 'setting', key, value, undefined, value ? 'ON' : 'OFF', value ? 'check' : 'circle-outline');
345:         item.command = {
346:             command: 'backgroundCover.setConfig',
347:             title: t('toggle'),
348:             arguments: [key, !value]
349:         };
350:         return item;
351:     }

136:

139:         bgLayer.remove();

141: 
142:         info(`${this.i18n.byePlugin}`);

144: 
145:     private async themeOnChange() {
146:         const [themeMode, themeName] = getCurrentThemeInfo();
147:         let prevTheme = confmngr.get('prevTheme')
148: 
149:         debug(`Theme changed! from ${prevTheme} to ${themeMode} | ${themeName}`)
150: 
151:         if (prevTheme !== themeName) {
152:             // 更换主题时且没有重载时，提示需要刷新笔记页面
153:             confmngr.set('prevTheme', themeName);
154:             await confmngr.save('[index][themeOnChange]')
155:             noticeUI.themeRefreshDialog();
156:             // 如果重载了，这个界面会在onLoadReady时被去掉
157:         }
158:     }

71: 
72: ## Specification
73: 
74: ### Parameters and return values
75: 
76: * Endpoint: `http://127.0.0.1:6806`
77: * Both are POST methods
78: * An interface with parameters is required, the parameter is a JSON string, placed in the body, and the header
79:   Content-Type is `application/json`
80: * Return value
81: 
82:    ````json
83:    {
84:      "code": 0,
85:      "msg": "",
86:      "data": {}
87:    }
88:    ````
89: 
90:     * `code`: non-zero for exceptions
91:     * `msg`: an empty string under normal circumstances, an error text will be returned under abnormal conditions
92:     * `data`: may be `{}`, `[]` or `NULL`, depending on the interface
93: 
94: ### Authentication
95: 
96: View API token in <kbd>Settings - About</kbd>, request header: `Authorization: Token xxx`
97: 
98: ## Notebooks
99: 
100: ### List notebooks
101: 
102: * `/api/notebook/lsNotebooks`
103: * No parameters
104: * Return value
105: 
106:   ```json
107:   {
108:     "code": 0,
109:     "msg": "",
110:     "data": {
111:       "notebooks": [
112:         {
113:           "id": "20210817205410-2kvfpfn",

122:           "icon": "1f4d4",
123:           "sort": 1,
124:           "closed": false
125:         }
126:       ]
127:     }
128:   }
129:   ```

150:   }

317: 
318: ## Documents
319: 
320: ### Create a document with Markdown
321: 
322: * `/api/filetree/createDocWithMd`
323: * Parameters
324: 
325:   ```json
326:   {
327:     "notebook": "20210817205410-2kvfpfn",
328:     "path": "/foo/bar",
329:     "markdown": ""
330:   }
331:   ```
332: 
333:     * `notebook`: Notebook ID
334:     * `path`: Document path, which needs to start with / and separate levels with / (path here corresponds to the
335:       database hpath field)
336:     * `markdown`: GFM Markdown content
337: * Return value
338: 
339:   ```json
340:   {
341:     "code": 0,
342:     "msg": "",
343:     "data": "20210914223645-oj2vnx2"
344:   }
345:   ```
346: 
347:     * `data`: Created document ID
348:     * If you use the same `path` to call this interface repeatedly, the existing document will not be overwritten
349: 
350: ### Rename a document
351: 
352: * `/api/filetree/renameDoc`
353: * Parameters
354: 
355:   ```json
356:   {
357:     "notebook": "20210831090520-7dvbdv0",
358:     "path": "/20210902210113-0avi12f.sy",
359:     "title": "New document title"
360:   }
361:   ```
362: 
363:     * `notebook`: Notebook ID
364:     * `path`: Document path
365:     * `title`: New document title
366: * Return value
367: 
368:   ```json
369:   {
370:     "code": 0,
371:     "msg": "",
372:     "data": null
373:   }
374:   ```
375: 
376: Rename a document by `id`:
377: 
378: * `/api/filetree/renameDocByID`
379: * Parameters
380: 
381:   ```json
382:   {
383:     "id": "20210902210113-0avi12f",
384:     "title": "New document title"
385:   }
386:   ```
387: 
388:     * `id`: Document ID
389:     * `title`: New document title
390: * Return value
391: 
392:   ```json
393:   {
394:     "code": 0,
395:     "msg": "",
396:     "data": null
397:   }
398:   ```
399: 
400: ### Remove a document
401: 
402: * `/api/filetree/removeDoc`
403: * Parameters
404: 
405:   ```json
406:   {
407:     "notebook": "20210831090520-7dvbdv0",
408:     "path": "/20210902210113-0avi12f.sy"
409:   }
410:   ```
411: 
412:     * `notebook`: Notebook ID
413:     * `path`: Document path
414: * Return value
415: 
416:   ```json
417:   {
418:     "code": 0,
419:     "msg": "",
420:     "data": null
421:   }
422:   ```
423: 
424: Remove a document by `id`:
425: 
426: * `/api/filetree/removeDocByID`
427: * Parameters
428: 
429:   ```json
430:   {
431:     "id": "20210902210113-0avi12f"
432:   }
433:   ```
434: 
435:     * `id`: Document ID
436: * Return value
437: 
438:   ```json
439:   {
440:     "code": 0,
441:     "msg": "",
442:     "data": null
443:   }
444:   ```
445: 
446: ### Move documents
447: 
448: * `/api/filetree/moveDocs`
449: * Parameters
450: 
451:   ```json
452:   {
453:     "fromPaths": ["/20210917220056-yxtyl7i.sy"],
454:     "toNotebook": "20210817205410-2kvfpfn",
455:     "toPath": "/"
456:   }
457:   ```
458: 
459:     * `fromPaths`: Source paths
460:     * `toNotebook`: Target notebook ID
461:     * `toPath`: Target path
462: * Return value
463: 
464:   ```json
465:   {
466:     "code": 0,
467:     "msg": "",
468:     "data": null
469:   }
470:   ```
471: 
472: Move documents by `id`:
473: 
474: * `/api/filetree/moveDocsByID`
475: * Parameters
476: 
477:   ```json
478:   {
479:     "fromIDs": ["20210917220056-yxtyl7i"],
480:     "toID": "20210817205410-2kvfpfn"
481:   }
482:   ```
483: 
484:     * `fromIDs`: Source docs' IDs
485:     * `toID`: Target parent doc's ID or notebook ID
486: * Return value
487: 
488:   ```json
489:   {
490:     "code": 0,
491:     "msg": "",
492:     "data": null
493:   }
494:   ```
495: 
496: ### Get human-readable path based on path
497: 
498: * `/api/filetree/getHPathByPath`
499: * Parameters
500: 
501:   ```json
502:   {
503:     "notebook": "20210831090520-7dvbdv0",
504:     "path": "/20210917220500-sz588nq/20210917220056-yxtyl7i.sy"
505:   }
506:   ```
507: 
508:     * `notebook`: Notebook ID
509:     * `path`: Document path
510: * Return value
511: 
512:   ```json
513:   {
514:     "code": 0,
515:     "msg": "",
516:     "data": "/foo/bar"
517:   }
518:   ```
519: 
520: ### Get human-readable path based on ID
521: 
522: * `/api/filetree/getHPathByID`
523: * Parameters
524: 
525:   ```json
526:   {
527:     "id": "20210917220056-yxtyl7i"
528:   }
529:   ```
530: 
531:     * `id`: Block ID
532: * Return value
533: 
534:   ```json
535:   {
536:     "code": 0,
537:     "msg": "",
538:     "data": "/foo/bar"
539:   }
540:   ```
541: 
542: ### Get storage path based on ID
543: 
544: * `/api/filetree/getPathByID`
545: * Parameters
546: 
547:   ```json
548:   {
549:     "id": "20210808180320-fqgskfj"
550:   }
551:   ```
552: 
553:     * `id`: Block ID
554: * Return value
555: 
556:   ```json
557:   {
558:     "code": 0,
559:     "msg": "",
560:     "data": {
561:     "notebook": "20210808180117-czj9bvb",
562:     "path": "/20200812220555-lj3enxa/20210808180320-fqgskfj.sy"
563:     }
564:   }
565:   ```
566: 
567: ### Get IDs based on human-readable path
568: 
569: * `/api/filetree/getIDsByHPath`
570: * Parameters
571: 
572:   ```json
573:   {
574:     "path": "/foo/bar",
575:     "notebook": "20210808180117-czj9bvb"
576:   }
577:   ```
578: 
579:     * `path`: Human-readable path
580:     * `notebook`: Notebook ID
581: * Return value
582: 
583:   ```json
584:   {
585:     "code": 0,
586:     "msg": "",
587:     "data": [
588:         "20200813004931-q4cu8na"
589:     ]
590:   }
591:   ```
592: 
593: ## Assets
594: 
595: ### Upload assets
596: 
597: * `/api/asset/upload`
598: * The parameter is an HTTP Multipart form
599: 
600:     * `assetsDirPath`: The folder path where assets are stored, with the data folder as the root path, for example:
601:         * `"/assets/"`: workspace/data/assets/ folder
602:         * `"/assets/sub/"`: workspace/data/assets/sub/ folder
603: 
604:       Under normal circumstances, it is recommended to use the first method, which is stored in the assets folder of the
605:       workspace, putting in a subdirectory has some side effects, please refer to the assets chapter of the user guide.
606:     * `file[]`: Uploaded file list
607: * Return value
608: 
609:   ```json
610:   {
611:     "code": 0,
612:     "msg": "",
613:     "data": {
614:       "errFiles": [""],
615:       "succMap": {
616:         "foo.png": "assets/foo-20210719092549-9j5y79r.png"
617:       }
618:     }
619:   }
620:   ```
621: 
622:     * `errFiles`: List of filenames with errors in upload processing
623:     * `succMap`: For successfully processed files, the key is the file name when uploading, and the value is
624:       assets/foo-id.png, which is used to replace the asset link address in the existing Markdown content with the
625:       uploaded address
626: 
627: ## Blocks
628: 
629: ### Insert blocks
630: 
631: * `/api/block/insertBlock`
632: * Parameters
633: 
634:   ```json
635:   {
636:     "dataType": "markdown",
637:     "data": "foo**bar**{: style=\"color: var(--b3-font-color8);\"}baz",
638:     "nextID": "",
639:     "previousID": "20211229114650-vrek5x6",
640:     "parentID": ""
641:   }
642:   ```
643: 
644:     * `dataType`: The data type to be inserted, the value can be `markdown` or `dom`
645:     * `data`: Data to be inserted
646:     * `nextID`: The ID of the next block, used to anchor the insertion position
647:     * `previousID`: The ID of the previous block, used to anchor the insertion position
648:     * `parentID`: The ID of the parent block, used to anchor the insertion position
649: 
650:   `nextID`, `previousID`, and `parentID` must have at least one value, using priority: `nextID` > `previousID` >
651:   `parentID`
652: * Return value
653: 
654:   ```json
655:   {
656:     "code": 0,
657:     "msg": "",
658:     "data": [
659:       {
660:         "doOperations": [
661:           {
662:             "action": "insert",
663:             "data": "<div data-node-id=\"20211230115020-g02dfx0\" data-node-index=\"1\" data-type=\"NodeParagraph\" class=\"p\"><div contenteditable=\"true\" spellcheck=\"false\">foo<strong style=\"color: var(--b3-font-color8);\">bar</strong>baz</div><div class=\"protyle-attr\" contenteditable=\"false\"></div></div>",
664:             "id": "20211230115020-g02dfx0",
665:             "parentID": "",
666:             "previousID": "20211229114650-vrek5x6",
667:             "retData": null
668:           }
669:         ],
670:         "undoOperations": null
671:       }
672:     ]
673:   }
674:   ```
675: 
676:     * `action.data`: DOM generated by the newly inserted block
677:     * `action.id`: ID of the newly inserted block
678: 
679: ### Prepend blocks
680: 
681: * `/api/block/prependBlock`
682: * Parameters
683: 
684:   ```json
685:   {
686:     "data": "foo**bar**{: style=\"color: var(--b3-font-color8);\"}baz",
687:     "dataType": "markdown",
688:     "parentID": "20220107173950-7f9m1nb"
689:   }
690:   ```
691: 
692:     * `dataType`: The data type to be inserted, the value can be `markdown` or `dom`
693:     * `data`: Data to be inserted
694:     * `parentID`: The ID of the parent block, used to anchor the insertion position
695: * Return value
696: 
697:   ```json
698:   {
699:     "code": 0,
700:     "msg": "",
701:     "data": [
702:       {
703:         "doOperations": [
704:           {
705:             "action": "insert",
706:             "data": "<div data-node-id=\"20220108003710-hm0x9sc\" data-node-index=\"1\" data-type=\"NodeParagraph\" class=\"p\"><div contenteditable=\"true\" spellcheck=\"false\">foo<strong style=\"color: var(--b3-font-color8);\">bar</strong>baz</div><div class=\"protyle-attr\" contenteditable=\"false\"></div></div>",
707:             "id": "20220108003710-hm0x9sc",
708:             "parentID": "20220107173950-7f9m1nb",
709:             "previousID": "",
710:             "retData": null
711:           }
712:         ],
713:         "undoOperations": null
714:       }
715:     ]
716:   }
717:   ```
718: 
719:     * `action.data`: DOM generated by the newly inserted block
720:     * `action.id`: ID of the newly inserted block
721: 
722: ### Append blocks
723: 
724: * `/api/block/appendBlock`
725: * Parameters
726: 
727:   ```json
728:   {
729:     "data": "foo**bar**{: style=\"color: var(--b3-font-color8);\"}baz",
730:     "dataType": "markdown",
731:     "parentID": "20220107173950-7f9m1nb"
732:   }
733:   ```
734: 
735:     * `dataType`: The data type to be inserted, the value can be `markdown` or `dom`
736:     * `data`: Data to be inserted
737:     * `parentID`: The ID of the parent block, used to anchor the insertion position
738: * Return value
739: 
740:   ```json
741:   {
742:     "code": 0,
743:     "msg": "",
744:     "data": [
745:       {
746:         "doOperations": [
747:           {
748:             "action": "insert",
749:             "data": "<div data-node-id=\"20220108003642-y2wmpcv\" data-node-index=\"1\" data-type=\"NodeParagraph\" class=\"p\"><div contenteditable=\"true\" spellcheck=\"false\">foo<strong style=\"color: var(--b3-font-color8);\">bar</strong>baz</div><div class=\"protyle-attr\" contenteditable=\"false\"></div></div>",
750:             "id": "20220108003642-y2wmpcv",
751:             "parentID": "20220107173950-7f9m1nb",
752:             "previousID": "20220108003615-7rk41t1",
753:             "retData": null
754:           }
755:         ],
756:         "undoOperations": null
757:       }
758:     ]
759:   }
760:   ```
761: 
762:     * `action.data`: DOM generated by the newly inserted block
763:     * `action.id`: ID of the newly inserted block
764: 
765: ### Update a block
766: 
767: * `/api/block/updateBlock`
768: * Parameters
769: 
770:   ```json
771:   {
772:     "dataType": "markdown",
773:     "data": "foobarbaz",
774:     "id": "20211230161520-querkps"
775:   }
776:   ```
777: 
778:     * `dataType`: The data type to be updated, the value can be `markdown` or `dom`
779:     * `data`: Data to be updated
780:     * `id`: ID of the block to be updated
781: * Return value
782: 
783:   ```json
784:   {
785:     "code": 0,
786:     "msg": "",
787:     "data": [
788:       {
789:         "doOperations": [
790:           {
791:             "action": "update",
792:             "data": "<div data-node-id=\"20211230161520-querkps\" data-node-index=\"1\" data-type=\"NodeParagraph\" class=\"p\"><div contenteditable=\"true\" spellcheck=\"false\">foo<strong>bar</strong>baz</div><div class=\"protyle-attr\" contenteditable=\"false\"></div></div>",
793:             "id": "20211230161520-querkps",
794:             "parentID": "",
795:             "previousID": "",
796:             "retData": null
797:             }
798:           ],
799:         "undoOperations": null
800:       }
801:     ]
802:   }
803:   ```
804: 
805:     * `action.data`: DOM generated by the updated block
806: 
807: ### Delete a block
808: 
809: * `/api/block/deleteBlock`
810: * Parameters
811: 
812:   ```json
813:   {
814:     "id": "20211230161520-querkps"
815:   }
816:   ```
817: 
818:     * `id`: ID of the block to be deleted
819: * Return value
820: 
821:   ```json
822:   {
823:     "code": 0,
824:     "msg": "",
825:     "data": [
826:       {
827:         "doOperations": [
828:           {
829:             "action": "delete",
830:             "data": null,
831:             "id": "20211230162439-vtm09qo",
832:             "parentID": "",
833:             "previousID": "",
834:             "retData": null
835:           }
836:         ],
837:        "undoOperations": null
838:       }
839:     ]
840:   }
841:   ```
842: 
843: ### Move a block
844: 
845: * `/api/block/moveBlock`
846: * Parameters
847: 
848:   ```json
849:   {
850:     "id": "20230406180530-3o1rqkc",
851:     "previousID": "20230406152734-if5kyx6",
852:     "parentID": "20230404183855-woe52ko"
853:   }
854:   ```
855: 
856:     * `id`: Block ID to move
857:     * `previousID`: The ID of the previous block, used to anchor the insertion position
858:     * `parentID`: The ID of the parent block, used to anchor the insertion position, `previousID` and `parentID` cannot
859:       be empty at the same time, if they exist at the same time, `previousID` will be used first
860: * Return value
861: 
862:   ```json
863:   {
864:     "code": 0,
865:     "msg": "",
866:     "data": [
867:         {
868:             "doOperations": [
869:                 {
870:                     "action": "move",
871:                     "data": null,
872:                     "id": "20230406180530-3o1rqkc",
873:                     "parentID": "20230404183855-woe52ko",
874:                     "previousID": "20230406152734-if5kyx6",
875:                     "nextID": "",
876:                     "retData": null,
877:                     "srcIDs": null,
878:                     "name": "",
879:                     "type": ""
880:                 }
881:             ],
882:             "undoOperations": null
883:         }
884:     ]
885:   }
886:   ```
887: 
888: ### Fold a block
889: 
890: * `/api/block/foldBlock`
891: * Parameters
892: 
893:   ```json
894:   {
895:     "id": "20231224160424-2f5680o"
896:   }
897:   ```
898: 
899:     * `id`: Block ID to fold
900: * Return value
901: 
902:   ```json
903:   {
904:     "code": 0,
905:     "msg": "",
906:     "data": null
907:   }
908:   ```
909: 
910: ### Unfold a block
911: 
912: * `/api/block/unfoldBlock`
913: * Parameters
914: 
915:   ```json
916:   {
917:     "id": "20231224160424-2f5680o"
918:   }
919:   ```
920: 
921:     * `id`: Block ID to unfold
922: * Return value
923: 
924:   ```json
925:   {
926:     "code": 0,
927:     "msg": "",
928:     "data": null
929:   }
930:   ```
931: 
932: ### Get a block kramdown
933: 
934: * `/api/block/getBlockKramdown`
935: * Parameters
936: 
937:   ```json
938:   {
939:     "id": "20201225220954-dlgzk1o"
940:   }
941:   ```
942: 
943:     * `id`: ID of the block to be got
944: * Return value
945: 
946:   ```json
947:   {
948:     "code": 0,
949:     "msg": "",
950:     "data": {
951:       "id": "20201225220954-dlgzk1o",
952:       "kramdown": "* {: id=\"20201225220954-e913snx\"}Create a new notebook, create a new document under the notebook\n  {: id=\"20210131161940-kfs31q6\"}\n* {: id=\"20201225220954-ygz217h\"}Enter <kbd>/</kbd> in the editor to trigger the function menu\n  {: id=\"20210131161940-eo0riwq\"}\n* {: id=\"20201225220954-875yybt\"}((20200924101200-gss5vee \"Navigate in the content block\")) and ((20200924100906-0u4zfq3 \"Window and tab\"))\n  {: id=\"20210131161940-b5uow2h\"}"
953:     }
954:   }
955:   ```
956: 
957: ### Get child blocks
958: 
959: * `/api/block/getChildBlocks`
960: * Parameters
961: 
962:   ```json
963:   {
964:     "id": "20230506212712-vt9ajwj"
965:   }
966:   ```
967: 
968:     * `id`: Parent block ID
969:     * The blocks below a heading are also counted as child blocks
970: * Return value
971: 
972:   ```json
973:   {
974:     "code": 0,
975:     "msg": "",
976:     "data": [
977:       {
978:         "id": "20230512083858-mjdwkbn",
979:         "type": "h",
980:         "subType": "h1"
981:       },
982:       {
983:         "id": "20230513213727-thswvfd",
984:         "type": "s"
985:       },
986:       {
987:         "id": "20230513213633-9lsj4ew",
988:         "type": "l",
989:         "subType": "u"
990:       }
991:     ]
992:   }
993:   ```
994: 
995: ### Transfer block ref
996: 
997: * `/api/block/transferBlockRef`
998: * Parameters
999: 
1000:   ```json
1001:   {
1002:     "fromID": "20230612160235-mv6rrh1",
1003:     "toID": "20230613093045-uwcomng",
1004:     "refIDs": ["20230613092230-cpyimmd"]
1005:   }
1006:   ```
1007: 
1008:     * `fromID`: Def block ID
1009:     * `toID`: Target block ID
1010:     * `refIDs`: Ref block IDs point to def block ID, optional, if not specified, all ref block IDs will be transferred
1011: * Return value
1012: 
1013:   ```json
1014:   {
1015:     "code": 0,
1016:     "msg": "",
1017:     "data": null
1018:   }
1019:   ```
1020: 
1021: ## Attributes
1022: 
1023: ### Set block attributes
1024: 
1025: * `/api/attr/setBlockAttrs`
1026: * Parameters
1027: 
1028:   ```json
1029:   {
1030:     "id": "20210912214605-uhi5gco",
1031:     "attrs": {
1032:       "custom-attr1": "line1\nline2"
1033:     }
1034:   }
1035:   ```
1036: 
1037:     * `id`: Block ID
1038:     * `attrs`: Block attributes, custom attributes must be prefixed with `custom-`
1039: * Return value
1040: 
1041:   ```json
1042:   {
1043:     "code": 0,
1044:     "msg": "",
1045:     "data": null
1046:   }
1047:   ```
1048: 
1049: ### Get block attributes
1050: 
1051: * `/api/attr/getBlockAttrs`
1052: * Parameters
1053: 
1054:   ```json
1055:   {
1056:     "id": "20210912214605-uhi5gco"
1057:   }
1058:   ```
1059: 
1060:     * `id`: Block ID
1061: * Return value
1062: 
1063:   ```json
1064:   {
1065:     "code": 0,
1066:     "msg": "",
1067:     "data": {
1068:       "custom-attr1": "line1\nline2",
1069:       "id": "20210912214605-uhi5gco",
1070:       "title": "PDF Annotation Demo",
1071:       "type": "doc",
1072:       "updated": "20210916120715"
1073:     }
1074:   }
1075:   ```
1076: 
1077: ## SQL
1078: 
1079: ### Execute SQL query
1080: 
1081: * `/api/query/sql`
1082: * Parameters
1083: 
1084:   ```json
1085:   {
1086:     "stmt": "SELECT * FROM blocks WHERE content LIKE'%content%' LIMIT 7"
1087:   }
1088:   ```
1089: 
1090:     * `stmt`: SQL statement
1091: * Return value
1092: 
1093:   ```json
1094:   {
1095:     "code": 0,
1096:     "msg": "",
1097:     "data": [
1098:       { "col": "val" }
1099:     ]
1100:   }
1101:   ```
1102: 
1103: Note: To ensure data security, access to this interface is prohibited in Publish Mode.
1104: 
1105: ### Flush transaction
1106: 
1107: * `/api/sqlite/flushTransaction`
1108: * No parameters
1109: * Return value
1110: 
1111:   ```json
1112:   {
1113:     "code": 0,
1114:     "msg": "",
1115:     "data": null
1116:   }
1117:   ```
1118: 
1119: ## Templates
1120: 
1121: ### Render a template
1122: 
1123: * `/api/template/render`
1124: * Parameters
1125: 
1126:   ```json
1127:   {
1128:     "id": "20220724223548-j6g0o87",
1129:     "path": "F:\\SiYuan\\data\\templates\\foo.md"
1130:   }
1131:   ```
1132: 
1133:     * `id`: The ID of the document where the rendering is called
1134:     * `path`: Template file absolute path
1135: * Return value
1136: 
1137:   ```json
1138:   {
1139:     "code": 0,
1140:     "msg": "",
1141:     "data": {
1142:       "content": "<div data-node-id=\"20220729234848-dlgsah7\" data-node-index=\"1\" data-type=\"NodeParagraph\" class=\"p\" updated=\"20220729234840\"><div contenteditable=\"true\" spellcheck=\"false\">foo</div><div class=\"protyle-attr\" contenteditable=\"false\">​</div></div>",
1143:       "path": "F:\\SiYuan\\data\\templates\\foo.md"
1144:     }
1145:   }

1156:   }

1169: ## File
1170: 
1171: ### Get file
1172: 
1173: * `/api/file/getFile`
1174: * Parameters
1175: 
1176:   ``json {
1177:   "path": "/data/20210808180117-6v0mkxr/20200923234011-ieuun1p.sy"
1178:   }
1179:   ``
1180:     * `path`: the file path under the workspace path
1181: * Return value
1182: 
1183:     * Response status code `200`: File content
1184:     * Response status code `202`: Exception information
1185: 
1186:       ```json
1187:       {
1188:         "code": 404,
1189:         "msg": "",
1190:         "data": null
1191:       }
1192:       ```
1193: 
1194:         * `code`: non-zero for exceptions
1195: 
1196:             * `-1`: Parameter parsing error
1197:             * `403`: Permission denied (file is not in the workspace)
1198:             * `404`: Not Found (file doesn't exist)
1199:             * `405`: Method Not Allowed (it's a directory)
1200:             * `500`: Server Error (stat file failed / read file failed)
1201:         * `msg`: a piece of text describing the error
1202: 
1203: ### Put file
1204: 
1205: * `/api/file/putFile`
1206: * The parameter is an HTTP Multipart form
1207: 
1208:     * `path`: the file path under the workspace path
1209:     * `isDir`: whether to create a folder, when `true` only create a folder, ignore `file`
1210:     * `modTime`: last access and modification time, Unix time
1211:     * `file`: the uploaded file
1212: * Return value
1213: 
1214:    ```json
1215:    {
1216:      "code": 0,
1217:      "msg": "",
1218:      "data": null
1219:    }
1220:    ```
1221:

1300: ## Export
1301: 
1302: ### Export Markdown
1303: 
1304: * `/api/export/exportMdContent`
1305: * Parameters
1306: 
1307:   ```json
1308:   {
1309:     "id": ""
1310:   }
1311:   ```
1312: 
1313:     * `id`: ID of the doc block to export
1314: * Return value
1315: 
1316:   ```json
1317:   {
1318:     "code": 0,
1319:     "msg": "",
1320:     "data": {
1321:       "hPath": "/Please Start Here",
1322:       "content": "## 🍫 Content Block\n\nIn SiYuan, the only important core concept is..."
1323:     }
1324:   }
1325:   ```
1326: 
1327:     * `hPath`: human-readable path
1328:     * `content`: Markdown content
1329: 
1330: ### Export files and folders
1331: 
1332: * `/api/export/exportResources`
1333: * Parameters
1334: 
1335:   ```json
1336:   {
1337:     "paths": [
1338:       "/conf/appearance/boot",
1339:       "/conf/appearance/langs",
1340:       "/conf/appearance/emojis/conf.json",
1341:       "/conf/appearance/icons/index.html"
1342:     ],
1343:     "name": "zip-file-name"
1344:   }
1345:   ```
1346: 
1347:     * `paths`: A list of file or folder paths to be exported, the same filename/folder name will be overwritten
1348:     * `name`: (Optional) The exported file name, which defaults to `export-YYYY-MM-DD_hh-mm-ss.zip` when not set
1349: * Return value
1350: 
1351:   ```json
1352:   {
1353:     "code": 0,
1354:     "msg": "",
1355:     "data": {
1356:       "path": "temp/export/zip-file-name.zip"
1357:     }
1358:   }
1359:   ```
1360: 
1361:     * `path`: The path of `*.zip` file created
1362:         * The directory structure in `zip-file-name.zip` is as follows:
1363:             * `zip-file-name`
1364:                 * `boot`
1365:                 * `langs`
1366:                 * `conf.json`
1367:                 * `index.html`
1368: 
1369: ## Conversion
1370: 
1371: ### Pandoc
1372: 
1373: * `/api/convert/pandoc`
1374: * Working directory
1375:     * Executing the pandoc command will set the working directory to `workspace/temp/convert/pandoc/${dir}`
1376:     * API [`Put file`](#put-file) can be used to write the file to be converted to this directory first
1377:     * Then call the API for conversion, and the converted file will also be written to this directory
1378:     * Finally, call the API [`Get file`](#get-file) to get the converted file
1379:         * Or call the API [Create a document with Markdown](#Create-a-document-with-Markdown)
1380:         * Or call the internal API `importStdMd` to import the converted folder directly
1381: * Parameters
1382: 
1383:   ```json
1384:   {
1385:     "dir": "test",
1386:     "args": [
1387:       "--to", "markdown_strict-raw_html",
1388:       "foo.epub",
1389:       "-o", "foo.md"
1390:    ]
1391:   }
1392:   ```
1393: 
1394:     * `args`: Pandoc command line parameters
1395: * Return value
1396: 
1397:   ```json
1398:   {
1399:     "code": 0,
1400:     "msg": "",
1401:     "data": {
1402:        "path": "/temp/convert/pandoc/test"
1403:     }
1404:   }
1405:   ```
1406:     * `path`: the path under the workspace
1407:

1462: ## Network
1463: 
1464: ### Forward proxy
1465: 
1466: * `/api/network/forwardProxy`
1467: * Parameters
1468: 
1469:   ```json
1470:   {
1471:     "url": "https://b3log.org/siyuan/",
1472:     "method": "GET",
1473:     "timeout": 7000,
1474:     "contentType": "text/html",
1475:     "headers": [
1476:         {
1477:             "Cookie": ""
1478:         }
1479:     ],
1480:     "payload": {},
1481:     "payloadEncoding": "text",
1482:     "responseEncoding": "text"
1483:   }
1484:   ```
1485: 
1486:     * `url`: URL to forward
1487:     * `method`: HTTP method, default is `POST`
1488:     * `timeout`: timeout in milliseconds, default is `7000`
1489:     * `contentType`: Content-Type, default is `application/json`
1490:     * `headers`: HTTP headers
1491:     * `payload`: HTTP payload, object or string
1492:     * `payloadEncoding`: The encoding scheme used by `pyaload`, default is `text`, optional values are as follows
1493: 
1494:         * `text`
1495:         * `base64` | `base64-std`
1496:         * `base64-url`
1497:         * `base32` | `base32-std`
1498:         * `base32-hex`
1499:         * `hex`
1500:     * `responseEncoding`: The encoding scheme used by `body` in response data, default is `text`, optional values are as
1501:       follows
1502: 
1503:         * `text`
1504:         * `base64` | `base64-std`
1505:         * `base64-url`
1506:         * `base32` | `base32-std`
1507:         * `base32-hex`
1508:         * `hex`
1509: * Return value
1510: 
1511:   ```json
1512:   {
1513:     "code": 0,
1514:     "msg": "",
1515:     "data": {
1516:       "body": "",
1517:       "bodyEncoding": "text",
1518:       "contentType": "text/html",
1519:       "elapsed": 1976,
1520:       "headers": {
1521:       },
1522:       "status": 200,
1523:       "url": "https://b3log.org/siyuan"
1524:     }
1525:   }
1526:   ```
1527: 
1528:     * `bodyEncoding`: The encoding scheme used by `body`, is consistent with field `responseEncoding` in request,
1529:       default is `text`, optional values are as follows
1530: 
1531:         * `text`
1532:         * `base64` | `base64-std`
1533:         * `base64-url`
1534:         * `base32` | `base32-std`
1535:         * `base32-hex`
1536:         * `hex`
1537:

237:                     // window.showInformationMessage('检测到单张在线图片！');
238:                     const actualImage = (images && images.length > 0) ? images[0] : path;
239:                     PickList.itemList.updateBackgound(actualImage, true);
240:                 }
241:             } catch (error: any) {
242:                 window.showErrorMessage(`在线资源检测失败: ${error.message}`);
243:                 const config = workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
244:                 PickList.itemList = new PickList(config);
245:                 PickList.itemList.setImageFileType(2);
246:                 PickList.itemList.updateBackgound(path, true);
247:             }
248:         });
249:     }
250: 
251:     public static gotoFilePath(path?: string) {
252:         if (path == undefined) {
253:             return window.showWarningMessage('无效菜单');
254:         }
255:         const extPath = extensions.getExtension("manasxx.background-cover")?.extensionPath;
256:         const tmpPath = "file:///" + extPath + path;
257:         const tmpurl = Uri.parse(tmpPath);
258:         commands.executeCommand('vscode.openFolder', tmpurl);
259:     }
