```
263:     public constructor(config: WorkspaceConfiguration, pickList?: QuickPick<ImgItem>) {
264:         this.config = config;
265:         this.imgPath = config.imagePath;
266:         this.opacity = config.opacity;
267:         this.sizeModel = config.sizeModel || 'cover';
268:         this.imageFileType = 0;
269:         this.blur = config.blur;
270: 
271:         if (pickList) {
272:             this.quickPick = pickList;
273:             this.quickPick.onDidAccept((e: any) => {
274:                 if (this.quickPick.selectedItems.length > 0) {
275:                     this.handleAction(
276:                         this.quickPick.selectedItems[0].imageType,
277:                         this.quickPick.selectedItems[0].path
278:                     );
279:                 }
280:             });
281:             this.quickPick.onDidHide(() => {
282:                 this.dispose();
283:             }, null, this._disposables);
284:             this.quickPick.show();
285:         }
286:     }

349: 
350:     public handleAction(type: ActionType, path?: string) {
351:         switch (type) {
352:             case ActionType.SelectPictures: this.showImageSelectionList(); break;
353:             case ActionType.AddDirectory: this.openFieldDialog(2); break;
354:             case ActionType.ManualSelection: this.openFieldDialog(1); break;
355:             case ActionType.UpdateBackground: this.updateBackgound(path); break;
356:             case ActionType.BackgroundOpacity: this.showInputBox(InputType.Opacity); break;
357:             case ActionType.InputPath: this.showInputBox(InputType.Path); break;
358:             case ActionType.CloseBackground: this.updateDom(true); break;
359:             case ActionType.ReloadWindow: commands.executeCommand('workbench.action.reloadWindow'); break;
360:             case ActionType.CloseMenu: this.quickPick.hide(); break;
361:             case ActionType.MoreMenu: this.showMoreMenu(); break;
362:             case ActionType.OpenExternalUrl: this.gotoPath(path); break;
363:             case ActionType.OpenFilePath: PickList.gotoFilePath(path); break;
364:             case ActionType.SizeModeMenu: this.showSizeModeMenu(); break;
365:             case ActionType.SetSizeMode: this.setSizeModel(path); break;
366:             case ActionType.OnlineImages: commands.executeCommand('workbench.view.extension.backgroundCover-explorer'); break;
367:             case ActionType.BackgroundBlur: this.showInputBox(InputType.Blur); break;
368:             case ActionType.RefreshOnlineFolder: this.refreshOnlineFolder(); break;
369:             case ActionType.AutoRandomSettings: this.showInputBox(InputType.AutoRandomSettings); break;
370:             case ActionType.OpenCacheFolder: this.openCacheFolder(); break;
371:             
372:             // Particle Effects
373:             case ActionType.ParticleSettings: this.particleEffectSettings(); break;
374:             case ActionType.ToggleParticle: this.toggleParticleEffect(); break;
375:             case ActionType.ParticleOpacity: this.showInputBox(InputType.ParticleOpacity); break;
376:             case ActionType.ParticleColor: this.showColorSelection(); break;
377:             case ActionType.ParticleCount: this.showInputBox(InputType.ParticleCount); break;
378:             case ActionType.SetParticleColor: if (path) { this.setContextValue('backgroundCoverParticleColor', Color(path), true); } break;
379:             case ActionType.InputParticleColor: this.showInputBox(InputType.ParticleColor); break;
380:             
381:             // Pet Assistant
382:             case ActionType.SelectPet: this.showPetSelection(); break;
383:             case ActionType.TogglePet: this.togglePet(); break;
384: 
385:             default: break;
386:         }
387:     }
388:

528:     private dispose() {
529:         PickList.itemList = undefined;
530:         this.quickPick.hide();
531:         while (this._disposables.length) {
532:             const x = this._disposables.pop();
533:             if (x) { x.dispose(); }
534:         }
535:     }
536: 
537:     private async autoUpdateBackground(persist: boolean = true): Promise<boolean> {
538:         const context = getContext();
539:         const onlineFolder = context.globalState.get<string>('backgroundCoverOnlineFolder');
540:         const cachedImages = context.globalState.get<string[]>('backgroundCoverOnlineImageList');
541:         
542:         if (onlineFolder && this.isOnlineUrl(onlineFolder)) {
543:             try {
544:                 let images = cachedImages as string[] | undefined;
545:                 if (!images || images.length === 0) {
546:                     if (persist) {
547:                         window.showInformationMessage('正在从在线文件夹获取图片列表...');
548:                     }
549:                     images = await OnlineImageHelper.getOnlineImages(onlineFolder);
550:                     context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverOnlineImageList', images);
551:                 }
552:                 if (images && images.length > 0) {
553:                     const randomImage = images[Math.floor(Math.random() * images.length)];
554:                     if (persist) {
555:                         this.handleAction(ActionType.UpdateBackground, randomImage);
556:                     } else {
557:                         this.updateBackgound(randomImage, false, false);
558:                     }
559:                     return true;
560:                 }
561:             } catch (error: any) {
562:                 console.error('从在线文件夹获取图片失败:', error);
563:                 if (persist) {
564:                     window.showWarningMessage('在线文件夹访问失败，请检查网络连接！');
565:                 }
566:                 this.clearOnlineFolder(true);
567:             }
568:         }
569: 
570:         const singleSource = context.globalState.get<string>('backgroundCoverSingleImageSource');
571:         if (singleSource && this.isOnlineUrl(singleSource)) {
572:             if (persist) {
573:                 this.handleAction(ActionType.UpdateBackground, singleSource);
574:             } else {
575:                 this.updateBackgound(singleSource, false, false);
576:             }
577:             return true;
578:         }
579: 
580:         const randomImageFolder = this.config.get<string>('randomImageFolder');
581:         if (randomImageFolder && this.checkFolder(randomImageFolder)) {
582:             const files = this.getFolderImgList(randomImageFolder);
583:             if (files.length > 0) {
584:                 const randomFile = files[Math.floor(Math.random() * files.length)];
585:                 const file = path.join(randomImageFolder, randomFile);
586:                 if (persist) {
587:                     this.handleAction(ActionType.UpdateBackground, file);
588:                 } else {
589:                     this.updateBackgound(file, false, false);
590:                 }
591:             }
592:         }
593:         return true;
594:     }
595: 
596:     private openCacheFolder() {
597:         const context = getContext();
598:         const cacheDir = path.join(context.globalStorageUri.fsPath, 'images');
599:         // 确保目录存在
600:         if (!fs.existsSync(cacheDir)) {
601:             fs.mkdirSync(cacheDir, { recursive: true });
602:         }
603:         env.openExternal(Uri.file(cacheDir));
604:     }
605: 
606:     private async refreshOnlineFolder() {
607:         const context = getContext();
608:         const onlineFolder = context.globalState.get<string>('backgroundCoverOnlineFolder');
609:         if (!onlineFolder) {
610:             window.showWarningMessage('未找到在线文件夹配置！');
611:             return;
612:         }
613:         let success = false;
614:         try {
615:             window.showInformationMessage('正在刷新在线文件夹图片列表...');
616:             const images = await OnlineImageHelper.getOnlineImages(onlineFolder);
617:             if (images && images.length > 0) {
618:                 const normalizedFolder = this.normalizePathKey(onlineFolder);
619:                 if (images.length === 1 && this.normalizePathKey(images[0]) === normalizedFolder) {
620:                     window.showInformationMessage('检测到链接仅返回单张图片，已切换为单图模式。');
621:                     this.updateBackgound(images[0], true);
622:                     success = true;
623:                 } else {
624:                     context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverOnlineImageList', images);
625:                     window.showInformationMessage(`刷新成功！发现 ${images.length} 张图片。`);
626:                     const randomImage = images[Math.floor(Math.random() * images.length)];
627:                     this.updateBackgound(randomImage);
628:                     success = true;
629:                 }
630:             } else {
631:                 window.showWarningMessage('未在该URL找到图片！');
632:                 this.clearOnlineFolder(true);
633:             }
634:         } catch (error: any) {
635:             window.showErrorMessage(`刷新失败: ${error.message}`);
636:             this.clearOnlineFolder(true);
637:         }
638:         if (success) { this.quickPick.hide(); }
639:     }
640: 
641:     private clearOnlineFolder(resetRandomFolder: boolean = false) {
642:         const context = getContext();
643:         const previousOnlineFolder = context.globalState.get<string>('backgroundCoverOnlineFolder');
644:         context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverOnlineFolder', undefined);
645:         context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverOnlineImageList', undefined);
646:         if (resetRandomFolder && previousOnlineFolder) {
647:             const currentRandomFolder = this.config.get<string>('randomImageFolder');
648:             if (this.normalizePathKey(currentRandomFolder) === this.normalizePathKey(previousOnlineFolder)) {
649:                 this.config.update('randomImageFolder', '', ConfigurationTarget.Global);
650:             }
651:         }
652:     }
653: 
654:     private normalizePathKey(value?: string | null): string {
655:         if (!value) { return ''; }
656:         const trimmed = value.trim();
657:         if (/^https?:/i.test(trimmed)) {
658:             try {
659:                 const parsed = new URL(trimmed);
660:                 const normalizedPath = parsed.pathname.replace(/\/+$/, '') || '/';
661:                 const search = parsed.search ?? '';
662:                 return `${parsed.protocol}//${parsed.host}${normalizedPath}${search}`;
663:             } catch {
664:                 return trimmed.replace(/\/+$/, '');
665:             }
666:         }
667:         return path.normalize(trimmed).replace(/\\+/g, '/');
668:     }
669: 
670:     private isOnlineUrl(url?: string): boolean {
671:         if (!url) { return false; }
672:         const lower = url.toLowerCase();
673:         return lower.startsWith('http://') || lower.startsWith('https://');
674:     }
675: 
676:     private showImageSelectionList(folderPath?: string) {
677:         let items: ImgItem[] = [{
678:             label: '$(diff-added) Manual selection',
679:             detail: '选择一张背景图',
680:             imageType: ActionType.ManualSelection
681:         }];
682: 
683:         const randomPath: any = folderPath ? folderPath : this.config.get<string>('randomImageFolder');
684:         if (this.checkFolder(randomPath)) {
685:             const files = this.getFolderImgList(randomPath);
686:             if (files.length > 0) {
687:                 const randomFile = files[Math.floor(Math.random() * files.length)];
688:                 items.push({
689:                     label: '$(light-bulb) Random pictures',
690:                     detail: '随机自动选择       ctrl+shift+F7',
691:                     imageType: ActionType.UpdateBackground,
692:                     path: path.join(randomPath, randomFile)
693:                 });
694:                 items.push({ label: '', description: '', imageType: 0, kind: QuickPickItemKind.Separator });
695:                 items = items.concat(files.map(
696:                     (e) => new ImgItem('$(tag) ' + e, e, ActionType.UpdateBackground, path.join(randomPath, e))
697:                 ));
698:             }
699:         }
700:         this.quickPick.items = items;
701:         this.quickPick.show();
702:     }
703: 
704:     private getFolderImgList(pathUrl: string): string[] {
705:         if (!pathUrl || pathUrl === '') { return []; }
706:         return fs.readdirSync(path.resolve(pathUrl)).filter((s) => {
707:             // 增加视频文件 '.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov'
708:             return s.endsWith('.png') || s.endsWith('.PNG') || s.endsWith('.jpg') || s.endsWith('.JPG')
709:                 || s.endsWith('.jpeg') || s.endsWith('.gif') || s.endsWith('.webp') || s.endsWith('.bmp')
710:                 || s.endsWith('.jfif') || s.endsWith('.mp4') || s.endsWith('.webm') || s.endsWith('.ogg') || s.endsWith('.mov');
711:         });
712:     }
713: 
714:     private checkFolder(folderPath: string) {
715:         if (!folderPath) { return false; }
716:         const fsStatus = fs.existsSync(path.resolve(folderPath));
717:         if (!fsStatus) { return false; }
718:         const stat = fs.statSync(folderPath);
719:         return stat.isDirectory();
720:     }
721: 
722:     private async showInputBox(type: InputType) {
723:         const context = getContext();
724:         let placeString = '';
725:         let promptString = '';
726: 
727:         switch (type) {
728:             case InputType.Path:
729:                 placeString = 'Please enter the image path to support local and HTTPS';
730:                 promptString = '输入图片路径：支持本地/https/json(api接口)/html(解析a标签)/在线图库（帖子地址）';
731:                 break;
732:             case InputType.Opacity:
733:                 placeString = 'Opacity ranges：0.00 - 1,current:(' + this.opacity + ')';
734:                 promptString = '设置图片不透明度：0 - 0.8,当前值：' + this.opacity;
735:                 break;
736:             case InputType.Blur:
737:                 placeString = 'Set image blur: 0-100,current:(' + this.blur + ')';
738:                 promptString = '设置图片模糊度：0 - 100,当前值：' + this.blur;
739:                 break;
740:             case InputType.AutoRandomSettings:
741:                 placeString = 'Auto update current:(' + this.config.get('autoInterval', 0) + ')';
742:                 promptString = '设置自动更换间隔(秒)，0表示关闭自动定时更换 / Set interval (0 to disable)';
743:                 break;
744:             case InputType.ParticleOpacity:
745:                 placeString = 'Particle opacity (0.1 - 1),current:(' + context.globalState.get("backgroundCoverParticleOpacity") + ')';
746:                 promptString = '粒子透明度 (0.1 - 1),当前值：' + context.globalState.get("backgroundCoverParticleOpacity");
747:                 break;
748:             case InputType.ParticleColor:
749:                 placeString = 'Particle color (e.g.:255,255,255),current:(' + context.globalState.get("backgroundCoverParticleColor") + ')';
750:                 promptString = '粒子颜色 (例如:255,255,255),当前值：' + context.globalState.get("backgroundCoverParticleColor");
751:                 break;
752:             case InputType.ParticleCount:
753:                 placeString = 'Particle count (1 - 200),current:(' + context.globalState.get("backgroundCoverParticleCount") + ')';
754:                 promptString = '粒子数量 (1 - 200),当前值：' + context.globalState.get("backgroundCoverParticleCount");
755:                 break;
756:         }
757: 
758:         const option: InputBoxOptions = {
759:             ignoreFocusOut: true,
760:             password: false,
761:             placeHolder: placeString,
762:             prompt: promptString
763:         };
764: 
765:         let value = await window.showInputBox(option);
766:         if (!value) {
767:             window.showWarningMessage('Please enter configuration parameters / 请输入配置参数！');
768:             return false;
769:         }
770: 
771:         let shouldClearOnlineCache = false;
772: 
773:         if (type === InputType.Path) {
774:             const fsStatus = fs.existsSync(path.resolve(value));
775:             const isUrl = (value.slice(0, 8).toLowerCase() === 'https://') || (value.slice(0, 7).toLowerCase() === 'http://');
776:             if (!fsStatus && !isUrl) {
777:                 window.showWarningMessage('No access to the file or the file does not exist! / 无权限访问文件或文件不存在！');
778:                 return false;
779:             }
780:             if (!isUrl) { shouldClearOnlineCache = true; }
781: 
782:             if (isUrl) {
783:                 let shouldReturn = false;
784:                 await window.withProgress({
785:                     location: ProgressLocation.Notification,
786:                     title: "正在检测在线资源类型... / Detecting online resource type...",
787:                     cancellable: false
788:                 }, async () => {
789:                     try {
790:                         const images = await OnlineImageHelper.getOnlineImages(value!);
791:                         if (images && images.length > 1) {
792:                             const config = workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
793:                             PickList.itemList = new PickList(config);
794:                             PickList.itemList.setImageFileType(2);
795:                             const context = getContext();
796:                             await context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverOnlineFolder', value);
797:                             await context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverOnlineImageList', images);
798:                             await config.update('randomImageFolder', value, ConfigurationTarget.Global);
799:                             const randomImage = images[Math.floor(Math.random() * images.length)];
800:                             PickList.itemList.updateBackgound(randomImage);
801:                             shouldReturn = true;
802:                         } else if (images && images.length === 1) {
803:                             value = images[0];
804:                             shouldClearOnlineCache = true;
805:                         }
806:                     } catch (err: any) {
807:                         console.error('[background-cover] OnlineImageHelper error:', err && err.message ? err.message : err);
808:                         window.showWarningMessage('在线资源检测失败，按单张图片处理 / Online detection failed, treating as single image');
809:                         shouldClearOnlineCache = true;
810:                     }
811:                 });
812:                 if (shouldReturn) { return true; }
813:             } else {
814:                 shouldClearOnlineCache = true;
815:             }
816:         } else if (type === InputType.Opacity) {
817:             const isOpacity = parseFloat(value);
818:             if (isOpacity < 0 || isOpacity > 0.8 || isNaN(isOpacity)) {
819:                 window.showWarningMessage('Opacity ranges in：0 - 0.8！');
820:                 return false;
821:             }
822:         } else if (type === InputType.Blur) {
823:             const blur = parseFloat(value);
824:             if (blur < 0 || blur > 100 || isNaN(blur)) {
825:                 window.showWarningMessage('Blur ranges in：0 - 100！');
826:                 return false;
827:             }
828:         } else if (type === InputType.AutoRandomSettings) {
829:             const interval = parseInt(value);
830:             if (interval < 0 || isNaN(interval)) {
831:                 window.showWarningMessage('Interval must be >= 0!');
832:                 return false;
833:             }
834:         } else if (type === InputType.ParticleOpacity) {
835:             const particleOpacity = parseFloat(value);
836:             if (particleOpacity < 0 || particleOpacity > 1 || isNaN(particleOpacity)) {
837:                 window.showWarningMessage('粒子透明度范围：0 - 1！');
838:                 return false;
839:             }
840:         } else if (type === InputType.ParticleColor) {
841:             if (!value.includes(',')) {
842:                 window.showWarningMessage('颜色格式无效，请使用RGB(255,255,255)格式！');
843:                 return false;
844:             }
845:         } else if (type === InputType.ParticleCount) {
846:             const particleCount = parseInt(value);
847:             if (particleCount < 1 || particleCount > 200 || isNaN(particleCount)) {
848:                 window.showWarningMessage('粒子数量范围：1 - 200！');
849:                 return false;
850:             }
851:         }
852: 
853:         if (type === InputType.Path && shouldClearOnlineCache) {
854:             this.clearOnlineFolder(true);
855:         }
856: 
857:         if (type === InputType.Path) {
858:             return this.updateBackgound(value, shouldClearOnlineCache);
859:         } else if (type === InputType.ParticleCount) {
860:             this.setContextValue('backgroundCoverParticleCount', parseInt(value), true);
861:         } else if (type === InputType.ParticleColor) {
862:             this.setContextValue('backgroundCoverParticleColor', value, true);
863:         } else if (type === InputType.ParticleOpacity) {
864:             this.setContextValue('backgroundCoverParticleOpacity', parseFloat(value), true);
865:         } else if (type === InputType.Opacity) {
866:             await this.setConfigValue('opacity', parseFloat(value), true);
867:         } else if (type === InputType.Blur) {
868:             await this.setConfigValue('blur', parseFloat(value), true);
869:         } else if (type === InputType.AutoRandomSettings) {
870:             const interval = parseInt(value);
871:             if (interval > 0) {
872:                 const context = getContext();
873:                 const hasRandomFolder = this.config.get('randomImageFolder');
874:                 const hasOnlineFolder = context.globalState.get('backgroundCoverOnlineFolder');
875:                 const hasSingleSource = context.globalState.get('backgroundCoverSingleImageSource');
876:                 if (!hasRandomFolder && !hasOnlineFolder && !hasSingleSource) {
877:                     window.showWarningMessage('Please add a directory first! / 请先添加目录！');
878:                     return false;
879:                 }
880:                 await this.setConfigValue('autoInterval', interval, false);
881:                 await this.setConfigValue('autoStatus', true, false);
882:                 await this.autoUpdateBackground();
883:             } else {
884:                 await this.setConfigValue('autoStatus', false, false);
885:                 await this.setConfigValue('autoInterval', 0, false);
886:             }
887:         }
888:     }
889: 
890:     private async setSizeModel(value?: string) {
891:         if (!value) { return vsHelp.showInfo('No parameter value was obtained / 未获取到参数值'); }
892:         await this.setConfigValue('sizeModel', value, true);
893:     }
894: 
895:     public setImageFileType(value: number) {
896:         this.imageFileType = value;
897:     }
898: 
899:     public async updateBackgound(path?: string, clearOnlineCache: boolean = false, persist: boolean = true) {
900:         if (!path) { path = this.config.get<string>('imagePath'); }
901:         if (!path) { return vsHelp.showInfo('Unfetched Picture Path / 未获取到图片路径'); }
902:         if (clearOnlineCache || !this.isOnlineUrl(path)) {
903:             this.clearOnlineFolder(true);
904:         }
905:         const shouldDisableAuto = persist && clearOnlineCache && this.isSingleImagePath(path);
906:         await this.setConfigValue('imagePath', path, true, persist);
907:         if (shouldDisableAuto) {
908:             await this.disableAutoRandomForSingleImage();
909:         }
910:     }
911: 
912:     private async openFieldDialog(type: number) {
913:         const isFolders = type === 1 ? false : true;
914:         const isFiles = type === 2 ? false : true;
915:         const filters = type === 1 ? { 'Images': ['png', 'jpg', 'gif', 'jpeg', 'jfif', 'webp', 'bmp', 'mp4', 'webm', 'ogg', 'mov'] } : undefined;
916:         const folderUris = await window.showOpenDialog({
917:             canSelectFolders: isFolders,
918:             canSelectFiles: isFiles,
919:             canSelectMany: false,
920:             openLabel: 'Select folder',
921:             filters: filters
922:         });
923:         if (!folderUris) { return false; }
924:         const fileUri = folderUris[0];
925:         if (type === 2) {
926:             this.clearOnlineFolder(true);
927:             this.setConfigValue('randomImageFolder', fileUri.fsPath, false);
928:             return this.showImageSelectionList(fileUri.fsPath);
929:         }
930:         if (type === 1) {
931:             this.clearOnlineFolder(true);
932:             return this.updateBackgound(fileUri.fsPath, true);
933:         }
934:         return false;
935:     }
936: 
937:     private async setConfigValue(name: string, value: any, updateDom: Boolean = true, persist: boolean = true) {
938:         if (persist) {
939:             await this.config.update(name, value, ConfigurationTarget.Global);
940:             this.config = workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
941:         }
942:         if (name === 'imagePath') {
943:             const context = getContext();
944:             const hasOnlineFolder = context.globalState.get('backgroundCoverOnlineFolder');
945:             if (typeof value === 'string' && value && this.isOnlineUrl(value) && !hasOnlineFolder) {
946:                 context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverSingleImageSource', value);
947:             } else {
948:                 context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverSingleImageSource', undefined);
949:             }
950:         }
951:         switch (name) {
952:             case 'opacity': this.opacity = value; break;
953:             case 'imagePath': this.imgPath = value; break;
954:             case 'sizeModel': this.sizeModel = value; break;
955:             case 'blur': this.blur = value; break;
956:             default: break;
957:         }
958:         if (updateDom) { await this.updateDom(); }
959:         return true;
960:     }
961: 
962:     private setContextValue(name: string, value: any, updateDom: Boolean = true) {
963:         getContext().globalState.update(name, value);
964:         onDidChangeGlobalState.fire();
965:         if (updateDom) { this.updateDom(); }
966:         return true;
967:     }
968: 
969:     private async disableAutoRandomForSingleImage(): Promise<void> {
970:         const autoStatus = this.config.get<boolean>('autoStatus');
971:         if (!autoStatus) {
972:             return;
973:         }
974:         await this.config.update('autoStatus', false, ConfigurationTarget.Global);
975:         this.config = workspace.getConfiguration('backgroundCover');
976:         window.showInformationMessage('检测到单张图片，已自动关闭自动更新功能。 / Detected single image source, auto update disabled.');
977:     }
978: 
979:     private isSingleImagePath(value: string): boolean {
980:         if (!value) {
981:             return false;
982:         }
983:         const sanitized = value.split('?')[0].split('#')[0];
984:         const ext = path.extname(sanitized).toLowerCase();
985:         if (!ext) {
986:             return false;
987:         }
988:         const singleExts = ['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.bmp', '.webp', '.jfif', '.svg', '.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov'];
989:         return singleExts.includes(ext);
990:     }
991: 
992:     public setRandUpdate(value: boolean) {
993:         this.randUpdate = value;
994:     }
995: 
996:     private async updateDom(uninstall: boolean = false, colorThemeKind: string = ""): Promise<boolean> {
997:         if (colorThemeKind == "") {
998:             colorThemeKind = BlendHelper.autoBlendModel();
999:         }
1000: 
1001:         const context = getContext();
1002:         context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverBlendModel', colorThemeKind);
1003: 
1004:         const dom = new FileDom(this.config, this.imgPath, this.opacity, this.sizeModel, this.blur, colorThemeKind);
1005:         let result = false;
1006: 
1007:         try {
1008:             if (uninstall) {
1009:                 this.config.update("imagePath", "", ConfigurationTarget.Global);
1010:                 result = await dom.clearBackground();
1011:             } else {
1012:                 result = await dom.install();
1013:             }
1014: 
1015:             if (result) {
1016:                 if (!dom.requiresReload) {
1017:                     if (this.quickPick) {
1018:                         this.quickPick.hide();
1019:                     }
1020:                     const triggerMsg = window.setStatusBarMessage('background-cover-reload-trigger');
1021:                     
1022:                     setTimeout(() => {
1023:                         triggerMsg.dispose();
1024:                         window.setStatusBarMessage('Background updated successfully! / 背景更新成功！', 5000);
1025:                     }, 1000);
1026:                     
1027:                     return false;
1028:                 }
1029: 
1030:                 if (this.quickPick) {
1031:                     this.quickPick.placeholder = 'Reloading takes effect? / 重新加载生效？';
1032:                     this.quickPick.items = [
1033:                         { label: '$(check) YES', detail: '立即重新加载窗口生效', imageType: ActionType.ReloadWindow },
1034:                         { label: '$(x) NO', detail: '稍后手动重启', imageType: ActionType.CloseMenu }
1035:                     ];
1036:                     this.quickPick.ignoreFocusOut = true;
1037:                     this.quickPick.show();
1038:                 } else {
1039:                     if (this.imageFileType === 2) {
1040:                         const value = await window.showInformationMessage(
1041:                             `"${this.imgPath}" | Reloading takes effect? / 重新加载生效？`,
1042:                             'YES', 'NO'
1043:                         );
1044:                         if (value === 'YES') {
1045:                             await commands.executeCommand('workbench.action.reloadWindow');
1046:                         }
1047:                     }
1048:                     if (this.randUpdate) {
1049:                         window.showInformationMessage(`背景将在1秒后自动更新！ / The background will be automatically updated in 1 second!`);
1050:                         await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
1051:                         await commands.executeCommand('workbench.action.reloadWindow');
1052:                     }
1053:                 }
1054:             }
1055:         } catch (error: any) {
1056:             await window.showErrorMessage(`更新失败: ${error.message}`);
1057:         }
1058:         return result && (dom.requiresReload || uninstall);
1059:     }
```

```
47:     const preferredHost = determineHostPreference();

51:     };

71:     const appHost = typeof env.appHost === 'string' ? env.appHost.toLowerCase() : undefined;
72:     if (appHost === 'desktop') {
73:         return 'desktop';
74:     }
75:     if (appHost === 'web') {
76:         return 'code-server';
77:     }

164:         
165:         this.initializePromise = this.initializeImage().catch((error: unknown) => {
166:             console.error('[FileDom] Failed to preprocess image:', error);
167:             throw error;
168:         });
169:     }
170: 
171:     // 检测是否为视频文件
172:     private checkIsVideo(filePath: string): boolean {
173:         const ext = path.extname(filePath).toLowerCase();
174:         return ['.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov'].includes(ext);
175:     }
176: 
177:     // 本地图片转换为vscode可访问路径
178:     private async initializeImage(): Promise<void> {
179:         let lowerPath = this.imagePath.toLowerCase();
180: 
181:         if (lowerPath.startsWith('http://') || lowerPath.startsWith('https://')) {
182:             await this.downloadAndCacheImage();
183:             lowerPath = this.imagePath.toLowerCase();
184:         }
185: 
186:         this.isVideo = this.checkIsVideo(this.imagePath);
187: 
188:         if (
189:             !lowerPath.startsWith('http://') &&
190:             !lowerPath.startsWith('https://') &&
191:             !lowerPath.startsWith('data:')
192:         ) {
193:             try {
194:                 if (IS_CODE_SERVER_TARGET) {
195:                     const assetUrl = await this.prepareCodeServerAsset(this.imagePath);
196:                     if (assetUrl) {
197:                         this.imagePath = assetUrl;
198:                     } else if (!this.isVideo) {
199:                         await this.imageToBase64();
200:                     } else {
201:                         this.localImgToVsc();
202:                     }
203:                 } else {
204:                     this.localImgToVsc();
205:                 }
206:             } catch (e) {
207:                 if (!this.isVideo) {
208:                     await this.imageToBase64();
209:                 } else {
210:                     this.localImgToVsc();
211:                 }
212:             }
213:         }
214:     }
215: 
216:     // 将在线图片下载并缓存到本地
217:     private async downloadAndCacheImage(): Promise<void> {
218:         try {
219:             const context = getContext();
220:             const cacheDir = path.join(context.globalStorageUri.fsPath, 'images');
221:             await fse.ensureDir(cacheDir);
222: 
223:             const urlHash = crypto.createHash('md5').update(this.imagePath).digest('hex');
224:             let ext = '.jpg';
225:             let isStaticImage = false;
226:             let uniqueDownload = false;
227: 
228:             try {
229:                 const urlObj = new URL(this.imagePath);
230:                 const detectedExt = path.extname(urlObj.pathname);
231:                 if (!detectedExt) {
232:                     uniqueDownload = true;
233:                 } else {
234:                     ext = detectedExt;
235:                     if (['.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.gif', '.bmp', '.webp', '.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov'].includes(ext.toLowerCase())) {
236:                         isStaticImage = true;
237:                     } else {
238:                         uniqueDownload = true;
239:                     }
240:                 }
241:             } catch {
242:                 uniqueDownload = true;
243:             }
244:             
245:             const cachePath = path.join(cacheDir, `${urlHash}${ext}`);
246: 
247:             if (isStaticImage && !uniqueDownload && await fse.pathExists(cachePath)) {
248:                 this.imagePath = cachePath;
249:                 return;
250:             }
251: 
252:             const timestamp = Date.now();
253:             const tempPath = path.join(cacheDir, `${urlHash}-${timestamp}${ext}.tmp`);
254: 
255:             try {
256:                 const { contentType } = await this.downloadFile(this.imagePath, tempPath);
257:                 let finalExt = ext;
258:                 if ((!ext || ext === '.img' || uniqueDownload) && contentType) {
259:                     finalExt = this.getExtensionFromContentType(contentType) || finalExt;
260:                 }
261: 
262:                 const targetPath = (!uniqueDownload && isStaticImage)
263:                     ? cachePath
264:                     : path.join(cacheDir, `${urlHash}-${timestamp}${finalExt || '.img'}`);
265: 
266:                 await fse.move(tempPath, targetPath, { overwrite: true });
267:                 this.imagePath = targetPath;
268:             } catch (error) {
269:                 if (await fse.pathExists(cachePath)) {
270:                     this.imagePath = cachePath;
271:                     console.warn('[FileDom] Download failed, using cached image:', error);
272:                 } else {
273:                     throw error;
274:                 }
275:             }
276:         } catch (error) {
277:             console.error('[FileDom] Failed to download image:', error);
278:             throw error;
279:         }
280:     }
281: 
282:     // 下载文件
283:     private downloadFile(url: string, dest: string, redirectCount = 0): Promise<{ contentType?: string }> {
284:         return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
285:             let urlObj: URL;
286:             try {
287:                 urlObj = new URL(url);
288:             } catch (error) {
289:                 reject(error);
290:                 return;
291:             }
292: 
293:             const headers = {
294:                 'User-Agent': DEFAULT_USER_AGENT,
295:                 'Accept': DEFAULT_ACCEPT_HEADER,
296:                 'Referer': `${urlObj.protocol}//${urlObj.host}/`,
297:             } as Record<string, string>;
298: 
299:             const protocolHandler = urlObj.protocol === 'https:' ? https : http;
300:             const request = protocolHandler.request(urlObj, { method: 'GET', headers }, (response) => {
301:                 const statusCode = response.statusCode ?? 0;
302: 
303:                 if ([301, 302, 303, 307, 308].includes(statusCode)) {
304:                     const location = response.headers.location;
305:                     if (!location) {
306:                         response.resume();
307:                         reject(new Error(`Failed to download: ${statusCode}`));
308:                         return;
309:                     }
310:                     if (redirectCount > 5) {
311:                         response.resume();
312:                         reject(new Error('Too many redirects'));
313:                         return;
314:                     }
315:                     const nextUrl = new URL(location, urlObj).toString();
316:                     response.resume();
317:                     this.downloadFile(nextUrl, dest, redirectCount + 1).then(resolve).catch(reject);
318:                     return;
319:                 }
320: 
321:                 if (statusCode !== 200) {
322:                     response.resume();
323:                     reject(new Error(`Failed to download: ${statusCode}`));
324:                     return;
325:                 }
326: 
327:                 const file = fs.createWriteStream(dest);
328:                 response.pipe(file);
329:                 file.on('finish', () => {
330:                     file.close();
331:                     resolve({ contentType: response.headers['content-type'] as string | undefined });
332:                 });
333:                 file.on('error', (err) => {
334:                     fs.unlink(dest, () => reject(err));
335:                 });
336:             });
337: 
338:             request.on('timeout', () => {
339:                 request.destroy(new Error('Request timeout'));
340:             });
341: 
342:             request.on('error', (err) => {
343:                 reject(err);
344:             });
345: 
346:             request.setTimeout(15000);
347:             request.end();
348:         });
349:     }
350: 
351:     //应用补丁安装
352:     public async install(): Promise<boolean> {
353:         if (!(await this.checkFileExists())) {
354:             return false;
355:         }
356: 
357:         await this.handleLegacyCleanup();
358:         await this.ensureBackup();
359: 
360:         return await this.applyPatch();
361:     }
362: 
363:     // 检查文件是否存在
364:     private async checkFileExists(): Promise<boolean> {
365:         const isExist = await fse.pathExists(this.filePath);
366:         if (!isExist) {
367:             await window.showErrorMessage(`文件不存在，提醒开发者修复吧！`);
368:             return false;
369:         }
370:         return true;
371:     }
372: 
373:     // 旧版本清理
374:     private async handleLegacyCleanup(): Promise<void> {
375:         const vsContext = getContext();
376:         const clearCssNum = Number(vsContext.globalState.get('ext_backgroundCover_clear_v2')) || 0;
377: 
378:         if (clearCssNum <= 5) {
379:             const cssContent = await this.getContent(CSS_FILE_PATH);
380:             if (this.getPatchContent(cssContent)) {
381:                 this.upCssContent = this.clearCssContent(cssContent);
382:             } else {
383:                 vsContext.globalState.update('ext_backgroundCover_clear_v2', clearCssNum + 1);
384:             }
385:         }
386:     }
387: 
388:     // 是否存在备份文件
389:     private async ensureBackup(): Promise<void> {
390:         const bakExist = await fse.pathExists(BAK_FILE_PATH);
391:         if (!bakExist) {
392:             this.bakStatus = true;
393:             window.setStatusBarMessage(`首次使用正在获取权限及备份文件，处理中... / First use is getting permission and backing up files, processing...`, 10000);
394:         }
395:     }
396: 
397:     // 应用补丁
398:     private async applyPatch(): Promise<boolean> {
399:         if (this.initializePromise) {
400:             await this.initializePromise;
401:             this.initializePromise = undefined;
402:         }
403: 
404:         const lockPath = path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'vscode-background.lock');
405:         let release: (() => Promise<void>) | undefined;
406: 
407:         try {
408:             if (!(await fse.pathExists(lockPath))) {
409:                 await fse.writeFile(lockPath, '', 'utf-8');
410:             }
411: 
412:             release = await lockfile.lock(lockPath, {
413:                 retries: {
414:                     retries: 10,
415:                     minTimeout: 100,
416:                     maxTimeout: 1000,
417:                     randomize: true
418:                 },
419:                 stale: 20000
420:             });
421: 
422:             // Save CSS first
423:             try {
424:                 await this.saveCssContent();
425:             } catch (e) {
426:                 window.showErrorMessage('Failed to write CSS file: ' + e);
427:                 return false;
428:             }
429: 
430:             const content = this.getJs().trim();
431:             if (!content) return false;
432: 
433:             const currentContent = await this.getContent(this.filePath);
434:             const patchHash = crypto.createHash('md5').update(content).digest('hex').slice(0, 8);
435:             
436:             // Check if we need to update JS
437:             const match = currentContent.match(new RegExp(`\\/\\*ext-${this.extName}-start\\*\\/([\\s\\S]*?)\\/\\*ext-${this.extName}-end\\*\\/`));
438:             if (match && match[0].trim() === content.trim()) {
439:                 const htmlChanged = await this.saveCodeServerHtmlContent(`${version}-${patchHash}`);
440:                 this.requiresReload = htmlChanged;
441:                 return true;
442:             }
443: 
444:             this.requiresReload = true;
445:             const bakContent = this.clearCssContent(currentContent);
446:             
447:             if (this.bakStatus) {
448:                 this.bakJsContent = bakContent;
449:             }
450: 
451:             const newContent = bakContent + content;
452:             const isSaved = await this.saveContent(newContent);
453:             await this.saveCodeServerHtmlContent(`${version}-${patchHash}`);
454:             return isSaved;
455: 
456:         } catch (error: any) {
457:             await window.showErrorMessage(`Installation failed: ${error.message}`);
458:             return false;
459:         } finally {
460:             if (release) {
461:                 try {
462:                     await release();
463:                 } catch (err) {
464:                     console.error(`Failed to unlock ${lockPath}:`, err);
465:                 }
466:             }
467:         }
468:     }
469: 
470:     // 获取文件权限
471:     public async getFilePermission(filePath: string): Promise<void> {
472:         try {
473:             if (!(await fse.pathExists(filePath))) {
474:                 if (this.systemType === SystemType.WINDOWS) {
475:                     await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`echo. > "${filePath}"`);
476:                 } else {
477:                     await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`touch "${filePath}"`);
478:                 }
479:             }
480:             switch (this.systemType) {
481:                 case SystemType.WINDOWS:
482:                     await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`takeown /f "${filePath}" /a`);
483:                     await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`icacls "${filePath}" /grant Users:F`);
484:                     break;
485:                 case SystemType.MACOS:
486:                     await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`chmod a+rwx "${filePath}"`);
487:                     break;
488:                 case SystemType.LINUX:
489:                     await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`chmod 666 "${filePath}"`);
490:                     break;
491:             }
492:         } catch (error) {
493:             console.error(`Failed to get permission for ${filePath}:`, error);
494:             throw error;
495:         }
496:     }
497: 
498:     // 清理补丁内容
499:     public async uninstall(): Promise<boolean> {
500:         try {
501:             const content = this.clearCssContent(await this.getContent(this.filePath));
502:             await this.saveContent(content);
503:             
504:             // Remove CSS file
505:             if (await fse.pathExists(CUSTOM_CSS_FILE_PATH)) {
506:                 try {
507:                     await fse.remove(CUSTOM_CSS_FILE_PATH);
508:                 } catch {
509:                     if (this.systemType === SystemType.WINDOWS) {
510:                         await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`del "${CUSTOM_CSS_FILE_PATH}"`);
511:                     } else {
512:                         await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`rm "${CUSTOM_CSS_FILE_PATH}"`);
513:                     }
514:                 }
515:             }
516: 
517:             await this.clearCodeServerHtmlContent();
518: 
519:             return true;
520:         } catch (error) {
521:             await window.showErrorMessage(`卸载失败: ${error}`);
522:             return false;
523:         }
524:     }
525: 
526:     // 清除背景
527:     public async clearBackground(): Promise<boolean> {
528:         try {
529:             await this.writeWithPermission(CUSTOM_CSS_FILE_PATH, '');
530:             this.requiresReload = false;
531:             return true;
532:         } catch (error) {
533:             await window.showErrorMessage(`清除背景失败: ${error}`);
534:             return false;
535:         }
536:     }
537: 
538:     // 读取原文件内容
539:     private async getContent(filePath: string): Promise<string> {
540:         return await fse.readFile(filePath, 'utf-8');
541:     }
542: 
543:     // 写入文件内容
544:     private async saveContent(content: string): Promise<boolean> {
545:         if (this.bakStatus) {
546:             await this.bakFile();
547:         }
548: 
549:         await this.writeWithPermission(this.filePath, content);
550: 
551:         if (this.upCssContent) {
552:             await this.writeWithPermission(CSS_FILE_PATH, this.upCssContent);
553:             this.upCssContent = '';
554:         }
555: 
556:         return true;
557:     }
558: 
559:     // 写入文件内容，带权限处理
560:     private async writeWithPermission(filePath: string, content: string): Promise<void> {
561:         try {
562:             await fse.writeFile(filePath, content, { encoding: 'utf-8' });
563:         } catch (err) {
564:             await this.getFilePermission(filePath);
565:             await fse.writeFile(filePath, content, { encoding: 'utf-8' });
566:         }
567:     }
568: 
569:     // 写入备份文件
570:     private async bakFile(): Promise<void> {
571:         try {
572:             await fse.writeFile(BAK_FILE_PATH, this.bakJsContent, { encoding: 'utf-8' });
573:         } catch (err) {
574:             await this.createAndWriteBakFile();
575:         }
576:     }
577: 
578:     // 创建并写入备份文件
579:     private async createAndWriteBakFile(): Promise<void> {
580:         if (this.systemType === SystemType.WINDOWS) {
581:             await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`echo. > "${BAK_FILE_PATH}"`);
582:             await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`icacls "${BAK_FILE_PATH}" /grant Users:F`);
583:         } else {
584:             await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`touch "${BAK_FILE_PATH}"`);
585:             const chmodCmd = this.systemType === SystemType.MACOS ? 'chmod a+rwx' : 'chmod 666';
586:             await SudoPromptHelper.exec(`${chmodCmd} "${BAK_FILE_PATH}"`);
587:         }
588:         await fse.writeFile(BAK_FILE_PATH, this.bakJsContent, { encoding: 'utf-8' });
589:     }
590: 
591:     public requiresReload: boolean = true;
592: 
593:     // 写入css内容
594:     private async saveCssContent(): Promise<void> {
595:         const css = this.getCss();
596:         await this.writeWithPermission(CUSTOM_CSS_FILE_PATH, css);
597:     }
598: 
599:     // code-server 静态资源会被浏览器长缓存，给 workbench.js URL 增加版本参数以确保首次注入后能加载新文件。
600:     private async saveCodeServerHtmlContent(cacheKey: string): Promise<boolean> {
601:         if (!IS_CODE_SERVER_TARGET || !HTML_FILE_PATH || !(await fse.pathExists(HTML_FILE_PATH))) {
602:             return false;
603:         }
604: 
605:         const content = await this.getContent(HTML_FILE_PATH);
606:         const patchedContent = this.patchCodeServerWorkbenchHtml(content, cacheKey);
607: 
608:         if (patchedContent === content) {
609:             return false;
610:         }
611: 
612:         await this.writeWithPermission(HTML_FILE_PATH, patchedContent);
613:         return true;
614:     }
615: 
616:     private async clearCodeServerHtmlContent(): Promise<void> {
617:         if (!IS_CODE_SERVER_TARGET || !HTML_FILE_PATH || !(await fse.pathExists(HTML_FILE_PATH))) {
618:             return;
619:         }
620: 
621:         const content = await this.getContent(HTML_FILE_PATH);
622:         const patchedContent = this.clearCodeServerWorkbenchHtmlPatch(content);
623: 
624:         if (patchedContent !== content) {
625:             await this.writeWithPermission(HTML_FILE_PATH, patchedContent);
626:         }
627:     }
628: 
629:     private patchCodeServerWorkbenchHtml(content: string, cacheKey: string): string {
630:         const workbenchScriptRegex = /(<script\b[^>]*\bsrc=["'])([^"']*\/out\/vs\/code\/browser\/workbench\/workbench\.js(?:\?[^"']*)?)(["'][^>]*>\s*<\/script>)/g;
631:         return content.replace(workbenchScriptRegex, (_match: string, prefix: string, scriptUrl: string, suffix: string) => {
632:             return `${prefix}${this.withHtmlCacheBust(scriptUrl, cacheKey)}${suffix}`;
633:         });
634:     }
635: 
636:     private clearCodeServerWorkbenchHtmlPatch(content: string): string {
637:         const workbenchScriptRegex = /(<script\b[^>]*\bsrc=["'])([^"']*\/out\/vs\/code\/browser\/workbench\/workbench\.js(?:\?[^"']*)?)(["'][^>]*>\s*<\/script>)/g;
638:         return content.replace(workbenchScriptRegex, (_match: string, prefix: string, scriptUrl: string, suffix: string) => {
639:             return `${prefix}${this.withoutHtmlCacheBust(scriptUrl)}${suffix}`;
640:         });
641:     }
642: 
643:     private withHtmlCacheBust(scriptUrl: string, cacheKey: string): string {
644:         const hashIndex = scriptUrl.indexOf('#');
645:         const hash = hashIndex === -1 ? '' : scriptUrl.substring(hashIndex);
646:         const urlWithoutHash = hashIndex === -1 ? scriptUrl : scriptUrl.substring(0, hashIndex);
647:         const queryIndex = urlWithoutHash.indexOf('?');
648:         const base = queryIndex === -1 ? urlWithoutHash : urlWithoutHash.substring(0, queryIndex);
649:         const query = queryIndex === -1 ? '' : urlWithoutHash.substring(queryIndex + 1);
650:         const paramPrefix = `${HTML_CACHE_BUST_PARAM}=`;
651:         const params = query.split('&').filter((param) => param && !param.startsWith(paramPrefix));
652: 
653:         params.push(`${paramPrefix}${encodeURIComponent(cacheKey)}`);
654: 
655:         return `${base}?${params.join('&')}${hash}`;
656:     }
657: 
658:     private withoutHtmlCacheBust(scriptUrl: string): string {
659:         const hashIndex = scriptUrl.indexOf('#');
660:         const hash = hashIndex === -1 ? '' : scriptUrl.substring(hashIndex);
661:         const urlWithoutHash = hashIndex === -1 ? scriptUrl : scriptUrl.substring(0, hashIndex);
662:         const queryIndex = urlWithoutHash.indexOf('?');
663: 
664:         if (queryIndex === -1) {
665:             return scriptUrl;
666:         }
667: 
668:         const base = urlWithoutHash.substring(0, queryIndex);
669:         const query = urlWithoutHash.substring(queryIndex + 1);
670:         const paramPrefix = `${HTML_CACHE_BUST_PARAM}=`;
671:         const params = query.split('&').filter((param) => param && !param.startsWith(paramPrefix));
672: 
673:         return `${base}${params.length ? `?${params.join('&')}` : ''}${hash}`;
674:     }
675: 
676:     // 获取要应用的js内容
677:     private getJs(): string {
678:         const particleJs = this.getParticleJs();
679: 
680:         return `
681:         /*ext-${this.extName}-start*/
682:         /*ext.${this.extName}.ver.${version}*/
683:         ${this.getLoaderJs()}
684:         ${particleJs}
685:         /*ext-${this.extName}-end*/
686:         `;
687:     }
688: 
689:     // 获取粒子效果js
690:     private getParticleJs(): string {
691:         const context = getContext();
692:         if (!context.globalState.get('backgroundCoverParticleEffect', false)) {
693:             return '';
694:         }
695: 
696:         const opacity = context.globalState.get('backgroundCoverParticleOpacity', 0.6);
697:         const color = context.globalState.get('backgroundCoverParticleColor', '#ffffff');
698:         const count = context.globalState.get('backgroundCoverParticleCount', 50);
699: 
700:         return getParticleEffectJs(opacity, color, count);
701:     }
702: 
703:     // 获取css内容
704:     private getCss(): string {
705:         const opacity = Math.min(this.imageOpacity, 0.8);
706:         const { sizeModelVal, repeatVal, positionVal } = this.getCssStyles();
707: 
708:         let rawPath = this.imagePath;
709:         const globalWindow = typeof globalThis !== 'undefined' ? (globalThis as any).window : undefined;
710:         
711:         if (this.forceHttpsUpgrade && rawPath.toLowerCase().startsWith('http://')) {
712:             if (globalWindow?.location?.protocol === 'https:') {
713:                 rawPath = rawPath.replace(/^http:\/\//i, 'https://');
714:             }
715:         }
716: 
717:         let cssPath = this.escapeTemplateLiteral(rawPath);
718: 
719:         if (this.isVideo) {
720:             const config = {
721:                 url: rawPath,
722:                 opacity: opacity,
723:                 blur: this.blur,
724:                 blendMode: this.blendModel
725:             };
726:             // Escape backticks and ${} for template literal safety, but keep backslashes as is (JSON stringified)
727:             const jsonConfig = JSON.stringify(config)
728:                 .replace(/`/g, '\\`')
729:                 .replace(/\$\{/g, '\\${');
730: 
731:             return `
732:             /*background-cover-video-start*/
733:             ${jsonConfig}
734:             /*background-cover-video-end*/
735:             ${this.getCorruptionWarningCss()}
736:             `;
737:         }
738: 
739:         return `
740:         body::before{
741:             content: "";
742:             top: 0;
743:             left: 0;
744:             width: 100%;
745:             height: 100%;
746:             position: absolute;
747:             background-size: ${sizeModelVal};
748:             background-repeat: ${repeatVal};
749:             background-position: ${positionVal};
750:             opacity:${opacity};
751:             background-image:url('${cssPath}');
752:             z-index: 2;
753:             pointer-events: none;
754:             filter: blur(${this.blur}px);
755:             mix-blend-mode: ${this.blendModel};
756:         }
757:         ${this.getCorruptionWarningCss()}
758:         `;
759:     }
760: 
761:     // 获取宠物配置
762:     private getPetConfig(): { enabled: boolean, walkUrl: string, idleUrl: string } {
763:         try {
764:             const context = getContext();
765:             let enabled = false;
766:             let type = 'akita';
767: 
768:             if (context) {
769:                 enabled = context.globalState.get<boolean>('backgroundCoverPetEnabled', false);
770:                 type = context.globalState.get<string>('backgroundCoverPetType', 'akita');
771:             }
772: 
773:             const mapping: any = {
774:                 'akita': { folder: 'dog', idle: 'akita_idle_8fps.gif', walk: 'akita_walk_8fps.gif' },
775:                 'totoro': { folder: 'totoro', idle: 'gray_idle_8fps.gif', walk: 'gray_walk_8fps.gif' },

836:             function updateVideo(config) {
837:                 let video = document.getElementById('background-cover-video');
838:                 if (!config) {
839:                     if (video) video.remove();
840:                     return;
841:                 }
842:                 if (!video) {
843:                     video = document.createElement('video');
844:                     video.id = 'background-cover-video';

846:                     video.loop = true;
847:                     video.muted = true;
848:                     video.style.position = 'absolute';
849:                     video.style.top = '0';
850:                     video.style.left = '0';
851:                     video.style.width = '100%';
852:                     video.style.height = '100%';
853:                     video.style.objectFit = 'cover';
854:                     video.style.zIndex = '2';
855:                     video.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
856:                     document.body.prepend(video);
857:                 }
858:                 
859:                 let url = config.url;
860:                 // HTTPS upgrade logic
861:                 if (url.toLowerCase().startsWith('http://') && window.location.protocol === 'https:') {
862:                     url = url.replace(/^http:\\/\\//i, 'https://');
863:                 }
864: 
865:                 // Ensure attributes are set
866:                 if (!video.loop) video.loop = true;
867:                 if (!video.muted) video.muted = true;
868: 
869:                 // Check if source actually changed to avoid reloading
870:                 // Use decodeURIComponent to handle encoded URLs (e.g. %20 for spaces)
871:                 let currentSrc = video.src;
872:                 let newSrc = url;
873:                 try {
874:                     if (currentSrc !== newSrc && decodeURIComponent(currentSrc) !== decodeURIComponent(newSrc)) {
875:                         video.src = newSrc;
876:                     }
877:                 } catch (e) {
878:                     if (currentSrc !== newSrc) {
879:                         video.src = newSrc;
880:                     }
881:                 }
882: 
883:                 video.style.opacity = config.opacity + '';
884:                 video.style.filter = 'blur(' + config.blur + 'px)';
885:                 video.style.mixBlendMode = config.blendMode;

889:                         if (e.name !== 'AbortError') {
890:                             console.error('BackgroundCover video play error:', e);
891:                         }
892:                     });
893:                 }
894:             }
895:         `;
896: 
897:         return `
898:         (function() {
899:             const cssDesktopUrl = '${escapedDesktopUrl}';
900:             const relativeCssPath = '${webCssPath}';
901:             const cssFileName = '${cssFileName}';
902:             const workbenchJsName = '${workbenchJsName}';

909: 
910:             function ensureTrailingSlash(value) {
911:                 if (!value) {
912:                     return '';
913:                 }
914:                 return value.endsWith('/') ? value : value + '/';
915:             }
916: 
917:             function getCssBaseHref(url) {
918:                 if (!url) {
919:                     return '';
920:                 }
921:                 let clean = url;
922:                 const hashIndex = clean.indexOf('#');
923:                 if (hashIndex !== -1) {
924:                     clean = clean.substring(0, hashIndex);
925:                 }
926:                 const queryIndex = clean.indexOf('?');
927:                 if (queryIndex !== -1) {
928:                     clean = clean.substring(0, queryIndex);
929:                 }
930:                 const slashIndex = clean.lastIndexOf('/');
931:                 if (slashIndex === -1) {
932:                     return ensureTrailingSlash(clean);
933:                 }
934:                 return ensureTrailingSlash(clean.substring(0, slashIndex + 1));
935:             }
936: 
937:             function replaceRelativeTokens(value, baseHref) {
938:                 if (!value || value.indexOf(relativePlaceholder) === -1) {
939:                     return value;
940:                 }
941:                 return value.split(relativePlaceholder).join(baseHref);
942:             }
943: 
944:             function deriveFromScript() {
945:                 if (typeof document === 'undefined') {
946:                     return undefined;
947:                 }
948: 
949:                 const buildFromSrc = (src) => {
950:                     try {
951:                         return new URL(cssFileName, src).toString();
952:                     } catch (error) {
953:                         console.error('[BackgroundCover] Script URL resolve error:', error);
954:                         return undefined;
955:                     }
956:                 };
957: 
958:                 const current = document.currentScript;
959:                 if (current && current.src) {
960:                     const candidate = buildFromSrc(current.src);
961:                     if (candidate) {
962:                         return candidate;
963:                     }
964:                 }
965: 
966:                 const scripts = document.getElementsByTagName ? document.getElementsByTagName('script') : [];
967:                 for (let i = scripts.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
968:                     const tag = scripts[i];
969:                     if (tag && tag.src && tag.src.indexOf(workbenchJsName) !== -1) {
970:                         const candidate = buildFromSrc(tag.src);
971:                         if (candidate) {
972:                             return candidate;
973:                         }
974:                     }
975:                 }
976: 
977:                 return undefined;
978:             }
979: 
980:             const resolveCssUrl = () => {
981:                 const scriptResolved = deriveFromScript();
982:                 if (scriptResolved) {
983:                     return scriptResolved;
984:                 }
985: 
986:                 const relativePath = relativeCssPath;
987:                 if (relativePath) {
988:                     const bases = [];
989:                     const monacoEnv = typeof globalThis !== 'undefined' ? globalThis.MonacoEnvironment || {} : {};
990:                     if (monacoEnv.baseUrl) {
991:                         bases.push(monacoEnv.baseUrl);
992:                     }
993:                     if (monacoEnv.appOrigin) {
994:                         bases.push(monacoEnv.appOrigin);
995:                     }
996:                     if (typeof document !== 'undefined' && document.baseURI) {
997:                         bases.push(document.baseURI);
998:                     }
999:                     if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.location) {
1000:                         const { origin, href } = window.location;
1001:                         if (origin) {
1002:                             bases.push(origin + '/');
1003:                         }
1004:                         if (href) {
1005:                             const slashIndex = href.lastIndexOf('/');
1006:                             if (slashIndex !== -1) {
1007:                                 bases.push(href.substring(0, slashIndex + 1));
1008:                             }
1009:                         }
1010:                     }
1011: 
1012:                     for (const base of bases) {
1013:                         try {
1014:                             return new URL(relativePath, base).toString();
1015:                         } catch (error) {
1016:                             console.error('[BackgroundCover] Base URL failed:', error);
1017:                         }
1018:                     }
1019: 
1020:                     if (!relativePath.startsWith('http')) {
1021:                         try {
1022:                             return new URL(relativePath, '/').toString();
1023:                         } catch (error) {
1024:                             console.error('[BackgroundCover] Relative URL failed:', error);
1025:                         }
1026:                     }
1027:                 }
1028:

1030:             };

1033:

1038:                 if (!style) {
```

```
4: export class BlendHelper {
5: 
6: 	public static autoBlendModel(): string {
7: 		let blendStr = '';
8: 		let themeKind = window.activeColorTheme.kind;
9: 		if ( themeKind === ColorThemeKind.Dark ) {
10: 			blendStr = 'lighten';
11: 		} else if ( themeKind === ColorThemeKind.Light ) {
12: 			// console.log('浅色模式');
13: 			blendStr = 'multiply';
14: 		} else {
15: 			// console.log('高对比模式');
16: 			blendStr = 'lighten';
17: 		}
18: 		return blendStr;
19: 	}
```

```
55:     context: WebviewViewResolveContext,
56:     _token: CancellationToken,
57:   ) {
58:     this._view = webviewView;
59: 
60:     webviewView.onDidDispose(() => {
61:       this._view = undefined;
62:     });
63: 
64:     this._view.webview.options = {
65:       enableScripts: true,
66:     };
67: 
68:     const pageToLoad = this._pendingPage;
69:     this._pendingPage = undefined;
70:     this._view.webview.html = this.getHtmlForWebview(pageToLoad);

72:         async message => {
73:             if (this._isProcessing) { return; }
74:             this._isProcessing = true;
75:             try {
76:                 switch (message.command) {
77:                     case 'set_img':
78:                       if(message.data.link){
79:                         let context = getContext();
80:                         await context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverOnlineDefault', message.data.link);
81:                       }
82:                       await PickList.updateImgPath(message.data.url);
83:                       break;
84:                     case 'set_home':
85:                       let context = getContext();
86:                       await context.globalState.update('backgroundCoverOnlineDefault', message.data.url);
87:                       await PickList.updateImgPath(message.data.url);
88:                       window.showInformationMessage("配置帖子图库成功，记得开启自动更换功能噢！/ Set successfully, remember to turn on the auto-change function!");
89:                       break;
90:                 }
91:             } finally {
92:                 this._isProcessing = false;
93:             }
94:         },
95:         this,
96:         this._disposables
97:     );
98:   }

121:         </style>
122:       </head>
```

```
190:     }else{
191:         // 0.5.0版本后数据结构重构，放弃直接修改crtBgObj的.offx offy
192:         // 因为需要考虑到不同的设备有不同的设置，而这个设置不应该同步
193:         // 所以使用存在local配置中的'bgObjCfg' -> [img.hash].offx offy来进行记录和控制
194:         let bgObjCfg = confmngr.get('bgObjCfg')
195: 
196:         let crtBgObj = confmngr.get('crtBgObj');
197:         let crtBgObjHash = crtBgObj?.hash ?? '';
198: 
199:         var offx: string = '50'  // 默认居中
200:         var offy: string = '50'
201:         if (crtBgObjHash in bgObjCfg) {
202:             offx = bgObjCfg[crtBgObjHash].offx
203:             offy = bgObjCfg[crtBgObjHash].offy
204:         }
205: 
206:         changeBgPosition(offx, offy)
207:     }
208:     
209:     settingsUI.updateSettingPanelElementStatus()
210: }

(End of file - total 210 lines)
</content>
```

```
163: export async function selectPictureByHand() {

167: export async function selectPictureRandom(manualPress: boolean = false) {
168:     const cacheImgNum = fileManagerUI.getCacheImgNum()
169:     if (cacheImgNum === 0) {
170:         // 没有缓存任何图片，使用默认的了了妹图片ULR来当作背景图
171:         bgRender.useDefaultLiaoLiaoBg();
172:         showMessage(`${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.noCachedImg4random}`, 3000, "info")
173:     } else if (cacheImgNum === 1) {
174:         // 只有一张图，无法进行随机抽选(无变化)
175:         if (manualPress) {
176:             showMessage(`${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.selectPictureRandomNotice}`, 3000, "info")
177:         }
178: 
179:         let belayerElement = document.getElementById('bglayer')
180:         // 如果当前背景不存在任何图片
181:         if (belayerElement.style.getPropertyValue('background-image') === '') {
182:             let bgObj = confmngr.get('fileidx')[0]
183:             bgRender.changeBackgroundContent(bgObj.path, bgObj.mode)
184:         }
185:     } else {
186:         // 随机选择一张图
187:         let fileidx = confmngr.get('fileidx')
188: 
189:         let crtBgObj = confmngr.get('crtBgObj');
190: 
191:         // 使用可选链 ?. 和空值合并 ?? 来安全地获取 crt_hash
192:         let crtHash = crtBgObj?.hash ?? '';
193:         if (crtHash === '') {
194:             crtHash = "emptyCrtObj"
195:         }
196: 
197:         let rndHash = ''
198: 
199:         while (true) {
200:             let r = Math.floor(Math.random() * cacheImgNum)
201:             rndHash = Object.keys(fileidx)[r]
202:             debug(`[topbarUI][selectPictureRandom] 随机抽一张，之前：${crtHash}，随机到：${rndHash}`)
203:             if (rndHash !== crtHash) {
204:                 // 确保随机到另一张图而不是当前的图片
205:                 debug(`[topbarUI][selectPictureRandom] 已抽到不同的背景图${rndHash}，进行替换`)
206:                 break
207:             }
208:         }
209:         debug('[topbarUI][selectPictureRandom] 跳出抽卡死循环,前景图为：', fileidx[rndHash])
210:         bgRender.changeBackgroundContent(fileidx[rndHash].path, fileidx[rndHash].mode)
211:         confmngr.set('crtBgObj', fileidx[rndHash])
212:     }
213:     await confmngr.save('[topbarUI][selectPictureRandom]')
214:     settingsUI.updateSettingPanelElementStatus()
215: }
216: 
217: export async function addSeveralLocalImagesFile() {
218: 
219:     const cacheImgNum = fileManagerUI.getCacheImgNum();
220: 
221:     if (cacheImgNum >= cst.cacheMaxNum) {
222:         showMessage(window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addSingleImageExceed1 + cst.cacheMaxNum + window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addSingleImageExceed2, 7000, 'error');
223:     }else{
224:         // return an Array
225:         const fileHandle = await os.openFilePicker(cst.supportedImageSuffix.toString(), true)
226:         let lastUploadedBgObj: any;
227: 
228:         for (const [index, file] of fileHandle.entries()) {
229:             const isLast = (index === fileHandle.length - 1);
230: 
231:             let bgObj = await fileManagerUI.uploadOneImage(file);
232: 
233:             // 文件不重复且上传成功
234:             if (bgObj !== undefined) {
235:                 lastUploadedBgObj = bgObj; // 记录最后一次成功上传的对象
236:                 // 只在最后一次循环时保存和更新UI，减少开销
237:                 if (isLast) {
238:                     await confmngr.save('[topbarUI][addSeveralLocalImagesFile]');
239:                     settingsUI.updateSettingPanelElementStatus();
240:                     bgRender.changeBackgroundContent(lastUploadedBgObj.path, lastUploadedBgObj.mode);
241:                 }
242:             };
243:         }
244:     };
245: };
246: 
247: export async function addDirectory() {
248:     const cacheImgNum = fileManagerUI.getCacheImgNum();
249: 
250:     const fileList = await os.openFolderPicker();
251: 
252:     let fileContainer:Array<File> = [];
253: 
254:     // 遍历文件夹中的每个文件
255:     for await (const file of fileList) {
256:         // 检查文件类型是否为文件，排除文件夹
257:         const fileName = file.name;
258: 
259:         const [prefix, suffix] = os.splitext(fileName)
260:         // suffix = 'jpg'
261:         debug(`[topbarUI][addDirectory] 当前图片${fileName}后缀为${suffix}, 存在于允许的图片后缀(${cst.supportedImageSuffix})中：${cst.supportedImageSuffix.includes(`.${suffix}`)}`)
262:         if (cst.supportedImageSuffix.includes(`.${suffix}`)) {
263: 
264:             let md5 = await fileManagerUI.imgExistsInCache(file, false);
265: 
266:             if (md5 !== 'exists') {
267:                 fileContainer.push(file)
268:             }else{
269:                 debug(`[topbarUI][addDirectory] 当前图片${fileName}md5为${md5}, 存在于缓存中`)
270:             }
271:         }
272: 
273:         debug(`[topbarUI][addDirectory] fileContainer`, fileContainer)
274: 
275:         if (fileContainer.length >= cst.cacheMaxNum - cacheImgNum) {
276:             showMessage(window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addDirectoryLabelError1 + cst.cacheMaxNum + window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addDirectoryLabelError2, 7000, 'error')
277:             break
278:         }
279:     }
280: 
281:     if (fileContainer.length >= 30) {
282:         confirm(
283:             window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addDirectoryLabelConfirmTitle,
284:             `${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addDirectoryLabelConfirm1} ${fileContainer.length} ${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addDirectoryLabelConfirm2}`,
285:             async () => {
286:                 // 同意上传，则开始批量上传
287:                 await fileManagerUI.batchUploadImages(fileContainer, true);
288:             }
289:         )
290:     }else{
291:          // 要上传的数量比较少，直接开始批量上传
292:         await fileManagerUI.batchUploadImages(fileContainer, true);
293:     }
294: }
295: 
296: export async function addNoteAssetsDirectory() {
297:     showNotImplementDialog();
298:     return;
299: 
300:     const selectedPath = await fileManagerUI.openAssetsFolderPickerDialog();
301: 
302:     if (selectedPath) {

307:         // 3. 触发文件索引同步
308:         showMessage(`已选择文件夹: ${selectedPath}`);
309:     } else {
310:         debug('[topbarUI][addNoteAssetsDirectory] User cancelled folder selection.');
311:     }
312: }
```

```
360:     const tabBar = dialog.element.querySelector('.b3-tab-bar');
361:     tabBar.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
362:         const target = event.target as HTMLElement;
363:         const tabElement = target.closest('li');
364: 
365:         if (tabElement && !tabElement.classList.contains('b3-list-item--focus')) {
366:             const tabName = tabElement.getAttribute('data-name');
367:             
368:             // Update tab buttons state
369:             tabBar.querySelectorAll('li').forEach(item => {
370:                 item.classList.remove('b3-list-item--focus');
371:             });
372:             tabElement.classList.add('b3-list-item--focus');
373: 
374:             // Update tab containers visibility
375:             dialog.element.querySelectorAll('.config__tab-container').forEach((container: HTMLElement) => {
376:                 container.classList.add('fn__none');
377:             });
378:             dialog.element.querySelector(`.config__tab-container[data-name="${tabName}"]`).classList.remove('fn__none');
379:         }
380:     });

382:     //=================
383:     // 图片偏移的相关设置
384:     //=================
385:     const cxElement = document.getElementById('cx') as HTMLInputElement;
386:     const cyElement = document.getElementById('cy') as HTMLInputElement;
387: 
388:     updateOffsetSwitch()
389:     window.addEventListener('resize', updateOffsetSwitch)
390: 
391:     let elementsArray = [cxElement, cyElement]
392:     // 用循环给两个element绑定相同的函数功能
393:     for (let i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
394:         // 拖动的时候，修改图片的位置
395:         elementsArray[i].addEventListener("input", () => {
396:             debug(elementsArray, cxElement.value, cyElement.value)
397:             bgRender.changeBgPosition(cxElement.value, cyElement.value)
398:         })
399:         // 停止拖动的时候，保存图片的位置
400:         elementsArray[i].addEventListener("change", () => {
401:             //
402:             let crtBgObj = confmngr.get('crtBgObj')
403: 
404:             // 使用默认的了了图，此时bgObj为undefined，没有下面这些属性，跳过
405:             if (crtBgObj !== undefined) {
406: 
407:                 // 0.5.0版本后数据结构重构，放弃直接修改crtBgObj的.offx offy
408:                 // 因为需要考虑到不同的设备有不同的设置，而这个设置不应该同步
409:                 // 所以使用存在local配置中的'bgObjCfg' -> [img.hash].offx offy来进行记录和控制
410:                 let crtBgObjHash = crtBgObj.hash
411: 
412:                 let bgObjCfg = confmngr.get('bgObjCfg')
413:                 let crtBjObjCfg = bgObjCfg[crtBgObjHash]
414: 
415:                 if (crtBjObjCfg === undefined) {
416:                     crtBjObjCfg = {
417:                         offx: '50',
418:                         offy: '50',
419:                     }
420:                 }
421: 
422:                 crtBjObjCfg.offx = cxElement.value
423:                 crtBjObjCfg.offy = cyElement.value
424: 
425:                 bgObjCfg[crtBgObjHash] = crtBjObjCfg
426: 
427:                 confmngr.set('bgObjCfg', bgObjCfg)
428: 
429:                 confmngr.save('[settingsUI][openSettingDialog][cxyElement.change]');
430:             }
431: 
432:         })
433:     }
```
