555: export function generatedisabledThemeElement(){
556:     const [themeMode, themeName] = getCurrentThemeInfo();
557: 
558:     const installedThemes = getInstalledThemes();
559:     /**
560:      installedThemes = [lightThemes, darkThemes]
561:      lightThemes = [
562:         {
563:             "name": "daylight",
564:             "label": "daylight（默认主题）"
565:         },
566:         ...
567:     ]
568:     **/
569: 
570:     const ThemeBlockContainer = [
571:         document.getElementById('lightThemeBlockContainer') as HTMLDivElement,
572:         document.getElementById('darkThemeBlockContainer') as HTMLDivElement,
573:     ]
574: 
575:     var disabledThemeConfig = confmngr.get('disabledTheme');
576:     const themeModeText = ['light', 'dark']
577:     debug('[settingsUI][generatedisabledThemeElement] Current block theme config:', disabledThemeConfig)
578:     
579:     // i==0 -> light; i == 1 -> dark
580:     for (var i = 0; i < installedThemes.length; i++) {
581:         var iThemes = installedThemes[i];
582: 
583:         // iter each mode themes
584:         for (var j = 0; j < iThemes.length; j++) {
585:             /**
586:              *  检查config里面的设置
587:              */ 
588:             var itheme = iThemes[j] // 安装的某个 dark|light theme
589:             // itheme = {"name": "daylight", "label": "daylight（默认主题）"}
590: 
591:             var btnOnOffValue: boolean;  // 该主题是否屏蔽
592: 
593:             // if "dark+" in 'disabledTheme.light' keys
594:             var ithemeConfig = disabledThemeConfig[themeModeText[i]]
595:             if (itheme["name"] in ithemeConfig) {
596:                 // 在设置中存在，直接读取之前的设置值
597:                 btnOnOffValue = ithemeConfig[itheme["name"]];
598:             } else {
599:                 // 在设置中不存在，添加然后设置值为false
600:                 btnOnOffValue = false;
601:                 ithemeConfig[itheme["name"]] = btnOnOffValue;
602:             }
603: 
604:             /**
605:              *  添加设置中的按钮
606:              */ 
607:             let parser = new DOMParser();
608:             var blockLabelItem = parser.parseFromString(`
609:             <div class="b3-card b3-card--wrap">
610:                 <div class="fn__flex-1 fn__flex-column">
611:                     <div class="b3-card__info b3-card__info--left fn__flex-1">
612:                         <span class="crt_plugin-placeholder">${itheme['name']}</span>
613:                         <!-- span class="ft__on-surface ft__smaller"></span -->
614:                         <div class="b3-card__desc">
615:                             ${itheme['label']}
616:                         </div>
617:                     </div>
618:                 </div>
619:                 <div class="b3-card__actions b3-card__actions--right">
620:                     <span class="fn__space"></span>
621:                     <input class="b3-switch fn__flex-center" data-mode="${themeModeText[i]}" data-theme="${itheme['name']}" type="checkbox"></input>
622:                 </div>
623:             </div>
624:             `, 'text/html').body.firstChild as HTMLDivElement
625:             
626:             ThemeBlockContainer[i].appendChild(blockLabelItem);
627: 
628:             // 高亮当前主题
629:             debug(`添加当前主题的蓝色高亮`, itheme["name"], themeName)
630:             if (themeMode === i && itheme["name"] === themeName) {
631:                 debug(`      => 匹配到一致的主题`)
632:                 let textSpan = blockLabelItem.querySelector('span.crt_plugin-placeholder') as HTMLElement;
633: 
634:                 textSpan.style.setProperty('color', 'var(--b3-theme-primary)');
635:                 textSpan.textContent += `[${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.crtThemeText}]`
636:             }
637: 
638:             /**
639:              * 绑定开关
640:              */
641:             let onOffBtn = blockLabelItem.querySelectorAll('input')[0]
642:             onOffBtn.checked = btnOnOffValue;
643: 
644:             onOffBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
645:                 var disabledThemeCfg = confmngr.get('disabledTheme');
646: 
647:                 let mode = onOffBtn.getAttribute('data-mode');
648:                 let theme = onOffBtn.getAttribute('data-theme');
649: 
650:                 disabledThemeCfg[mode][theme] = !disabledThemeCfg[mode][theme]
651:                 debug(`[settingsUI] User changed disabledTheme ${theme} in ${mode} mode`)
652:                 
653:                 confmngr.set('disabledTheme', disabledThemeCfg);
654:                 confmngr.save('[settingsUI][generatedisabledThemeElement][onOffBtn.click]');
655: 
656:                 await bgRender.applySettings();
657:             })
658:         }
659:     }
660:     confmngr.set('disabledTheme', disabledThemeConfig);
661:     confmngr.save('[settingsUI][generatedisabledThemeElement]');
662: }
663: 
664: export function updateSliderElement(elementid:string, value:string, setAriaLabel:boolean=true) {
665:     let sliderElement = document.getElementById(elementid) as HTMLInputElement
666:     if (sliderElement === null || sliderElement=== undefined) {
667:         // debug(`Setting panel not open`) 
668:     } else {
669:         sliderElement.value = value;
670:         if (setAriaLabel) {
671:             sliderElement.parentElement.setAttribute('aria-label', value);
672:         }
673:     }
674: }
675: 
676: export function updateCheckedElement(elementid:string, value:boolean) {
677:     let checkedElement = document.getElementById(elementid) as HTMLInputElement
678:     if (checkedElement === null || checkedElement === undefined) {
679:         // debug(`Setting panel not open`) 
680:     } else {
681:         checkedElement.checked = value;
682:     }
683: }
684: 
685: export function opacityShortcut(isAdd:boolean) {
686:     var opacity = confmngr.get('opacity');
687:     if (isAdd) {
688:         opacity = Number((opacity + 0.1).toFixed(2));
689:     } else {
690:         opacity = Number((opacity - 0.1).toFixed(2));
691:     };
692: 
693:     if (opacity > 1 || opacity < 0) {
694:         showMessage(`[${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addTopBarIcon}]${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.opacityShortcutOverflow}`, 4000, 'info')
695:         return;
696:     } else {
697:         confmngr.set('opacity', opacity);
698:         confmngr.save('[settingsUI][opacityShortcut]');
699:         if (confmngr.get('activate')) {
700:             bgRender.changeOpacity(opacity);
701:         }
702:         updateSliderElement('opacityInput', `${opacity}`);
703:     };
704: 
705: }
706: 
707: export function blurShortcut(isAdd:boolean) {
708:     var blur = confmngr.get('blur');
709:     if (isAdd) {
710:         blur = Number((blur + 1).toFixed(0));
711:     } else {
712:         blur = Number((blur - 1).toFixed(0));
713:     };
714: 
715:     if (blur > 10 || blur < 0) {
716:         showMessage(`[${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addTopBarIcon}]${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.blurShortcutOverflow}`, 4000, 'info')
717:         return;
718:     } else {
719:         confmngr.set('blur', blur);
720:         confmngr.save('[settingsUI][blurShortcut]');
721:         if (confmngr.get('activate')) {
722:             bgRender.changeBlur(blur);
723:         }
724:         updateSliderElement('blurInput', `${blur}`);
725:     };
726: }
727: 
728: export function updateSettingPanelElementStatus() {
729:     // update current image URL
730:     let crtImageNameElement = document.getElementById('crtImgName')
731:     if (crtImageNameElement === null || crtImageNameElement === undefined) {
732:         // debug(`Setting panel not open`) 
733:     } else {
734:         let bgObj = confmngr.get('crtBgObj')
735:         if (confmngr.get('crtBgObj') === undefined) {
736:             crtImageNameElement.textContent = cst.demoImgURL.toString()
737:         } else {
738:             crtImageNameElement.textContent = bgObj.name
739:         }
740:     }
741: 
742:     updateOffsetSwitch()
743: 
744:     // 更新setting中的[imgNum]数字
745:     let cacheImgNumEle = document.getElementById('cacheImgNumElement')
746:     if (cacheImgNumEle === null || cacheImgNumEle === undefined) {
747:         // debug(`Setting panel not open`) 
748:     } else {
749:         const cacheImgNum = fileManagerUI.getCacheImgNum()
750:         cacheImgNumEle.textContent = `[ ${cacheImgNum} ]`
751:     }
752: 
753:     // update onoff switch button
754:     updateCheckedElement('onoffInput', confmngr.get('activate'))
755: 
756:     // 更新autorefresh相关按钮
757:     updateAutoFreshStatus()
758: 
759:     // 更新opacity滑动条
760:     updateSliderElement('opacityInput', confmngr.get('opacity'))
761: 
762:     // 更新blur滑动条
763:     updateSliderElement('blurInput', confmngr.get('blur'))
764: 
765:     // 更新开发者模式按钮
766:     updateCheckedElement('devModeInput', confmngr.get('inDev'))
767: 
768: }
769: 
770: export function updateOffsetSwitch() {
771:     let cxElement = document.getElementById('cx') as HTMLInputElement
772:     let cyElement = document.getElementById('cy') as HTMLInputElement
773: 
774:     if (cxElement === null || cxElement === undefined) {
775:         // debug(`Setting panel not open`) 
776:     } else {
777:         let bglayerElement = document.getElementById('bglayer')
778:         if (confmngr.get('activate')) {
779:             const container_h = parseInt(getComputedStyle(bglayerElement).height)  // -> '1280px'
780:             const container_w = parseInt(getComputedStyle(bglayerElement).width)
781: 
782:             let fullside: string
783:             // 使用默认的了了图
784:             if (confmngr.get('crtBgObj') === undefined) {
785:                 fullside = cv2.getFullSide(
786:                     container_w, container_h,
787:                     2458, 1383 // 默认了了图的宽高
788:                 )
789:                 // 重新设置一下x和y的值
790:                 cxElement.value = '50'
791:                 cyElement.value = '50'
792:             }else{
793:                 fullside = cv2.getFullSide(
794:                     container_w, container_h,
795:                     confmngr.get('crtBgObj').width, confmngr.get('crtBgObj').height
796:                 )
797:             }
798: 
799:             if (fullside === 'X') {
800:                 cxElement.disabled = true
801:                 cyElement.disabled = false
802:                 cxElement.style.setProperty('opacity', '0.1')

805:                 cyElement.disabled = true
806:                 cxElement.disabled = false
807:                 cyElement.style.setProperty('opacity', '0.1')
808:                 cxElement.style.removeProperty('opacity')
809:             }
810:         } else {
811:             cyElement.disabled = true
812:             cxElement.disabled = true
813:             cyElement.style.setProperty('opacity', '0.1')
814:             cxElement.style.setProperty('opacity', '0.1')
815:         }
816:     }
817: }

819: export function updateAutoFreshStatus() {
820:     updateCheckedElement('autoRefreshInput', confmngr.get('autoRefresh'))
821: 
822:     // 如果auto refresh 是 off的情况，需要更新一下定时切换时间的状态为disabled
823:     const autoRefreshTimeElement = document.getElementById('autoRefreshTimeInput') as HTMLInputElement;
824:     if (autoRefreshTimeElement === null || autoRefreshTimeElement === undefined) {
825:         // debug(`Setting panel not open`) 
826:     } else {
827:         if (!confmngr.get('autoRefresh')) {
828:             autoRefreshTimeElement.disabled = true;
829:             autoRefreshTimeElement.style.setProperty('background-color', 'var(--b3-theme-surface-lighter)');
830:             autoRefreshTimeElement.style.setProperty('color', 'var(--b3-theme-disabled)');

832:             autoRefreshTimeElement.disabled = false;
833:             autoRefreshTimeElement.style.removeProperty('background-color');

63:   public async siyuanRequest(url: string, data: object): Promise<SiyuanData> {
64:     const reqUrl = `${siyuanApiUrl}${url}`
65: 
66:     const fetchOps = {
67:       body: JSON.stringify(data),
68:       method: "POST",
69:     }
70:

76:       })

80: 
81:     const response = await fetch(reqUrl, fetchOps)
82:     const resJson = (await response.json()) as SiyuanData
83: 
84:     debug("[utils][api.ts][siyuanRequest] 思源请求数据返回，resJson=>", resJson)
85: 
86:     if (resJson.code === -1) {
87:       throw new Error(resJson.msg)
88:     }
89:     return resJson
90:   }

148:             resolve(data)
149:           } else {

292:     public async getLocalStorage(key?: string): Promise<SiyuanData | any> {
293:       const response = await this.siyuanRequest("/api/storage/getLocalStorage", {});
294:       if (response.code !== 0) {
295:         throw new Error(`获取存储失败: ${response.msg}`);
296:       }
297:       const storageData = response.data as LocalStorageData;
298:       if (key === undefined) {
299:         // 返回全部数据
300:         return storageData;
301:       }
302:       if (!(key in storageData)) {
303:         // throw new Error(`存储键 "${key}" 不存在`);
304:         return undefined;
305:       }
306:       // 返回指定键值
307:       return storageData[key];
308:     }

311:      * 更新思源笔记本地存储中的指定键值
312:      * @param key 要更新的键名
313:      * @param value 要设置的值
314:      */
315:     public async setLocalStorage<T = any>(key: string, value: T): Promise<void> {
316:       // 1. 复用 getLocalStorage 获取当前完整存储
317:       let currentStorage: LocalStorageData = {};
318:       
319:       try {
320:         const response = await this.getLocalStorage();
321:         currentStorage = response || {};
322:       } catch (e) {
323:         console.warn("获取当前存储失败，将使用空对象", e);
324:       }
325:       // 2. 创建更新后的存储对象
326:       const updatedStorage = {
327:         ...currentStorage,
328:         [key]: value
329:       };
330:       // 3. 设置更新后的完整存储
331:       const setResponse = await this.siyuanRequest("/api/storage/setLocalStorage", {
332:         // key: "", // 注意: 思源API可能需要空key表示整个存储
333:         val: updatedStorage
334:       });
335:       if (setResponse.code !== 0) {
336:         throw new Error(`存储更新失败: ${setResponse.msg}`);
337:       }
338:     }
339: 
340: }

(End of file - total 340 lines)
</content>
```

4: export function getCurrentThemeInfo() {
5:     // 0 -> light, 1 -> dark
6:     const themeMode = (window as any).siyuan.config.appearance.mode
7:     let themeName = ''
8:

92:

138:     } else {

167: export async function clearCacheFolder(mode: tps.bgMode){
168:     // 图片模式
169:     if (mode == tps.bgMode.image) {
170:         // 这里应该获取fileidx里面的列表，而不是文件夹内的文件，不然图片缺失的话，删除不掉

174:

176:         for (let i in imgList) {
177:             let item = imgList[i]
178: 
179:             if (item.isDir) {
180:                 // 如果是文件夹，则递归删除，由于这个已经是根目录了，里面的任何文件夹直接无脑删除
181:                 os.rmtree(`${cst.pluginAssetsDir}/${item.name}/`)
182:             }else{
183:                 let full_path = `${cst.pluginAssetsDir}/${item.name}`
184:                 await ka.removeFile(full_path)
185: 
186:                 const [hash_name, suffix] = os.splitext(item.name.split('-')[1])
187: 
188:                 delete fileidx[hash_name]
189:             }
190:         }
191: 
192:         confmngr.set('fileidx', fileidx)
193: 
194:         // 清除缓存控制面板中的列表项和图片缓存
195:         let ulContainerElement = document.getElementById('cacheImgList');
196:         if (ulContainerElement) {
197:             ulContainerElement.innerHTML = null;
198:         }
199:         
200:         let displayDivElement = document.getElementById("displayCanvas");
201:         if (displayDivElement) {
202:             displayDivElement.innerHTML = null;
203:         }
204:     }    
205:

207:     if (cacheImgNum === 0) {
208:         // 没有缓存任何图片，使用默认的了了妹图片ULR来当作背景图
209:         bgRender.useDefaultLiaoLiaoBg();
210:     };
211: 
212:     await confmngr.save('[fileManagerUI][clearCacheFolder]');
213: }
214: 
215: export async function imgExistsInCache(file: File, notice: boolean = true): Promise<string> {
216:     let fileidx = confmngr.get('fileidx')
217: 
218:     const blobSlice = File.prototype.slice
219:     var chunk_blob = blobSlice.call(file, 0, Math.min(file.size, cst.hashLength)); // 2mb header blob
220: 
221:     let file_content = await chunk_blob.text()
222:     
223:     var md5_slice = Md5.hashStr(`${file_content}${file.size}`).slice(0, 15);
224: 
225:     debug(`[fileManagerUI][imgExistsInCache] Blob content: [${file_content.slice(20,40)} ...] with length = ${file_content.length}file.size=${file.size}`);
226: 
227:     if (fileidx !== undefined && md5_slice in fileidx) {
228:         if (notice) {
229:             const dialog = new Dialog({
230:                 title: `${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.inDevTitle}`,
231:                 content: `<div class="b3-dialog__content">${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.imageFileExist}</div>`,
232:                 width: window.bgCoverPlugin.isMobileLayout ? "92vw" : "520px",
233:             });
234:         }else{
235:             debug(`[fileManagerUI][imgIsInCache] 当前图片${file.name}已存在`)
236:         }
237:         return 'exists'
238:     } else {
239:         return md5_slice
240:     }
241: }
242: 
243: export async function uploadOneImage(file: File) {
244:     let fileSizeMB: number = (file.size / 1024 / 1024);
245: 
246:     let md5_slice = await imgExistsInCache(file);
247: 
248:     if (md5_slice !== 'exists') {
249:         showMessage(`${file.name}-${fileSizeMB.toFixed(2)}MB<br>${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addSingleImageUploadNotice}`, 3000, "info");
250:     }
251: 
252:     let fileidx = confmngr.get('fileidx');
253:     if (fileidx === undefined || fileidx === null) {
254:         fileidx = {};
255:     };
256: 
257:     // 检查是否已经在缓存目录中存在了该图片
258:     if (md5_slice !== 'exists') {
259:         const [prefix, suffix] = os.splitext(file.name)
260:         const hashedName = `hash-${md5_slice}.${suffix}`
261: 
262:         const uploadResult = await ka.putFile(`${cst.pluginAssetsDir}/${hashedName}`, file);
263: 
264:         if (uploadResult.code === 0) {
265:             // slice(5) to remove '/data' prefix
266:             const imgPath = `${cst.pluginAssetsDir.slice(5)}/${hashedName}`
267: 
268:             const imageSize = await cv2.getImageSize(imgPath)
269: 
270:             let bgObj: tps.bgObj = {
271:                 name: file.name,
272:                 hash: md5_slice,
273:                 mode: tps.bgMode.image,
274:                 path: imgPath,
275:                 width: imageSize.width,
276:                 height: imageSize.height,
277:                 parent: cst.pluginAssetsId
278:             }
279: 
280:             fileidx[bgObj.hash] = bgObj;
281: 
282:             confmngr.set('crtBgObj', bgObj);
283:             confmngr.set('fileidx', fileidx);
284: 
285:             debug(`[fileManagerUI][addSingleLocalImageFile]: fileidx ${fileidx}`);
286: 
287:             return bgObj
288:         } else {
289:             error(`fail to upload file ${file.name} with error code ${uploadResult}`)
290:             return null
291:         }
292:     }
293: }
294: 
295: export async function batchUploadImages(
296:     fileArray: Array<File>, 
297:     applySetting:boolean=false
298:     ) 
299: {
300:     let bgObj:tps.bgObj;
301: 
302:     debug('[fileManagerUI][batchUploadImages] fileArray', fileArray)
303: 
304:     if (fileArray.length === 0) {
305:         debug('[fileManagerUI][batchUploadImages] fileArray为空，不存在需要上传的图片')
306:     }else{
307:         for (let file of fileArray) {
308:             bgObj = await uploadOneImage(file);
309: 
310:             debug('[fileManagerUI][batchUploadImages] 在上传的循环内', bgObj)
311:         };
312: 
313:         await confmngr.save('[fileManagerUI][batchUploadImages]');
314: 
315:         if (applySetting){
316:             debug('[fileManagerUI][batchUploadImages] 在应用设置的判断内', bgObj)
317:             bgRender.changeBackgroundContent(bgObj.path, bgObj.mode);
318:             settingsUI.updateSettingPanelElementStatus();
319:         }
320:     }
321: }

468:             bgRender.changeBackgroundContent(bgObj.path, bgObj.mode);
469:             confmngr.set('crtBgObj', bgObj);
470:         
471:             confmngr.save('[fileManagerUI][generateCacheImgList][setBgBtn.click]');
472:         });
473: 
474: 
475:         /**
476:          * 删除当前背景图
477:          */
478:         delBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
479:             debug('Remove the background');
480:     
481:             // 移除管理面板中的项目
482:             let ulContainerElement = document.getElementById('cacheImgList');
483:             let rmLiEle = ulContainerElement.querySelectorAll(`[data-hash="${bgObj.hash}"]`)[0];
484:             rmLiEle.remove();
485:         
486:             // 清理管理面板下方的图片预览
487:             let displayDivElement = document.getElementById("displayCanvas");
488:             displayDivElement.innerHTML = null;
489:         
490:             // 移除fileidx中的项目
491:             topbarUI.selectPictureRandom();
492:             let fileidx = confmngr.get('fileidx');
493:             delete fileidx[bgObj.hash];
494:             confmngr.set('fileidx', fileidx);
495:         
496:             // 调用os来移除本地文件夹中的缓存文件
497:             debug(`[fileManagerUI][_rmBg] 移除下列路径的图片：${cst.pluginAssetsDir}/${bgObj.name}`);
498:             ka.removeFile(`data/${bgObj.path}`);
499:         
500:             // 检查当前文件数量是否为空，如果为空则设置为默认了了图
501:             const cacheImgNum = getCacheImgNum();
502:             if (cacheImgNum === 0) {
503:                 // 没有缓存任何图片，使用默认的了了妹图片ULR来当作背景图
504:                 bgRender.useDefaultLiaoLiaoBg();
505:             };
506:         
507:             confmngr.save('[fileManagerUI][generateCacheImgList][delBtn.click]');
508:         });
509: 
510:         /**
511:          * 鼠标悬停显示背景图
512:          */
513:         ulElementHtml.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
514:             let displayDivElement = document.getElementById("displayCanvas");
515: 
516:             displayDivElement.innerHTML = `<img style="max-height: 100%" src="${bgObj.path}">`;
517:         });
518: 
519:         listHtml.push(ulElementHtml);
520:     }
521: 
522:     return listHtml;
523: }

527: // Asset UI Manager //
528: //////////////////////
529: 
530:  export function openAssetsFolderPickerDialog(): Promise<string[] | null> {
531:     const rootPath = 'data/assets';
532:     const selectedPaths: Set<string> = new Set();
533:     
534:     // siyuan file tree:
535:     //
536:     // <div class="b3-list b3-list--border b3-list--background">
537:     //     <div class="b3-list-item b3-list-item--narrow toggle">
538:     //         <span class="b3-list-item__toggle b3-list-item__toggle--hl">
539:     //             <svg class="b3-list-item__arrow b3-list-item__arrow--open">
540:     //                 <use xlink:href="#iconRight"></use>
541:     //             </svg>
542:     //         </span>
543:     //         <span class="b3-list-item__text ft__on-surface">插件</span>
544:     //     </div>
545:     //     <div class="b3-list__panel">
546:     //         <!-- repeat -->
547:     //         <div class="b3-list-item b3-list-item--narrow toggle">
548: 
549:     return new Promise((resolve) => {
550:         const dialog = new Dialog({
551:             title: window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.addNoteAssetsDirectoryLabel,
552:             width: window.bgCoverPlugin.isMobileLayout ? "92vw" : "600px",
553:             height: "70vh",
554:             content: `
555:             <div class="b3-dialog__content" style="height: calc(100% - 62px);">
556:                 <div id="folderTreeContainer" class="b3-label file-tree" style="height: 100%;">
557:                     <!-- Tree will be rendered here -->
558:                 </div>
559:             </div>
560:             <div class="b3-dialog__action">
561:                 <button class="b3-button b3-button--cancel">${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.cancel}</button>
562:                 <div class="fn__space"></div>
563:                 <button class="b3-button b3-button--text" id="folderPickerSelect">${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.confirm}</button>
564:             </div>
565:             `,
566:             destroyCallback: () => {
567:                 resolve(null);
568:             }
569:         });
570: 
571:         const renderSubfolderNode = async (path: string, parentElement: HTMLElement, level: number = 0) => {
572:             // 预先读取目录内容以确定是否有子文件夹
573:             let subDirs: { isDir: boolean; name: string }[] = [];
574:             let imageCount = 0;
575:             let hasSubDirs = false;
576:             try {
577:                 const res = await ka.readDir(path);
578:                 if (res.code === 0 && res.data) {
579:                     const items = res.data as { isDir: boolean; name: string }[];
580:                     debug(`ka.readDir -> items:`, items);
581: 
582:                     subDirs = items.filter(item => item.isDir);
583:                     debug(`读取文件夹${path}的子文件夹内容:`, subDirs)
584: 
585:                     // 计算图片数量
586:                     // let fileext = os.splitext('ea95f7576f32674cd.jfif')[1].toLowerCase()
587:                     // fileext => 'jfif' 缺少前面的'.'
588:                     // debug(`计算图片后缀是否符合`, fileext, cst.supportedImageSuffix.includes(fileext) )
589:                     imageCount = items.filter(item => 
590:                         !item.isDir && cst.supportedImageSuffix.includes(`.${os.splitext(item.name)[1].toLowerCase()}`)
591:                     ).length;
592:                     hasSubDirs = subDirs.length > 0;
593:                 }
594:             } catch (err) {
595:                 console.error(`[fileManagerUI] 读取路径失败 ${path}:`, err);
596:             }
597: 
598:             const nodeElement = document.createElement('div');
599:             const folderName = path.split('/').pop() || path;
600: 
601:             // 根据是否存在子文件夹，条件性地渲染展开/折叠的箭头
602:             const arrowHTML = hasSubDirs
603:                 // 如果有子文件夹：
604:                 ? `<span class="b3-list-item__toggle b3-list-item__toggle--hl">
605:                        <svg class="b3-list-item__arrow"><use xlink:href="#iconRight"></use></svg>
606:                    </span>`
607:                 // 如果没有子文件夹
608:                 : `<span class="b3-list-item__toggle"></span>`; // 使用一个空的span来保持对齐
609:             
610:             const badgeHTML = `
611:             <span class="counter counter--bg fn__flex-center b3-tooltips b3-tooltips__w" 
612:                 aria-label="${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.folderBgCountLabel}">
613:                 ${imageCount}
614:             </span>`
615: 
616:             nodeElement.innerHTML = `
617:             <div class="b3-list-item b3-list-item--narrow toggle">
618:                 ${arrowHTML}
619:                 <span class="b3-list-item__text ft__on-surface" >${folderName}</span>
620:                 <span class="fn__space"></span>
621:                 <input class="b3-switch fn__flex-center" type="checkbox" data-path="${path}" ${imageCount === 0 ? 'disabled' : ''}>
622:                 ${badgeHTML}
623:             </div>
624:             <div class="b3-list__panel" style="display: none;"></div>
625:             `;
626:             parentElement.appendChild(nodeElement);
627: 
628:             const panel = nodeElement.querySelector('.b3-list__panel') as HTMLElement;
629:             const checkbox = nodeElement.querySelector('.b3-switch') as HTMLInputElement;
630: 
631:             checkbox.addEventListener('change', () => {
632:                 if (checkbox.checked) {
633:                     selectedPaths.add(path);
634:                 } else {
635:                     selectedPaths.delete(path);
636:                 }
637:             });
638: 
639:             // 仅当存在子文件夹时，才添加展开/折叠功能
640:             if (hasSubDirs) {
641:                 const toggle = nodeElement.querySelector('.b3-list-item__toggle') as HTMLElement;
642:                 const arrow = nodeElement.querySelector('.b3-list-item__arrow') as SVGElement;
643: 
644:                 toggle.addEventListener('click', async () => {
645:                     const isOpen = arrow.classList.toggle('b3-list-item__arrow--open');
646:                     panel.style.display = isOpen ? '' : 'none';
647: 
648:                     // 仅在第一次展开时加载内容
649:                     if (isOpen && panel.childElementCount === 0) {
650:                         // 我们已经预加载了subDirs，现在直接使用它们来渲染
651:                         for (const item of subDirs) {
652:                             await renderSubfolderNode(`${path}/${item.name}`, panel, level + 1);
653:                         }
654:                     }
655:                 });
656:             }
657:         };
658: 
659:         const treeContainer = dialog.element.querySelector('#folderTreeContainer') as HTMLDivElement;
660:         
661:         // Main function to initialize the tree view
662:         const initTree = async () => {
663:             treeContainer.innerHTML = `<div class="fn__loading" style="text-align: center; padding: 20px;"><img src="/stage/loading-pure.svg"></div>`;
664:             try {
665:                 const res = await ka.readDir(rootPath);
666:                 treeContainer.innerHTML = ''; // Clear loading
667:                 if (res.code === 0 && res.data) {
668:                     const rootDirs = (res.data as { isDir: boolean; name: string }[]).filter(item => item.isDir);
669:                     if (rootDirs.length > 0) {
670:                         for (const dir of rootDirs) {
671:                             const listContainer = document.createElement('div');
672:                             listContainer.className = 'b3-list b3-list--border b3-list--background';
673:                             treeContainer.appendChild(listContainer);
674:                             await renderSubfolderNode(`${rootPath}/${dir.name}`, listContainer, 0);
675:                         }
676:                     } else {
677:                         treeContainer.innerHTML = `<div class="b3-list-item b3-list-item--narrow"><span class="b3-list-item__text ft__on-surface ft__smaller">${window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n.emptyFolder}</span></div>`;
678:                     }
679:                 }
680:             } catch (err) {
681:                 console.error("Failed to read root assets directory:", err);
682:                 treeContainer.innerHTML = `<div class="b3-list-item"><span class="b3-list-item__text" style="color: var(--b3-theme-error);">Failed to load assets directory.</span></div>`;
683:             }
684:         };
685: 
686:         initTree();
687: 
688:         // 确认选择按钮
689:         const confirmButton = dialog.element.querySelector('#folderPickerSelect') as HTMLButtonElement;
690:         confirmButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
691:             resolve(Array.from(selectedPaths));
692:             dialog.destroy();
693:         });
694:         
695:         // 取消按钮
696:         const cancelButton = dialog.element.querySelector('.b3-button--cancel') as HTMLButtonElement;
697:         cancelButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
698:             dialog.destroy();
699:         });
700:  
701:     });
702: }

34:         const container_ratio = container_w / container_h
35:         const img_ratio = img_w / img_h
36:

38:

52: export class OS {
53: 
54:     private ka = new KernelApi()
55: 
56:     public async rmtree(dir:string) {
57:         let out = await this.listdir(dir)
58: 
59:         for (let i in out) {
60:             let item = out[i]
61: 
62:             if (item.isDir) {
63:                 // 如果是文件夹，则递归删除
64:                 this.rmtree(`${dir}/${item.name}/`)
65:             }else{
66:                 let full_path = `${dir}/${item.name}`
67:                 await this.ka.removeFile(full_path)
68:             }
69:         }
70: 
71:         // 删除文件夹本身
72:         if (dir.slice(-1) === '/') {
73:             await this.ka.removeFile(dir)
74:         }else{
75:             await this.ka.removeFile(dir + '/')
76:         }
77:     }
78: 
79:     public async listdir(dir:string) {
80:         interface outArray {
81:             isDir: number; name: string
82:         }
83:         interface outArray extends Array<outArray>{}
84: 
85:         var outArray: outArray
86:         let out = await this.ka.readDir(dir);
87:         if (out !== null || out !== undefined) {
88:             debug("[os.listdir] out.data ->", out.data)
89:             outArray = out.data as outArray
90:         }
91:         
92:         return outArray
93:     }
94: 
95:     /**
96:      * 判断文件夹是否存在
97:      * @param dir 文件夹路径
98:      * @returns 存在返回true，不存在返回false
99:      */
100:     public async folderExists(dir: string): Promise<boolean> {
101:         try {
102:             const out = await this.ka.readDir(dir);
103:             debug(`[utils][pythonic.ts][OS.folderExists] 返回 out =>`, out)
104:             // 成功返回且code为0表示文件夹存在
105:             if (out && out.code === 0) {
106:                 debug(`[utils][pythonic.ts][OS.folderExists] 成功返回且code为0表示文件夹存在 => true`)
107:                 return true;
108:             }
109:             // 404错误表示文件夹不存在
110:             if (out && out.code === 404) {
111:                 debug(`[utils][pythonic.ts][OS.folderExists] 404错误表示文件夹不存在 => false`)
112:                 return false;
113:             }
114:             // 其他错误情况也视为不存在
115:             debug(`[utils][pythonic.ts][OS.folderExists] 遇到了其他错误 => false`)
116:             return false;
117:         } catch (error) {
118:             debug("[utils][pythonic.ts][OS.folderExists] 捕捉到报错:", error);
119:             return false;
120:         }
121:     }
122: 
123:     public async mkdir(dir:string) {
124:         // await this.ka.mkdir(dir)
125:         try {
126:             const out = await this.ka.putFolder(dir);
127:             // 成功返回且code为0表示文件夹存在
128:             if (out && out.code === 0) {
129:                 return true;
130:             }
131:             // 404错误表示文件夹不存在
132:             if (out && out.code === 404) {
133:                 return false;
134:             }
135:             // 其他错误情况也视为不存在
136:             return false;
137:         } catch (error) {
138:             debug("[os.pathExists] error:", error);
139:             return false;
140:         }
141:     }
142:     
143: 
144:     public splitext(filename:string) {
145:         let suffix = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('.')+1, filename.length) || filename
146:         let prefix = filename.substring(0, filename.lastIndexOf('.')) || filename
147: 
148:         return [prefix, suffix]
149:     }
150: 
151:     /**
152:      * The function to open a localhost file url to File object
153:      * @param url 
154:      * @param fileName 
155:      * @param fileType 
156:      * @returns File
157:      * Example:
158:      * >>> const url = 'https://example.com/path/to/file.txt'; // Replace with your desired URL
159:      * >>> const fileName = 'file.txt'; // Replace with the desired file name
160:      * >>> const fileType = 'text/plain'; // Replace with the desired file type
161:      * 
162:      * openFile(url, fileName, fileType)
163:         .then((file) => {
164:             if (file) {
165:             // File-like object is created, you can now use it
166:             console.log('File:', file);
167:             } else {
168:             console.log('File could not be fetched.');
169:             }
170:         })
171:         .catch((error) => {
172:             console.error('Error:', error);
173:         });
174:      */
175:     public async openFile(url:string, fileName:string, fileType:string) {
176:         try {
177:             const response = await fetch(url);
178:             const data = await response.blob();
179:         
180:             // Create a File-like object
181:             const file = new File([data], fileName, { type: fileType });
182:         
183:             return file;
184:         } catch (error) {
185:             console.error('Error fetching the file:', error);
186:             return null;
187:         }
188:     }
189: 
190:     /**
191:      * 
192:      * @param acceptedFileTypes : '.jpg,.png'
193:      * @returns 
194:      */
195:     public async openFilePicker(acceptedFileTypes?: string, multipleSelect = false): Promise<File[] | null> {
196:         return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
197:           const input = document.createElement('input');
198:           input.type = 'file';
199:           input.multiple = multipleSelect;
200:           input.value = '';
201: 
202:           if (acceptedFileTypes) {
203:             input.accept = acceptedFileTypes;
204:           }
205:       
206:           input.addEventListener('change', () => {
207:             if (input.files) {
208:               resolve(Array.from(input.files));
209:             } else {
210:               reject(new Error('No file selected'));
211:             }
212:           });
213:       
214:           input.click();
215:         });
216:     };

218:     public async openFolderPicker(): Promise<File[] | null> {

222:             input.webkitdirectory = true;
223:             input.multiple = true;
224:             input.value = '';
225:

<content>
1: function getTimestamp(): string {
2:     const now = new Date();
3:     const hours = String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
4:     const minutes = String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
5:     const seconds = String(now.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');
6:     const milliseconds = String(now.getMilliseconds()).padStart(3, '0');
7:     return `[${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}.${milliseconds}]`;
8: }
9: 
10: // simple logging functions
11: export function info(...msg: any[]): void {
12:     console.log(`[BgCover Plugin]${getTimestamp()} [INFO]`, ...msg);
13: }
14: 
15: export function debug(...msg: any[]): void {
16:     if (window.bgCoverPlugin.isDev) {
17:         console.log(`[BgCover Plugin]${getTimestamp()}[DEBUG]`, ...msg);
18:     }
19: }
20: 
21: export function error(...msg: any[]): void {
22:     console.error(`[BgCover Plugin]${getTimestamp()}[ERROR]`, ...msg);
23: }
24: 
25: export function warn(...msg: any[]): void {
26:     console.warn(`[BgCover Plugin]${getTimestamp()} [WARN]`, ...msg);
27: }

43:      * 然后用两级追溯parementElement.parenetElement，去获取dialog的Element
44:      * <div class="b3-dialog--open">
45:      *   <div class="b3-dialog">
46:      *      <div class="b3-dialog__scrim"></div>
47:      *   => <div class="b3-dialog__container" ...
48:      */
49:     if (dialog !== undefined) {
50:         dialog.parentElement.parentElement.remove();
51:     }
52: }

(End of file - total 52 lines)
</content>
```

400:     "cb-get-all" | // 获取所有块
401:     "cb-get-backlink" | // 悬浮窗为传递型需展示上下文
402:     "cb-get-unundo" | // 不需要记录历史
403:     "cb-get-scroll" | // 滚动到指定位置，用于直接打开文档，必有 rootID
404:     "cb-get-search" | // 使用搜索打开搜索
405:     "cb-get-context" | // 包含上下文
406:     "cb-get-rootscroll" | // 如果为 rootID 就滚动到指定位置，必有 rootID
407:     "cb-get-html" | // 直接渲染，不需要再 /api/block/getDocInfo，否则搜索表格无法定位
408:     "cb-get-history" | // 历史渲染
409:     "cb-get-opennew"  // 编辑器只读后新建文件需为临时解锁状态 & https://github.com/siyuan-note/siyuan/issues/12197

663: /** @link https://ld246.com/article/1549638745630#options-upload */
664: interface IUpload {
665:     /** 上传 url */
666:     url?: string;
667:     /** 上传文件最大 Byte */
668:     max?: number;
669:     /** 剪切板中包含图片地址时，使用此 url 重新上传 */
670:     linkToImgUrl?: string;
671:     /** CORS 上传验证，头为 X-Upload-Token */
672:     token?: string;
673:     /** 文件上传类型，同 [input accept](https://www.w3schools.com/tags/att_input_accept.asp) */
674:     accept?: string;
675:     /** 跨站点访问控制。默认值: false */
676:     withCredentials?: boolean;
677:     /** 请求头设置 */
678:     headers?: IObject;
679:     /** 额外请求参数 */
680:     extraData?: { [key: string]: string | Blob };
681:     /** 上传字段名。默认值：file[] */
682:     fieldName?: string;
683: 
684:     /** 每次上传前都会重新设置请求头 */
685:     setHeaders?(): IObject;
686: 
687:     /** 上传成功回调 */
688:     success?(editor: HTMLDivElement, msg: string): void;
689: 
690:     /** 上传失败回调 */
691:     error?(msg: string): void;
692: 
693:     /** 文件名安全处理。 默认值: name => name.replace(/\W/g, '') */
694:     filename?(name: string): string;
695: 
696:     /** 校验，成功时返回 true 否则返回错误信息 */
697:     validate?(files: File[]): string | boolean;
698: 
699:     /** 自定义上传，当发生错误时返回错误信息 */
700:     handler?(files: File[]): string | null;
701: 
702:     /** 对服务端返回的数据进行转换，以满足内置的数据结构 */
703:     format?(files: File[], responseText: string): string;
704: 
705:     /** 将上传的文件处理后再返回  */
706:     file?(files: File[]): File[];
707: 
708:     /** 图片地址上传后的回调  */
709:     linkToImgCallback?(responseText: string): void;
710: }
711:

283:                 return -1;
284:             }

310:         inputElement.focus();
311:         btnsElement[0].addEventListener("click", () => {
312:             dialog.destroy();
313:         });
314:         btnsElement[1].addEventListener("click", () => {
315:             this.saveData(STORAGE_NAME, {readonlyText: inputElement.value});
316:             dialog.destroy();
317:         });
318:     }
319:     */
320: 
321:     private eventBusPaste(event: any) {
322:         // 如果需异步处理请调用 preventDefault， 否则会进行默认处理
323:         event.preventDefault();
324:         // 如果使用了 preventDefault，必须调用 resolve，否则程序会卡死
325:         event.detail.resolve({
326:             textPlain: event.detail.textPlain.trim(),
327:         });
328:     }
329: 
330:     private eventBusLog({detail}: any) {
331:         console.log(detail);
332:     }
333: 
334:     private blockIconEvent({detail}: any) {
335:         detail.menu.addItem({
336:             id: "pluginSample_removeSpace",
337:             iconHTML: "",
338:             label: this.i18n.removeSpace,
339:             click: () => {
340:                 const doOperations: IOperation[] = [];
341:                 detail.blockElements.forEach((item: HTMLElement) => {
342:                     const editElement = item.querySelector('[contenteditable="true"]');
343:                     if (editElement) {
344:                         editElement.textContent = editElement.textContent.replace(/ /g, "");
345:                         doOperations.push({
346:                             id: item.dataset.nodeId,
347:                             data: item.outerHTML,
348:                             action: "update",
349:                         });
350:                     }
351:                 });
352:                 detail.protyle.getInstance().transaction(doOperations);
353:             },
354:         });
355:     }
356: 
357:     private showDialog() {
358:         const dialog = new Dialog({
359:             title: `SiYuan ${Constants.SIYUAN_VERSION}`,
360:             content: `<div class="b3-dialog__content">
361:     <div>appId:</div>
362:     <div class="fn__hr"></div>
363:     <div class="plugin-sample__time">${this.app.appId}</div>
364:     <div class="fn__hr"></div>
365:     <div class="fn__hr"></div>
366:     <div>API demo:</div>
367:     <div class="fn__hr"></div>
368:     <div class="plugin-sample__time">System current time: <span id="time"></span></div>
369:     <div class="fn__hr"></div>
370:     <div class="fn__hr"></div>
371:     <div>Protyle demo:</div>
372:     <div class="fn__hr"></div>
373:     <div id="protyle" style="height: 360px;"></div>
374: </div>`,
375:             width: this.isMobile ? "92vw" : "560px",
376:             height: "540px",
377:         });
378:         new Protyle(this.app, dialog.element.querySelector("#protyle"), {
379:             blockId: this.getEditor().protyle.block.rootID,
380:         });
381:         fetchPost("/api/system/currentTime", {}, (response) => {
382:             dialog.element.querySelector("#time").innerHTML = new Date(response.data).toString();
383:         });
384:     }

354:                     }

402:     async updateCards(options: ICardData) {
403:         options.cards.sort((a: ICard, b: ICard) => {
404:             if (a.blockID < b.blockID) {
405:                 return -1;
406:             }
407:             if (a.blockID > b.blockID) {
408:                 return 1;
409:             }
410:             return 0;
411:         });
412:         return options;
413:     }
414:     /**
415:      * A custom setting pannel provided by svelte
416:      */
417:     openSetting(): void {
418:         let dialog = new Dialog({
419:             title: "SettingPannel",
420:             content: `<div id="SettingPanel" style="height: 100%;"></div>`,
421:             width: "800px",
422:             destroyCallback: (options) => {
423:                 console.log("destroyCallback", options);
424:                 //You'd better destroy the component when the dialog is closed
425:                 pannel.$destroy();
426:             }
427:         });
428:         let pannel = new SettingExample({
429:             target: dialog.element.querySelector("#SettingPanel"),
430:         });
431:     }
432: 
433:     private eventBusPaste(event: any) {
434:         // 如果需异步处理请调用 preventDefault， 否则会进行默认处理
435:         event.preventDefault();
436:         // 如果使用了 preventDefault，必须调用 resolve，否则程序会卡死
437:         event.detail.resolve({
438:             textPlain: event.detail.textPlain.trim(),
439:         });
440:     }
441: 
442:     private eventBusLog({ detail }: any) {
443:         console.log(detail);
444:     }
445: 
446:     private blockIconEvent({ detail }: any) {
447:         detail.menu.addItem({
448:             id: "pluginSample_removeSpace",
449:             iconHTML: "",
450:             label: this.i18n.removeSpace,
451:             click: () => {
452:                 const doOperations: IOperation[] = [];
453:                 detail.blockElements.forEach((item: HTMLElement) => {
454:                     const editElement = item.querySelector('[contenteditable="true"]');
455:                     if (editElement) {
456:                         editElement.textContent = editElement.textContent.replace(/ /g, "");
457:                         doOperations.push({
458:                             id: item.dataset.nodeId,
459:                             data: item.outerHTML,
460:                             action: "update"
461:                         });
462:                     }
463:                 });
464:                 detail.protyle.getInstance().transaction(doOperations);
465:             }
466:         });
467:     }
468: 
469:     private showDialog() {
470:         const docId = this.getEditor().protyle.block.rootID;
471:         svelteDialog({
472:             title: `SiYuan ${Constants.SIYUAN_VERSION}`,
473:             width: this.isMobile ? "92vw" : "720px",
474:             constructor: (container: HTMLElement) => {
475:                 return new HelloExample({
476:                     target: container,
477:                     props: {
478:                         app: this.app,
479:                         blockID: docId
480:                     }
481:                 });
482:             }
483:         });
484:     }
485: 
486:     private addMenu(rect?: DOMRect) {
487:         const menu = new Menu("topBarSample", () => {
488:             console.log(this.i18n.byeMenu);
489:         });
490:         menu.addItem({
491:             icon: "iconSettings",
492:             label: "Open SiYuan Setting",
493:             click: () => {
494:                 openSetting(this.app);
495:             }
496:         });
497:         menu.addItem({
498:             icon: "iconSettings",
499:             label: "Open Plugin Setting",
500:             click: () => {
501:                 this.openSetting();
502:             }
503:         });
504:         menu.addSeparator();
505:         menu.addItem({
506:             icon: "iconDrag",
507:             label: "Open Attribute Panel",
508:             click: () => {
509:                 openAttributePanel({
510:                     nodeElement: this.getEditor().protyle.wysiwyg.element.firstElementChild as HTMLElement,
511:                     protyle: this.getEditor().protyle,
512:                     focusName: "custom",
513:                 });
514:             }
515:         });
516:         menu.addItem({
517:             icon: "iconInfo",
518:             label: "Dialog(open doc first)",
519:             accelerator: this.commands[0].customHotkey,
520:             click: () => {
521:                 this.showDialog();
522:             }
523:         });
524:         menu.addItem({
525:             icon: "iconFocus",
526:             label: "Select Opened Doc(open doc first)",
527:             click: () => {
528:                 (getModelByDockType("file") as Files).selectItem(this.getEditor().protyle.notebookId, this.getEditor().protyle.path);
529:             }
530:         });
531:         if (!this.isMobile) {
532:             menu.addItem({
533:                 icon: "iconFace",
534:                 label: "Open Custom Tab(open doc first)",
535:                 click: () => {
536:                     const tab = openTab({
537:                         app: this.app,
538:                         custom: {
539:                             icon: "iconFace",
540:                             title: "Custom Tab",
541:                             data: {
542:                                 // text: platformUtils.isHuawei() ? "Hello, Huawei!" : "This is my custom tab",
543:                                 blockID: this.getEditor().protyle.block.rootID,
544:                             },
545:                             id: this.name + TAB_TYPE
546:                         },
547:                     });
548:                     console.log(tab);
549:                 }
550:             });
551:             menu.addItem({
552:                 icon: "iconImage",
553:                 label: "Open Asset Tab(First open the Chinese help document)",
554:                 click: () => {
555:                     const tab = openTab({
556:                         app: this.app,
557:                         asset: {
558:                             path: "assets/paragraph-20210512165953-ag1nib4.svg"
559:                         }
560:                     });
561:                     console.log(tab);
562:                 }
563:             });
564:             menu.addItem({
565:                 icon: "iconFile",
566:                 label: "Open Doc Tab(open doc first)",
567:                 click: async () => {
568:                     const tab = await openTab({
569:                         app: this.app,
570:                         doc: {
571:                             id: this.getEditor().protyle.block.rootID,
572:                         }
573:                     });
574:                     console.log(tab);
575:                 }
576:             });
577:             menu.addItem({
578:                 icon: "iconSearch",
579:                 label: "Open Search Tab",
580:                 click: () => {
581:                     const tab = openTab({
582:                         app: this.app,
583:                         search: {
584:                             k: "SiYuan"
585:                         }
586:                     });
587:                     console.log(tab);
588:                 }
589:             });
590:             menu.addItem({
591:                 icon: "iconRiffCard",
592:                 label: "Open Card Tab",
593:                 click: () => {
594:                     const tab = openTab({
595:                         app: this.app,
596:                         card: {
597:                             type: "all"
598:                         }
599:                     });
600:                     console.log(tab);
601:                 }
602:             });
603:             menu.addItem({
604:                 icon: "iconLayout",
605:                 label: "Open Float Layer(open doc first)",
606:                 click: () => {
607:                     this.addFloatLayer({
608:                         refDefs: [{ refID: this.getEditor().protyle.block.rootID }],
609:                         x: window.innerWidth - 768 - 120,
610:                         y: 32,
611:                         isBacklink: false
612:                     });
613:                 }
614:             });
615:             menu.addItem({
616:                 icon: "iconOpenWindow",
617:                 label: "Open Doc Window(open doc first)",
618:                 click: () => {
619:                     openWindow({
620:                         doc: { id: this.getEditor().protyle.block.rootID }
621:                     });
622:                 }
623:             });
624:         } else {
625:             menu.addItem({
626:                 icon: "iconFile",
627:                 label: "Open Doc(open doc first)",
628:                 click: () => {
629:                     openMobileFileById(this.app, this.getEditor().protyle.block.rootID);
630:                 }
631:             });
632:         }
633:         menu.addItem({
634:             icon: "iconLock",
635:             label: "Lockscreen",
636:             click: () => {
637:                 lockScreen(this.app);
638:             }
639:         });
640:         menu.addItem({
641:             icon: "iconQuit",
642:             label: "Exit Application",
643:             click: () => {
644:                 exitSiYuan();
645:             }
646:         });
647:         menu.addItem({
648:             icon: "iconDownload",
649:             label: "Save Layout",
650:             click: () => {
651:                 saveLayout(() => {
652:                     showMessage("Layout saved");

<content>
1: import * as https from 'https';
2: import * as http from 'http';
3: import { URL } from 'url';
4: import { isIP } from 'net';
5: import { extensions } from 'vscode';
6: 
7: export class OnlineImageHelper {
8:     private static cachedUserAgent: string | null = null;
9: 
10:     /**
11:      * 获取在线图片列表（混合方案）
12:      */
13:     public static async getOnlineImages(urlString: string): Promise<string[]> {
14:         try {
15:             const isImage = await this.isImageUrl(urlString);
16:             if (isImage) {
17:                 console.log('[OnlineImageHelper] 检测为单张图片');
18:                 return [urlString];
19:             }
20:             // url是否为vs.20988.xyz
21:             if (urlString.includes('vs.20988.xyz')) {
22:                 const vs20988xyzImages = await this.tryParseVs20988xyz(urlString);
23:                 if (vs20988xyzImages && vs20988xyzImages.length > 0) {
24:                     console.log('[OnlineImageHelper] VS20988xyz 获取成功，获取到', vs20988xyzImages.length, '张图片');
25:                     return vs20988xyzImages;
26:                 }else{
27:                     return [];
28:                 }
29:             }
30:             
31:             const apiImages = await this.tryJsonApi(urlString);
32:             if (apiImages && apiImages.length > 0) {
33:                 console.log('[OnlineImageHelper] JSON API 成功，获取到', apiImages.length, '张图片');
34:                 return apiImages;
35:             }
36: 
37:             const htmlImages = await this.tryParseDirectory(urlString);
38:             if (htmlImages && htmlImages.length > 0) {
39:                 console.log('[OnlineImageHelper] HTML 解析成功，获取到', htmlImages.length, '张图片');
40:                 return htmlImages;
41:             }
42:             console.log('[OnlineImageHelper] 无法识别URL类型，当作单图处理');
43:             return [urlString];
44:         } catch (error: any) {
45:             console.error('[OnlineImageHelper] 获取在线图片失败:', error?.message || error);
46:             return [urlString];
47:         }
48:     }
49: 
50:     private static async tryJsonApi(urlString: string): Promise<string[] | null> {
51:         try {
52:             const apiUrls = [
53:                 urlString,
54:                 `${urlString}?format=json`,
55:                 `${urlString}?list=json`,
56:                 `${urlString.replace(/\/$/, '')}.json`,
57:             ];
58:             for (const apiUrl of apiUrls) {
59:                 try {
60:                     const data = await this.fetchJson(apiUrl);
61:                     const imageFiles = this.collectImagesFromApiData(data, urlString);
62:                     if (imageFiles.length > 0) {
63:                         return imageFiles;
64:                     }
65:                 } catch (err) {
66:                     continue;
67:                 }
68:             }
69:             return null;
70:         } catch (error) {
71:             return null;
72:         }
73:     }
74: 
75: 
76:     private static async tryParseDirectory(urlString: string): Promise<string[] | null> {
77:         try {
78:             const html = await this.fetchText(urlString);
79:             const patterns = [
80:                 /<a\s+href=["']([^"']+\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|webp|bmp|jfif))["']/gi,
81:                 /<a\s+[^>]*href=["']([^"']+)["'][^>]*>/gi,
82:             ];
83:             const foundImages = new Set<string>();
84:             for (const pattern of patterns) {
85:                 const matches = html.matchAll(pattern);
86:                 for (const match of matches) {
87:                     const imagePath = match[1];
88:                     if (this.isImageFileName(imagePath)) {
89:                         const fullUrl = this.resolveImageUrl(urlString, imagePath);
90:                         foundImages.add(fullUrl);
91:                     }
92:                 }
93:             }
94:             return foundImages.size > 0 ? Array.from(foundImages) : null;
95:         } catch (error) {
96:             return null;
97:         }
98:     }
99: 
100:     // 适配 VS20988xyz 论坛的图片提取
101:     private static async tryParseVs20988xyz(urlString: string): Promise<string[] | null> {
102:         try {
103:             const html = await this.fetchText(urlString);
104:             
105:             // 先尝试提取 Post-body 节点内的内容
106:             let targetContent = html;
107:             const postBodyRegex = /<div\s+[^>]*class=["'][^"']*Post-body[^"']*["'][^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/div>/gi;
108:             let match;
109:             let combinedContent = '';
110:             let foundBody = false;
111:             
112:             while ((match = postBodyRegex.exec(html)) !== null) {
113:                 if (match[1]) {
114:                     combinedContent += match[1];
115:                     foundBody = true;
116:                 }
117:             }
118: 
119:             if (foundBody) {
120:                 targetContent = combinedContent;
121:                 console.log('[OnlineImageHelper] 找到 Post-body 节点，将在其中查询图片');
122:             }
123:             
124:             const patterns = [
125:                 /<img\s+src=["']([^"']+\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|webp|bmp|jfif))["']/gi,
126:                 /<img\s+[^>]*src=["']([^"']+)["'][^>]*>/gi,
127:             ];
128:             const foundImages = new Set<string>();
129:             for (const pattern of patterns) {
130:                 const matches = targetContent.matchAll(pattern);
131:                 for (const match of matches) {
132:                     const imagePath = match[1];
133:                     if (this.isImageFileName(imagePath)) {
134:                         const fullUrl = this.resolveImageUrl(urlString, imagePath);
135:                         foundImages.add(fullUrl);
136:                     }
137:                 }
138:             }
139:             return foundImages.size > 0 ? Array.from(foundImages) : null;
140:         } catch (error) {
141:             return null;
142:         }
143:     }
144: 
145:     private static async isImageUrl(urlString: string): Promise<boolean> {
146:         try {
147:             const headInfo = await this.fetchHeaders(urlString, 'HEAD');
148:             const headType = headInfo.contentType?.toLowerCase();
149:             if (headType && headType.startsWith('image/')) {
150:                 return true;
151:             }
152:         } catch (error) {
153:             // ignore and fall back to GET probing below
154:         }
155:         try {
156:             const getInfo = await this.fetchHeaders(urlString, 'GET');
157:             const getType = getInfo.contentType?.toLowerCase();
158:             if (getType && getType.startsWith('image/')) {
159:                 return true;
160:             }
161:         } catch (error) {
162:             // ignore
163:         }
164:         return this.isImageFileName(urlString);
165:     }
166: 
167:     private static isImageFileName(filename: string): boolean {
168:         return /\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|webp|bmp|jfif)(\?.*)?$/i.test(filename);
169:     }
170: 
171:     private static extractImageFromValue(value: unknown, depth = 0): string | null {
172:         if (value === null || value === undefined) {
173:             return null;
174:         }
175:         if (depth > 4) {
176:             return null;
177:         }
178:         if (typeof value === 'string') {
179:             return this.isImageFileName(value) ? value : null;
180:         }
181:         if (Array.isArray(value)) {
182:             for (const entry of value) {
183:                 const nested = this.extractImageFromValue(entry, depth + 1);
184:                 if (nested) {
185:                     return nested;
186:                 }
187:             }
188:             return null;
189:         }
190:         if (typeof value === 'object') {
191:             const record = value as Record<string, unknown>;
192:             const prioritizedKeys = ['imageUrl', 'fullUrl', 'url', 'thumbUrl', 'src', 'original', 'name', 'path'];
193:             for (const key of prioritizedKeys) {
194:                 if (key in record) {
195:                     const nested = this.extractImageFromValue(record[key], depth + 1);
196:                     if (nested) {
197:                         return nested;
198:                     }
199:                 }
200:             }
201:             for (const entry of Object.values(record)) {
202:                 const nested = this.extractImageFromValue(entry, depth + 1);
203:                 if (nested) {
204:                     return nested;
205:                 }
206:             }
207:         }
208:         return null;
209:     }
210: 
211:     private static collectImagesFromApiData(data: unknown, baseUrl: string): string[] {
212:         const found = new Set<string>();
213:         const traverse = (value: unknown, depth = 0) => {
214:             if (value === null || value === undefined || depth > 6) {
215:                 return;
216:             }
217:             if (typeof value === 'string') {
218:                 if (this.isImageFileName(value)) {
219:                     found.add(this.resolveImageUrl(baseUrl, value));
220:                 }
221:                 return;
222:             }
223:             if (Array.isArray(value)) {
224:                 for (const entry of value) {
225:                     traverse(entry, depth + 1);
226:                 }
227:                 return;
228:             }
229:             if (typeof value === 'object') {
230:                 const record = value as Record<string, unknown>;
231:                 if (record && typeof record['ext'] === 'string' && record['pid'] && record['uid'] && record['urls']) {
232:                     const urlCandidate = this.extractImageFromValue(record['urls'], depth + 1);
233:                     if (urlCandidate) {
234:                         found.add(this.resolveImageUrl(baseUrl, urlCandidate));
235:                     }
236:                 }
237:                 const prioritizedKeys = ['images', 'files', 'data', 'results', 'items', 'list'];
238:                 for (const key of prioritizedKeys) {
239:                     if (Array.isArray(record[key])) {
240:                         traverse(record[key], depth + 1);
241:                     }
242:                 }
243:                 for (const entry of Object.values(record)) {
244:                     traverse(entry, depth + 1);
245:                 }
246:             }
247:         };
248:         traverse(data);
249:         return Array.from(found);
250:     }
251: 
252:     private static resolveImageUrl(baseUrl: string, imagePath: string): string {
253:         if (imagePath.startsWith('http://') || imagePath.startsWith('https://')) {
254:             return imagePath;
255:         }
256:         const base = baseUrl.endsWith('/') ? baseUrl : `${baseUrl}/`;
257:         imagePath = imagePath.replace(/^\.\//, '');
258:         if (imagePath.startsWith('/')) {
259:             const parsed = new URL(baseUrl);
260:             return `${parsed.protocol}//${parsed.host}${imagePath}`;
261:         }
262:         return base + imagePath;
263:     }
264: 
265:     private static async fetchJson(urlString: string): Promise<unknown> {
266:         const text = await this.fetchText(urlString);
267:         return JSON.parse(text);
268:     }
269: 
270:     private static fetchText(urlString: string): Promise<string> {
271:         return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
272:             let parsed: URL;
273:             try {
274:                 parsed = this.parseAndValidateUrl(urlString);
275:             } catch (error) {
276:                 reject(error);
277:                 return;
278:             }
279:             const client = parsed.protocol === 'https:' ? https : http;
280:             const options: https.RequestOptions = {
281:                 method: 'GET',
282:                 timeout: 10000,
283:                 headers: {
284:                     'User-Agent': this.getUserAgent()
285:                 }
286:             };
287:             const req = client.get(parsed, options, (res) => {
288:                 const status = res.statusCode ?? 0;
289:                 if ([301, 302, 307, 308].includes(status)) {
290:                     const redirectUrl = res.headers.location;
291:                     if (redirectUrl) {
292:                         const nextUrl = new URL(redirectUrl, parsed).toString();
293:                         try {
294:                             this.parseAndValidateUrl(nextUrl);
295:                         } catch (validationError: any) {
296:                             res.resume();
297:                             reject(new Error(`Redirect URL is invalid or unsafe: ${validationError?.message || validationError}`));
298:                             return;
299:                         }
300:                         res.resume();
301:                         this.fetchText(nextUrl).then(resolve).catch(reject);
302:                         return;
303:                     }
304:                     res.resume();
305:                     reject(new Error(`Redirect response received (HTTP ${status}) but no location header was provided.`));
306:                     return;
307:                 }
308:                 if (status !== 200) {
309:                     res.resume();
310:                     reject(new Error(`HTTP ${status}`));
311:                     return;
312:                 }
313:                 let data = '';
314:                 res.setEncoding('utf8');
315:                 res.on('data', (chunk) => { data += chunk; });
316:                 res.on('end', () => resolve(data));
317:             });
318:             req.on('error', reject);
319:             req.on('timeout', () => {
320:                 req.destroy();
321:                 reject(new Error('Request timeout'));
322:             });
323:         });
324:     }
325: 
326:     private static fetchHeaders(urlString: string, method: 'HEAD' | 'GET' = 'HEAD', redirectCount = 0): Promise<{ headers: http.IncomingHttpHeaders; statusCode?: number; contentType?: string; }> {
327:         return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
328:             let parsed: URL;
329:             try {
330:                 parsed = this.parseAndValidateUrl(urlString);
331:             } catch (error) {
332:                 reject(error);
333:                 return;
334:             }
335:             const client = parsed.protocol === 'https:' ? https : http;
336:             const options: https.RequestOptions = {
337:                 method,
338:                 timeout: method === 'HEAD' ? 5000 : 7000,
339:                 headers: {
340:                     'User-Agent': this.getUserAgent(),
341:                     'Accept': method === 'HEAD' ? '*/*' : 'image/*,*/*;q=0.8'
342:                 }
343:             };
344:             const req = client.request(parsed, options, (res) => {
345:                 const status = res.statusCode ?? 0;
346:                 if ([301, 302, 307, 308].includes(status)) {
347:                     const redirectUrl = res.headers.location;
348:                     if (redirectUrl) {
349:                         const nextUrl = new URL(redirectUrl, parsed).toString();
350:                         res.resume();
351:                         if (redirectCount >= 5) {
352:                             reject(new Error('Too many redirects'));
353:                             return;
354:                         }
355:                         try {
356:                             this.parseAndValidateUrl(nextUrl);
357:                         } catch (validationError: any) {
358:                             reject(new Error(`Redirect URL is invalid or unsafe: ${validationError?.message || validationError}`));
359:                             return;
360:                         }
361:                         this.fetchHeaders(nextUrl, method, redirectCount + 1).then(resolve).catch(reject);
362:                         return;
363:                     }
364:                 }
365:                 const contentType = (res.headers['content-type'] as string | undefined) ?? undefined;
366:                 resolve({ headers: res.headers, statusCode: res.statusCode, contentType });
367:                 if (method === 'GET') {
368:                     res.destroy();
369:                 } else {
370:                     res.resume();
371:                 }
372:             });
373:             req.on('error', reject);
374:             req.on('timeout', () => {
375:                 req.destroy();
376:                 reject(new Error('Request timeout'));
377:             });
378:             req.end();
379:         });
380:     }
381: 
382:     private static parseAndValidateUrl(urlString: string): URL {
383:         const parsed = new URL(urlString);
384:         if (!/^https?:$/.test(parsed.protocol)) {
385:             throw new Error('仅支持 HTTPS 或 HTTP 协议');
386:         }
387:         if (!parsed.hostname) {
388:             throw new Error('URL 缺少主机');
389:         }
390:         if (this.isPrivateAddress(parsed.hostname)) {
391:             throw new Error('禁止访问私有网络地址');
392:         }
393:         return parsed;
394:     }
395: 
396:     private static isPrivateAddress(hostname: string): boolean {
397:         const lower = hostname.toLowerCase();
398:         if (lower === 'localhost' || lower === '127.0.0.1' || lower === '::1') {
399:             return true;
400:         }
401:         const ipVersion = isIP(hostname);
402:         if (ipVersion === 4) {
403:             const parts = hostname.split('.').map((segment) => Number(segment));
404:             if (parts.length === 4 && parts.every((part) => !Number.isNaN(part))) {
405:                 const [first, second] = parts;
406:                 if (first === 10) {
407:                     return true;
408:                 }
409:                 if (first === 127) {
410:                     return true;
411:                 }
412:                 if (first === 169 && second === 254) {
413:                     return true;
414:                 }
415:                 if (first === 172 && second >= 16 && second <= 31) {
416:                     return true;
417:                 }
418:                 if (first === 192 && second === 168) {
419:                     return true;
420:                 }
421:                 if (first === 0) {
422:                     return true;
423:                 }
424:             }
425:         }
426:         if (ipVersion === 6) {
427:             if (lower === '::1') {
428:                 return true;
429:             }
430:             if (lower.startsWith('fc') || lower.startsWith('fd') || lower.startsWith('fe80') || lower.startsWith('fec0')) {
431:                 return true;
432:             }
433:         }
434:         return false;
435:     }
436: 
437:     private static getUserAgent(): string {
438:         if (!this.cachedUserAgent) {
439:             const extension = extensions.getExtension('manasxx.background-cover');
440:             const version = extension?.packageJSON?.version;
441:             const suffix = version ? `/${version}` : '';
442:             this.cachedUserAgent = `VSCode-Background-Cover${suffix}`;
443:         }
444:         return this.cachedUserAgent;
445:     }
446: 
447:     /**
448:      * 检测URL类型（用于调试）
449:      */
450:     public static async detectUrlType(urlString: string): Promise<{ type: string; url?: string; images?: string[]; error?: string }> {
451:         try {
452:             const images = await this.getOnlineImages(urlString);
453:             if (images.length === 1 && images[0] === urlString) {
454:                 return { type: 'image', url: urlString };
455:             }
456:             return { type: 'folder', images };
457:         } catch (error: any) {
458:             return { type: 'unknown', error: error.message };
459:         }
460:     }
461: }

(End of file - total 461 lines)
</content>

1518:     // 图片转为Base64
1519:     private async imageToBase64(): Promise<boolean> {
1520:         try {
1521:             const extname = path.extname(this.imagePath).substr(1);
1522:             const imageBuffer = await fs.promises.readFile(path.resolve(this.imagePath));
1523:             this.imagePath = `data:image/${extname};base64,${imageBuffer.toString('base64')}`;
1524:             return true;
1525:         } catch {
1526:             return false;
1527:         }
1528:     }
1529: 
1530:     private async prepareCodeServerAsset(sourcePath: string): Promise<string | undefined> {
1531:         try {
1532:             await fse.ensureDir(CUSTOM_ASSET_DIR);
1533:             const buffer = await fse.readFile(path.resolve(sourcePath));
1534:             const hash = crypto.createHash('md5').update(buffer).digest('hex');
1535:             const ext = path.extname(sourcePath) || '.img';
1536:             const fileName = `${hash}${ext}`;
1537:             const destPath = path.join(CUSTOM_ASSET_DIR, fileName);
1538: 
1539:             if (!(await fse.pathExists(destPath))) {
1540:                 await fse.writeFile(destPath, buffer);
1541:             }
1542: 
1543:             const relativeUrl = this.getRelativeAssetUrl(destPath);
1544:             if (!relativeUrl) {
1545:                 return undefined;
1546:             }
1547: 
1548:             const normalized = relativeUrl.replace(/^\/+/, '');
1549:             return `${RELATIVE_URL_PLACEHOLDER}/${normalized}`;
1550:         } catch (error) {
1551:             console.error('[FileDom] Failed to prepare code-server asset:', error);
1552:             return undefined;
1553:         }
1554:     }
1555: 
1556:     private getExtensionFromContentType(contentType?: string): string | undefined {
1557:         if (!contentType) {
1558:             return undefined;
1559:         }
1560:         const cleanType = contentType.split(';')[0].trim().toLowerCase();
1561:         const map: Record<string, string> = {
1562:             'image/jpeg': '.jpg',
1563:             'image/jpg': '.jpg',
1564:             'image/png': '.png',
1565:             'image/gif': '.gif',
1566:             'image/webp': '.webp',
1567:             'image/bmp': '.bmp',
1568:             'image/svg+xml': '.svg',
1569:             'video/mp4': '.mp4',
1570:             'video/webm': '.webm',
1571:             'video/ogg': '.ogg',
1572:             'video/quicktime': '.mov'
1573:         };
1574:         return map[cleanType] || undefined;
1575:     }
1576: 
1577:     private getRelativeAssetUrl(targetPath: string): string | undefined {
1578:         try {
1579:             const relative = path.relative(selectedWorkbench.root, targetPath);
1580:             if (!relative || relative.startsWith('..')) {
1581:                 return undefined;
1582:             }
1583:             return relative.split(path.sep).join('/');
1584:         } catch (error) {
1585:             console.error('[FileDom] Failed to resolve asset url:', error);
1586:             return undefined;
1587:         }
1588:     }
1589: 
1590:     private localImgToVsc(): void {
1591:         // 使用 Uri.file 自动处理路径分隔符和编码，避免手动拼接导致的路径错误（如 macOS 下的双斜杠问题）
1592:         this.imagePath = Uri.file(this.imagePath).with({ scheme: 'vscode-file', authority: 'vscode-app' }).toString();
1593:     }
1594: 
1595:     private clearCssContent(content: string): string {
1596:         const regex = new RegExp(`\\/\\*ext-${this.extName}-start\\*\\/[\\s\\S]*?\\/\\*ext-${this.extName}-end\\*\\/`, 'g');
1597:         return content.replace(regex, '').trim();
1598:     }
1599: 
1600:     public getPatchContent(content: string): boolean {
1601:         const match = content.match(/\/\*ext-backgroundCover-start\*\/[\s\S]*?\/\*ext-backgroundCover-end\*\//g);
1602:         return !!match;
1603:     }
1604: }

This is your source of truth for backend API calls.

### `.agents/references/petal/`
